**【章节】NEUROLOGY**

**Anatomy/Development**

> **Alar: dorsal = sensory** (neural plate originates here - dorsal midline)
>
> **Basal plate: ventral = motor**

**A**lar = **A**fferent = sensory 背面（alar）负责“听消息”

**B**asal = **B**ehavior/output = motor肚子那面（basal）负责“发指令”

> **脊髓**
>
> dorsal horn → sensory → alar plate
>
> ventral horn → motor → basal plate
>
> **脑干**
>
> sensory nuclei → alar plate
>
> motor nuclei → basal plate
>
> further pattern:

medial=motor

lateral=sensory

> **Notochord** forms at **3 weeks**
>
> **Brain** form at **8 weeks** - right after gastrulation

Notocod needs **vitamin A (retinoic acid)** and peptides **Sonic Hedgehog/SHH** induce formation of nerovus Sustem

> Risk of encountering **teratogenic** are at **3-8 weeks**
>
> CSF: needs vitamin A and ses carbonic anhydrase enzyme

CSF主要由**脉络丛**产生，依赖**carbonic anhydrase**

**Acetazolamide** 抑制 carbonic anhydrase🡪可减少 CSF 生成，用于

**idiopathic intracranial hypertension**

**glaucoma**

**altitude sickness**

**过多 vitamin A / isotretinoin** 可导致 **pseudotumor cerebri**

> **<span class="mark">Hypoxia</span>**🡪**vasoconstriction in <span class="mark">lungs</span>**
>
> **Hyperventilation** 🡪 low CO₂/**<span class="mark">hypocapnia</span> → vasoconstriction in the <span class="mark">brain</span>**
>
> **Acid and ammonia** increase GABA release → inhibitory → shuts down everything

**肝性脑病 Hepatic Encephalopathy**

**1）肝功能差 / 门体分流→ NH₃（ammonia）↑→ 脑内 astrocyte 摄取 NH₃\
→ NH₃ + glutamate → glutamine ↑→ astrocyte swelling（星形胶质细胞肿胀）🡪神经递质失衡（抑制性↑）→ hepatic encephalopathy**

**2）神经递质公式**

**Hyperammonemia→ inhibitory tone ↑（GABAergic tone ↑）→ 脑功能被“刹车”→ 嗜睡 / 意识模糊 / 昏迷**

**3）细胞水平公式**

**NH₃ ↑→ astrocyte 内 glutamine ↑→ 渗透压↑→ 水进入细胞→ astrocyte swelling→ 脑功能异常**

**4）临床表现公式**

**高氨 + 脑抑制↑→ confusion→ somnolence→ asterixis→ coma**

**5）<span class="mark">扑翼样震颤</span>公式**

**脑功能异常→ 维持姿势的肌张力短暂中断→ negative myoclonus→ asterixis（扑翼样震颤）**

**6）常见诱因**

**GI bleed**

**肠道内血液↑\
→ 蛋白负荷↑\
→ 细菌分解产氨↑\
→ NH₃ ↑\
→ hepatic encephalopathy**

**Constipation**

**粪便停留时间↑\
→ 肠道细菌分解含氮物↑\
→ NH₃ ↑**

**Infection / dehydration / TIPS**

**肝代谢负担↑ or 门体分流↑\
→ NH₃ 清除↓\
→ encephalopathy**

**7）治疗公式**

**<span class="mark">Lactulose</span>→ 肠道酸化→ NH₃ → NH₄⁺（不易吸收）**

> **泻下作用\
> → 肠道含氮物排出↑\
> → 血氨↓**

**<span class="mark">Rifaximin</span>→ 肠道细菌↓→ 产氨↓→ 血氨↓**

**8）最常考四联公式**

**肝硬化病人**

> **confusion**
>
> **asterixis**
>
> **ammonia ↑= hepatic encephalopathy**

神经管缺陷

开放性神经管缺陷

> AFP ↑
>
> AChE ↑
>
> 羊水也可异常

闭合性神经管缺陷

> AFP 正常

**<u>Anencephaly</u>**

> Characteristic: Spinal cord doesn’t meet the brain
>
> Cause: due to **folate deficiency** or **amphetamine abuse**
>
> Labs: **high AFP**, high AChE, **low beta-hCG**

**<u>Spina Bifida Aperta</u>**

> Characteristic: open
>
> Labs: **high AFP**

**<u>Spina Bifida Occulta</u>椎弓未闭合，但皮肤完整**

> Characteristic: closed; **tuft of hair or skin dimple**; **deformity in the vertebral column** that has missing vertebral
>
> Labs: **normal AFP**

<u>**Encephalo Myelomeningocele**</u>

> Characteristic: includes **brain, spine, and meninges**

**Base of brain**

> Labs: **high AFP**

**<u>Myelomeningocele</u>**

脊髓 + 脑膜 突出到囊内

多见于腰骶部

> 开放性神经管缺陷
>
> AFP 高

临床情景

新生儿腰骶部囊性肿物\
伴下肢神经功能缺损、膀胱肠道功能问题

**Meningomyelocele**

> Characteristic: includes **meninges and spine**

In the **sacrum**

> Labs: **high AFP**

<img src="images/media/image1.png" style="width:5.76806in;height:1.84514in" />

<img src="images/media/image2.png" style="width:1.60069in;height:2in" /><img src="images/media/image3.png" style="width:1.84792in;height:1.80069in" />**<u>Dandy Walker Malformation</u>**

> Characteristic: **early morning vomiting and 4th ventricle enlarged** because there is **no cerebellum** → **brain starts to herniate through the foramen magnum**
>
> **小脑蚓部发育不全/缺如**
>
> **第四脑室扩大**
>
> **后颅窝扩大**
>
> **可致脑积水**

**婴儿：**

> **头围增大**
>
> **呕吐**
>
> <img src="images/media/image4.jpeg" style="width:2.80972in;height:1.73403in" />**发育迟缓**
>
> **共济失调**

**<u>Chiari I Malformation</u>**

> Characteristic: **foramen magnum is large** so brain starts to slides

**Asymptomatic**

**小脑扁桃体下疝 through foramen magnum**

> **常在<span class="mark">青少年/成人</span>发现**
>
> **儿童期一般无症状**
>
> **可头痛occipital headache、neck pain**
>
> **physical activity or Valsalva (cough, straining)🡪pressure of cerebellar tonsil on foramen magnum 🡪 dizziness, worsening pain**
>
> **ICP↑**
>
> **Brainstem compression 🡪 cranial neuropathies (dysarthria)**
>
> **Cerebellar dysfunction (ataxia)**
>
> **常合并 <span class="mark">syringomyelia</span>**

**高频联想**

> **Cape-like pain/temp loss**
>
> **手部小肌无力\
> 来自合并脊髓空洞，不是 Chiari I 本身直接“foramen magnum 大”。**

**<u>syringomyelia</u>中央脊髓空洞损伤前连合交叉纤维\
→ 双侧 pain & temperature loss\
常呈：**

> **cape-like distribution（披肩样）**

**常见相关**

> **Chiari I**
>
> **trauma** to shoulder or neck，“成人肩颈外伤后”
>
> <img src="images/media/image5.jpeg" style="width:3.09028in;height:3.33681in" />**tumor**

**<u>Chiari II Malformation</u>**

> **小脑蚓部、脑干**向下移位
>
> 几乎总与 **<span class="mark">myelomeningocele</span>** 相关
>
> **<span class="mark">婴儿</span>**更常见

表现

> 吞咽困难
>
> 喂养差
>
> 喘鸣
>
> 呼吸暂停
>
> 上肢无力
>
> 脑积水

**<u>Vomiting Center</u>**

> Responds to **high intracranial pressure<span class="mark">晨起头痛 + 呕吐→ 想高颅压</span>**
>
> So **migraines** are due to vasodilation leading to **nausea and vomiting**
>
> Responds to **taste and smell**

**Chemoreceptor trigger zone = <u>area postrema</u>**

> at the **floor of the 4th ventricle第四脑室底部附近**
>
> **位于 blood-brain barrier 较薄弱/缺失区域, 所以能感知血中毒素、药物。**

**Stimulated by**

> **dopamine**
>
> **serotonin**
>
> **substance P 等**

**临床情景**

> **化疗后恶心呕吐**
>
> **阿片类药物引起恶心**
>
> **尿毒症/毒素引起呕吐**

**治疗**

> **<span class="mark">metoclopramide / prochlorperazine</span> 抗多巴胺**
>
> **<span class="mark">ondansetron</span> 抗 5-HT3**

**Neurocutaneous Disorders背**

**<u>Subependymal giant cell astrocytoma / tumor（SEGA）</u>**

> 位于脑室旁、ependyma 下
>
> 可阻塞 Monro 孔
>
> 导致**梗阻性脑积水**

<span class="mark">AASSRASH</span>

**Ash-leaf**

**Angiofibroma**

**Shagreen patches**

**Seizure**

**Rhabdomyomas**

**Retardation智力障碍**

**Angiomyolipomas**

**Subependymal tumor**

**Hematoma**

**<u>Infantile spasms seizures</u>**

**无明显诱因**

**成串**clusters**反复**，常在醒后 

**brief, sudden, symmetric contractions**

每次只持续 **1–2秒**，但会**连续发很多下**

病理性，常提示严重神经发育问题: **developmental regression，**发育停滞，智力预后差

**Neurofibromatosis 1**:**皮肤**（cafe-au-lait, freckling, neurofibromas），**眼** (**lisch nodules, optic glioma**🡪 **decreased visual acuity, alterations in color vision, optic nerve atrophy, and proptosis**)，**骨畸形**

**Neurofibromatosis 2**: **耳**（**bilateral** acoustic **neuromas**），**中枢肿瘤**（**meningiomas**, ependymomas）

**Sturge weber presentation（somatic mosaic）**: kid had port wine stain in face and **vascular malformation**, **seizures**, **mental retardation** in future; episcleral hemangioma🡪**early-onset glaucoma**

**<u>AV Malformations</u>**

> Characteristic: **↑ preload, ↓ afterload**
>
> **<u>Osler Weber Rendu</u>**: AVM in **<span class="mark">lungs, CNS, GI</span>**

Characteristic: painless bleeding and telangiectasia

> **反复鼻出血 + telangiectasia + 肺/脑 AVM。肺 AVM 可导致低氧和反常栓塞/脑脓肿**
>
> **<u>Von-Hipper-Lindau</u>**: AVM in **<span class="mark">head, retina</span>** (**AD** VHL Gene, Chrom **3**p)

**Retinal, brainstem, cerebellum, spine hemangioblastoma**

**Angiomatosis**

**bilateral renal cell carcinoma**

**pheochromocytoma**

**小脑/脊髓/视网膜 hemangioblastoma + RCC + pheo**

**<u>Hydrocephalus</u>**

> **Communicating hydrocephalus**: **impaired absorption** of CSF (Arachnoid granulations)

脑室之间“通着”，但 CSF **吸收差**。常见于蛛网膜下腔出血、脑膜炎后。

> **Noncommunicating hydrocephalus**: **obstruction in the draining** of CSF

CSF 流动在脑室系统某处被堵住，典型是**中脑导水管狭窄**，第三脑室到第四脑室不通

Blockage typically in midbrain

**Cerebral aqueduct (aqueduct of Sylvius)** – which runs through the midbrain and connects the third ventricle to the fourth ventricle.

Cause: aqueductal stenosis in the midbrain

**婴儿**

头围增大

囟门膨隆

呕吐、烦躁、落日征

**成人/老年**

头痛、恶心、呕吐

视乳头水肿

<span class="mark">肿瘤造成阻塞时想 **noncommunicating hydrocephalus**</span>

> **<u>Intraventricular hemorrhage</u>**

Characteristic: **<span class="mark">premature</span> baby** with **seizure** and **communicating hydrocephalus**

> **<u>DeGeorge Syndrome</u>**

Characteristic: **<span class="mark">newborn</span> tetany** and **seizures in 24 hours**, **<span class="mark">hypocalcemia</span>**

> **<u>Pseudotumor Cerebri</u>**

Characteristic: **communicating hydrocephalus** in **<span class="mark">young adult</span>**, **headache when leans forward**

Cause: **<span class="mark">overdose on Vitamin A</span>**

Treatment: **stop vitamin A** and give **<span class="mark">acetazolamide</span>**

<p><strong>CSF</strong> = cerebrospinal fluid; <strong>ICP</strong> = intracranial pressure.</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

> **<u>Vitamin K deficiency bleeding</u>**

**Classic VKDB**

**first week** of life

easy bruising, mucosal and gastrointestinal bleeding

**Late-onset VKDB**

between **age 2 weeks and 6 months**

associated with **<span class="mark">intracranial hemorrhage</span>**🡪block cerebrospinal fluid flow🡪**<span class="mark">obstructive hydrocephalus</span>**

imaging: the **layered, hyperdense fluid collection** (red area) is located in the **posterior ventricles** on imaging due to supine positioning

> <img src="images/media/image10.png" style="width:3.80218in;height:2.30623in" />
>
> <img src="images/media/image11.png" style="width:4.97155in;height:6.61538in" />

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 22%" />
<col style="width: 77%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Idiopathic intracranial hypertension</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Risk factors</strong></td>
<td><p>Women of childbearing age <strong>(pregnancy)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Recent weight gain/obesity</strong></p>
<p>Medications (eg, <strong>retinoids/vitamin A</strong>, <strong>tetracyclines, growth hormone</strong>)</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td>Impaired CSF resorption &amp; intracranial venous hypertension</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical<br />
features</strong></td>
<td><p>Holocranial or lateralized <strong>headache/nausea/vomiting</strong></p>
<p><strong>positional headaches, worse when lying flat, improve with sitting</strong></p>
<p><strong>Visual changes (transient obscurations; vision loss; diplopia</strong> due to CN VI palsy<strong>)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Pulsatile tinnitus (due to increased vascular pulsations)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Retrobulbar pain/neck pain/back pain</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td><p><strong><mark>Complete ocular exam</mark>🡪Papilledema &amp; enlarged blind spots</strong></p>
<p><strong>Neuroimaging exclude space-occupying lesion</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>MRI</mark></strong> to rule out <strong>mass lesions/hydrocephalus</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>MR venography</mark></strong> to rule out <strong>venous thrombosis</strong></p>
<p>Or <strong><mark>CT scan</mark></strong>: faster and easier</p>
<p><strong><mark>Lumbar puncture</mark></strong>: elevated opening pressure (<strong>&gt;250</strong> mm H<sub>2</sub>O) <mark></mark></p>
<p><strong><mark>在正常影像之后，所有有 papilledema 的患者都应做 lumbar puncture</mark></strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td><p><strong><mark>Weight loss</mark></strong>, including bariatric surgery</p>
<p>Carbonic anhydrase inhibitor (<strong><mark>acetazolamide, topiramate</mark></strong>)</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**MR angiograms** indicated for

**Subarachnoid hemorrhage**

**Trigeminal neuralgia**

**<u>Normal Pressure Hydrocephalus/NPH</u>**

(communicating, nonobstructive hydrocephalus, frontal lobe and basal ganglia) **large ventricles with normal sulci on CT scan of the brain脑实质萎缩，所以颅压正常**

**Classic Triad <span class="mark">elderly patient</span>** presents with triad (**<span class="mark">步态，认知，尿失禁</span>**)

> **gait disturbance / <span class="mark">magnetic gait</span>=wobbly <span class="mark">似Parkinson</span>**
>
> **Incontinence=wet**
>
> **Dementia=wacky**

communicating hydrocephalus

可有**UMN signs**

**Initial Test**

> **<span class="mark">CT</span>: Enlarged ventricles, atrophy of brain**

**<span class="mark">Lumbar Puncture</span> Finding**

> **Normal pressure** with a **large amount of fluid**

**Definitive Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">high-volume lumbar puncture, Shunt</span>**

**Symptoms That Improve With Repeated LPs**

> **Ataxia**
>
> **Incontinence**

**Cognition Pearl**

> **Dementia** generally **does not improve much**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **<span class="mark">NPH = gait and bladder improve more than cognition</span>**

**NPH vs. WKS**

| **特征**     | **正常压力脑积水 (NPH)** | **Wernicke-Korsakoff (WKS)**         |
|:-------------|:-------------------------|:-------------------------------------|
| **共有症状** | 痴呆、尿失禁、步态异常   | 痴呆、尿失禁（严重时）、步态异常     |
| **眼部表现** | **无**                   | **眼球震颤、眼肌麻痹**               |
| **记忆特征** | 整体认知下降             | **显著的遗忘 + 虚谈 Confabulation)** |
| **病因**     | 脑脊液回吸收障碍         | **维生素 B1 缺乏 (酒精滥用)**        |
| **影像学**   | 脑室显著扩大             | **乳头体萎缩 (MRI)**                 |
| **首选治疗** | 脑室-腹腔分流术 (Shunt)  | **静脉补充 B1 (先 B1 后葡萄糖！)**   |

> <span class="mark">**看到“Wet, Wacky, Wobbly”：** 先别急，找有没有“**眼震 (Nystagmus)**”</span>。

**有眼震 + 喝酒🡪** **Wernicke**。

**没眼震 + 步态像脚粘在地板上 (Magnetic gait)🡪** **NPH**。

**<u>Wernicke encephalopathy</u>背**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 16%" />
<col style="width: 83%" />
</colgroup>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Associated conditions</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Chronic alcohol use</mark></strong> (most common)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Malnutrition</mark> (eg, anorexia nervosa, short-gut syndrome</strong>)</p>
<p><strong>Hyperemesis gravidarum</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Thiamine (B1) deficiency</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Encephalopathy</strong> (mammillary bodies)🡪<strong><mark>confusion</mark>, lethargy, disorientation</strong></p>
<p><strong>Oculomotor</strong> dysfunction</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>horizontal nystagmus</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>bilateral abducens palsy水平运动受限</mark></strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Gait ataxia <mark>(wide-based gait)</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Intravenous thiamine</mark> followed by <mark>glucose infusion</mark> <mark>（dextrose）</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 14%" />
<col style="width: 42%" />
<col style="width: 43%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>特征</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>Wernicke 脑病 (WE)</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>Korsakoff 综合征 (KS) 慢性，不可逆</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>阶段</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>急性期 / 亚急性</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>慢性期 / 后遗症期</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>可逆性</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>高度可逆（若能及时补 B1）</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>极难逆转（永久性脑损伤）</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>核心三联征</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>1. 意识障碍/脑病</strong></p>
<p><strong>2. <mark>眼球运动障碍 (眼震)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>3. <mark>步态共济失调</mark></strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>1. 严重的顺行性/逆行性遗忘</strong></p>
<p><strong>2. <mark>虚谈症 (Confabulation)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>3. 认知功能缺陷</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>病理受累部位</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>中脑导水管周围、乳头体、丘脑</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>主要是乳头体 (Mammillary bodies)、丘脑内侧核的萎缩</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>主要矛盾</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>代谢性急症导致的神经元功能障碍</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>结构性破坏（神经元死亡、胶质增生）</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>处理优先级</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>急诊静脉补充 B1</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>长期营养支持 + 记忆辅助训练</strong></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

** Wernicke (CAN)： Confusion (脑病), Ataxia (共济失调), Nystagmus (眼震)。**

** Korsakoff (PAC)： Psychosis (精神症状), Amnesia (遗忘), Confabulation (虚谈)。**

<img src="images/media/image12.png" style="width:2.50035in;height:1.55992in" /> <img src="images/media/image13.png" style="width:2.77995in;height:1.56789in" />

**NPH:** 脑室（中央的黑色区域）显著且圆钝地扩大，但最关键的是**大脑顶部的脑沟（脑回之间）非常挤压、狭窄**。这就是所谓的“不成比例”。

**AD：** 脑室虽然也大，但那是由于脑组织萎缩“腾出”的空间，所以你会看到**全脑的脑沟（包括外侧裂和顶部）都变得很宽、很深**。

| **特征** | **正常压力脑积水 (NPH)** | **脑萎缩 (Hydrocephalus ex vacuo)** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **病理本质** | **“胀”： <span class="mark">脑脊液回吸收不畅</span>**，把脑室顶开了。 | **“空”：** **<span class="mark">脑组织自己萎缩了</span>**，留下的空间被脑脊液填满了。 |
| **脑室表现** | **不成比例显著扩大**，尤其是侧脑室和第三脑室。 | 随脑组织萎缩程度而成比例扩大。 |
| **脑沟（Sulci）** | **<span class="mark">受压变窄</span>：** 尤其是头顶（高凸面）的脑沟很窄，被挤扁了。 | **<span class="mark">增宽变深</span>：** 脑回变细，脑沟里全是水。 |
| **脑池（Cisterns）** | 侧裂池（Sylvian fissures）可能显著增宽。 | 整体均匀增宽。 |

> **<u>Dandy Walker Cyst</u>**

**Noncommunicating** hydrocephalus in baby

Characteristic: **early morning vomiting** because of cyst at the floor of the 4th ventricle

> **Noncommunicating hydrocephalus in adult/elderly**: think **tumor**

<table style="width:100%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />
<col style="width: 86%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Cerebral vein &amp; venous sinus thrombosis</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Risk<br />
factors</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Thrombophilia (eg, <strong>factor V Leiden</strong>)</p>
<p><strong>Pregnancy &amp; postpartum</strong></p>
<p><strong>Oral contraceptive pills</strong></p>
<p><strong>Malignancy</strong></p>
<p><strong>Infection</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical<br />
features*</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Headache, <mark>↑ ICP</mark> (eg, vomiting, papilledema)</strong></p>
<p><strong>±Focal neurologic symptoms, seizures</strong></p>
<p><strong>Encephalopathy</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>MRI of the head with <strong><mark>MR venography</mark></strong> (<strong>↑ sensitivity</strong>)</p>
<p><strong>CT scan of the head with CT venography</strong> (rapid, ↑ availability)<strong>可正常</strong></p>
<p><strong>Elevated D-dimer</strong> (supports diagnosis)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Anticoagulation</mark> (unfractionated heparin or LMWH acutely)</strong></p>
<p><strong>CVST 即使有出血性梗死，治疗也通常仍是抗凝</strong>，有助于降低窦内压，改善症状</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p>*Presentation is highly variable &amp; often mixed, depending on thrombus location/distribution.</p>
<p><strong>ICP</strong> = intracranial pressure; <strong>LMWH</strong> = low molecular weight heparin.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**产后抽搐，先分两类：**

**1. Eclampsia: <span class="mark">高血压</span>**、蛋白尿、产前或产后都可

> 治疗：**<span class="mark">magnesium sulfate</span>**

**2. CVST：**头痛、papilledema、vomiting、seizure；CT可正常，**产后/高凝状态**

> 检查：**<span class="mark">MRV / CTV</span>**
>
> **脑静脉血栓** = **CVT (cerebral venous thrombosis)**，是**总称**\
> 指血栓发生在**脑静脉系统**，包括：

**硬脑膜静脉窦(cerebral venous sinus thrombosis/CVST)**

**皮质静脉/深静脉**（cortical veins, deep cerebral veins）

> **静脉窦血栓** = **CVST🡪堵在大静脉回流主干**，更偏指\
> **CVT（脑静脉血栓） ⊃ CVST（静脉窦血栓）**

**1) 静脉窦血栓（CVST）更像“颅压增高型”**

因为静脉窦，尤其是上矢状窦等，<span class="mark">和 **CSF 吸收** 有关</span>；堵了以后更容易出现：

> 头痛
>
> 清晨重
>
> 呕吐
>
> 乳头水肿
>
> 癫痫可有可无。

**2) 脑静脉血栓里如果是“皮质静脉血栓”更像“局灶皮层刺激型”**

孤立性皮质静脉血栓是 CVT 的一个少见亚型，常更容易出现：

> 局灶性神经功能缺损
>
> 癫痫
>
> 皮层附近水肿或出血性静脉梗死。

所以：

> <span class="mark">**窦为主** → 更偏**颅压增高**</span>
>
> <span class="mark">**皮质静脉为主** → 更偏**局灶缺损 / seizure**</span>
>
> **<span class="mark">MR venography / CT venography</span>** 都可用于诊断。

<img src="images/media/image14.png" style="width:4.59028in;height:2.99035in" />

> **<u>Meningitis</u>**

Characteristic: **neck stiffness, photophobia, nausea, vomiting**

Bugs for **baby**: **Group B strep, E.coli, Listeria**

Bugs for **adult**: **Neisseria, Echovirus, Strep Pneumo**

Bugs for **elderly**: **Listeria, Strep Pneumo**

**<u>Brudzinski sign</u>** positive: patient lies flat and looks upward. As neck is lifted, patient flexes the knees and hip flexes被动屈颈诱发髋膝屈曲

**<u>Kernig Sign</u>** positive: lies supine, hip 90 flex and extend knee; positive if resistance or pain屈髋90°后伸膝引起疼痛/抵抗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />
<col style="width: 86%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Bacterial meningitis in children</strong> (age &gt;1 month)</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Etiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><em>Streptococcus pneumoniae</em></p>
<p><em>Neisseria meningitidis</em></p>
<p><em>Haemophilus influenzae</em></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Fever</p>
<p>Age &lt;1: bulging fontanelle, irritability, poor feeding</p>
<p>Age &gt;1: signs of <strong>increased ICP</strong> (eg, headache, vomiting), <strong>meningeal signs</strong> (eg, nuchal rigidity)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Cerebrospinal fluid culture</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Vancomycin + ceftriaxone (or cefotaxime)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>± Dexamethasone</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Complications</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Intellectual/behavioral disabilities</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Hearing loss</mark></strong> （<em>Streptococcus pneumoniae</em> meningitis🡪inflammation of the cochlea and/or labyrinth）</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Hearing loss是小儿细菌性脑膜炎最常见的长期神经系统后遗症</mark>；地塞米松辅助治疗主要是为了降低这一风险。<mark>所有患脑膜炎康复的孩子，出院前或出院后早期必须进行听力测试</mark>（Audiology testing）。</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Cerebral palsy</strong></p>
<p><strong>Epilepsy</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

Suspected/confirmed **acute bacterial meningitis**:

Give **<span class="mark">dexamethasone</span>** **<span class="mark">before or with the first dose of antibiotics</span>**

To **reduce the host inflammatory response** triggered by bacterial lysis

To reduce **brain edema / ICP / neurologic sequelae**

To reduce **hearing loss**, especially in **Hib** and also in important adult **pneumococcal** disease

**Not for every meningitis**, and **not routine for generic encephalitis**

> **<u>Bacterial Meningitis</u>**

Protein ↑

Glucose ↓

Cells: **neutrophils**

Meningococcal meningitis🡪progress **within hours or a few days** to septic shock and death

> **<u>Viral Meningitis</u>**

Protein: normal to ↑

Glucose normal

Cells: **lymphocytes**

If **CSF <span class="mark">bloody: herpes</span>**

> **<u>Fungal Meningitis</u>**

Protein ↑

Glucose ↓

Cells: **lymphocytes**

**<u>Cryptococcus</u>: immunosuppressant, subacute, <span class="mark">ICP↑</span> (headache, vomiting, confusion)**

> **<u>TB Meningitis</u>**

Protein ↑

Glucose ↓

Cells: **Monocytes （lymphocytic predominance）**

Progress in **<span class="mark">weeks</span>**

↑risk in impaired immune function (**alcohol use disorder**, substance use disorder, malnutrition, immunomodulatory medications, or HIV)

> **<u>Encephalitis</u>**

Characteristic: **confusion, altered mental status, seizures, focal deficits, neck stiffness, photophobia, nausea, vomiting** - **neuro symptoms first🡪**encephalitis

Neurological symptoms first vs meningitis lacks that

**<u>Herpes encephalitis</u>**:

encephalitis symptoms + **<span class="mark">olfactory hallucinations</span>**

Treatment: **<span class="mark">IV acyclovir</span>**

**<u>HIV patient with Toxoplasmosis encephalitis</u>**:

encephalitis symptoms + **multiple ring enhancing lesion** in the brain

**<u>HIV patient with CMV encephalitis</u>**:

encephalitis symptoms + **<span class="mark">retinitis, esophagitis/colitis</span>**

Treatment: **<span class="mark">ganciclovir</span>**

**<u>Neurocysticercosis</u>脑囊虫病**

patient travelled to **South America** and encephalitis symptoms

由 **Taenia solium eggs** 引起

Imaging: CT - black fluid filled cysts囊性病灶、环形强化，后期可钙化

Cause: due to **undercooked pork**

**Tx: <span class="mark">albendazole</span>**

**Brain Cancers**

> **Most common** brain cancer: **metastasis / Meningioma**
>
> **Most common primary** cancer of the brain: <u>**astrocytoma**</u> - **<u>grade 4 glioblastoma multiforme</u>**
>
> **中老年，恶性、坏死、跨胼胝体**

**Liquefactive necrosis**

can cause **death within a year** of diagnosis and necrosis of BBB, not a tumor but rather a necrosis of BBB

This area of brain mostly water

因肿瘤生长快，中央容易缺血坏死, 同时 BBB 被破坏，增强影像可见环形强化和血管通透性增加

**GFAP positive, pseudopalisading necrosis, butterfly glioma**

> **<u>ring-enhancing lesion</u>**:

GBM

metastasis

abscess

toxoplasmosis

> Brain tumor with the **best prognosis: <u>meningioma</u>** - most common according to NBME
>
> **女性，脑外、硬膜附着、psammoma**

Brain grows around a mass - psammoma body

影像见脑外肿块，贴着硬脑膜, 可压迫周围脑组织，但通常不浸润

常与 <span class="mark">**NF2** 相关</span>

> **<u>Ependymoma</u>儿童、4<sup>th</sup> ventricle、梗阻性脑积水**

Characteristic: brain tumor in **children <span class="mark">儿童</span>**常见

**4<sup>th</sup> ventricle tumor**, **<span class="mark">obstruction</span> of CSF** → **noncommunicating hydrocephalus**

Imaging: CT - **enlarged ventricles**

儿童，头痛，呕吐，步态不稳，脑积水表现

**<u>choroid plexus papilloma</u>（脉络丛乳头状瘤）→ CSF 产生增多🡪婴儿 + 侧脑室肿块 + 脑积水**

**<span class="mark">婴儿</span>**多见

**侧脑室**多见

**CSF <span class="mark">production ↑</span>**

> **<u>Medulloblastoma</u><span class="mark">儿童</span>、小脑蚓部、晨吐、步态不稳**

**小儿，小脑，位于cerebellar vermis🡪压迫4th ventricle，可经CSF播散**

**early morning vomiting** because the tumor is at the 4th ventricle

**hydrocephalus**

**共济失调**

**小孩，走路不稳，truncal ataxia，早晨呕吐，posterior fossa mass**

> **<u>Schwannoma</u>单侧 hearing loss + tinnitus + vertigo**

**CN VIII听🡪ipsilateral sensorineural hearing loss, tinnitus and vertigo**

肿瘤变大后还可压到：

**<span class="mark">CN VII面</span>** → facial weakness / taste change

**<span class="mark">CN V三叉</span>** → facial sensory loss, decreased corneal reflex

bilateral vestibular schwannomas = **<span class="mark">NF2</span>**

> **<u>Craniopharyngioma</u><span class="mark">儿童</span>，鞍上，占位 + 视交叉压迫 + calcification**

Derived from **Rathke pouch remnants**

**Suprasellar mass**，所以会压迫：

<span class="mark">pituitary/hypothalamus</span>🡪**panhypopituitarism**🡪生长迟缓, hypothyroidism, Addison's disease, DI

<span class="mark">optic chiasm</span> **🡪 bitemporal hemianopsia**

**child, headache**

**Calcifications, “machine oil” cyst** contents

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>

<p>Derived from remnants of Rathke pouch</p>
<p>Bimodal age distribution (age 5-14 &amp; 50-75)</p>
</blockquote></td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Optic chiasm compression → bitemporal hemianopsia</p>
<p>Pituitary stalk compression → endocrinopathies</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Growth failure in children (↓ TSH or ↓ GH)</p>
<p>Pubertal delay in children or sexual dysfunction in adults (↓ LH &amp; FSH)</p>
<p>Diabetes insipidus (↓ ADH)</p></td>

<p><strong>Clinical features of hypopituitarism</strong></p>
</blockquote></th>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Etiology</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td><ul>
<li><p><strong>Pituitary</strong> causes</p>
<ul>
<li><p>Primary (eg, adenoma) or metastatic mass</p></li>
<li><p>Infiltration (eg, hemochromatosis, lymphocytic hypophysitis)</p></li>
<li><p>Hemorrhage (pituitary apoplexy) or infarction (Sheehan syndrome)</p></li>
</ul></li>
<li><p><strong>Hypothalamic</strong> causes</p>
<ul>
<li><p>Mass lesions</p></li>
<li><p>Radiation therapy</p></li>
<li><p>Infiltration (sarcoidosis)</p></li>
<li><p>Trauma to skull base</p></li>
<li><p>Infections (tuberculosis meningitis)</p></li>
</ul></li>
</ul></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Clinical presentation</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td><ul>
<li><p><strong>ACTH deficiency (secondary adrenal insufficiency)</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Postural hypotension, tachycardia, fatigue, weight loss, hypoglycemia, eosinophilia</p></li>
<li><p>Aldosterone normal (RAAS调节)</p></li>
</ul></li>
<li><p><strong>Hypothyroidism (central)</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Fatigue, cold intolerance, constipation, dry skin, bradycardia, slowed deep tendon reflexes</p></li>
<li><p>Low or inappropriately normal TSH, low free T4</p></li>
</ul></li>
<li><p><strong>Gonadotropins</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><p>Women: Amenorrhea, infertility</p></li>
<li><p>Men: Infertility, loss of libido</p></li>
</ul></li>
</ul></td>

> **<u>Pinealoma</u><span class="mark">青少年</span>，上视不能 + 头痛**

**Pineal germinoma**

**Child**, **headache**

**precocious puberty**

Compression of cerebral aqueduct🡪**<span class="mark">obstructive hydrocephalus</span>**

Compression of dorsal midbrain**🡪<span class="mark">Parinaud syndrome</span>**

**upward gaze palsy 上视不能**

**light-near dissociation 对光反射消失，辐辏反射正常**

**convergence-retraction nystagmus 内收性震颤（向上看发生眼球汇聚，回缩, 伴眼震）**

**<u>儿童 + bitemporal hemianopsia</u>**

**Craniopharyngioma**

**pituitary adenoma（成人更多）**

**optic pathway glioma**

**Strokes**

> Characteristic: **numbness, paralysis, difficulty walking and speaking, neurological deficit, drooping of face, wrist drop**
>
> **Hemorrhage** is bleeding
>
> **Ischemic** stroke is blockage
>
> Number one cause of stroke is **ischemia**
>
> 任何卒中题，先抓四件事：
>
> **突然发生**
>
> **定位症状**（脸、手、腿、说话、视野、平衡）
>
> **是前循环还是后循环**
>
> **是 cortical 还是 brainstem/cerebellar**

<img src="images/media/image16.png" style="width:3.63314in;height:2.20447in" /><img src="images/media/image17.png" style="width:3.76724in;height:2.19525in" />

> **<u>Anterior cerebral artery</u>=leg下肢**

**contralateral lower extremity weakness** (**somatosensory** deficit) **leg \> arm**

**<span class="mark">Urinary incontinence</span>**

ACA 主要供血**额顶叶内侧面**，也就是负责：

**对侧下肢运动/感觉**

**行为、执行功能**

**排尿控制**相关额叶区域

**临床情景**

突然走路怪

**对侧腿无力/感觉差，** 比手臂明显

可伴 **urinary incontinence**

executive/behavioral change可有 abulia意志缺失、行为改变

> **<u>Basilar Artery</u>**

Characteristic: **<span class="mark">Locked in syndrome</span>** - patient can only move their eyes

> **<u>Middle Cerebral Artery</u>=face/arm上肢远端、头面部**

Characteristic:

**Contralateral hemiparesis**

**wernicke's (language comprehension)**

**broca's (language production)**

<span class="mark">Eye deviation **towards** the stroke site</span>

MCA 常累及 frontal eye field（额叶注视中枢），而每个 frontal eye field 的作用是把双眼推向对侧。**“破坏性大脑卒中，眼看病灶；刺激性癫痫放电，眼看对侧。”**

因为**癫痫发作**是“过度激活”一个 frontal eye field，会把眼睛强行推向**对侧**；而**卒中**是“破坏”这个区域，所以出现相反结果。

MCA 供血大脑外侧面，覆盖：

**对侧face/arm** motor-sensory cortex

**语言区（优势半球）**

**视辐射部分区域**,

<img src="images/media/image18.jpeg" style="width:2.35417in;height:1.88056in" />**临床情景**

**优势半球**（通常左）：**aphasia <span class="mark">所有语言区均由MCA供血</span>**

**<span class="mark">Broca aphasia—frontal lobe</span>**

> “broken broca”🡪expressive aphasia表达性失语, sparse, nonfluent

**<span class="mark">Wernicke aphasia—temporal lobe</span>**

> “word salad”🡪fluent but meaningless

**global aphasia** –**大面积dominant MCA lesion**

非优势半球：

**hemineglect**

可有 gaze preference。

**<u>superior division</u>** 更偏 **Broca/face-arm weakness**

**<u>inferior division</u>** 更偏 **Wernicke/visual field symptoms**

**<u>大范围 MCA</u>** 才可能 **global aphasia**

> **<u>Posterior Inferior Cerebral Artery</u>**

Characteristic: Blurry vision, ataxia, vertigo, ipsilateral face and contralateral body

> **<u>Posterior Cerebral Artery</u>=<span class="mark">vision视力视野</span>**

PCA 供血：

枕叶occipital视觉皮层

颞叶下内侧部分

丘脑部分结构

**临床情景**

**Contralateral homonymous hemianopia** 对侧同向偏盲

**hallucinations, agnosia** (can't recognize things)

**macular sparing**

左 PCA 可有 alexia without agraphia。

> **<u>Posterior communicating artery</u>** = 连接颈内动脉和后大脑动脉的交通支，是 Willis 环前后循环的桥

**<span class="mark">P Com aneurysm</span>** 🡪compressing **<span class="mark">CN III</span>**

**ptosis 上睑下垂**

**"down and out" eye🡪复视**

**blown pupil 瞳孔散大**

> CN III 副交感纤维位于神经表面🡪先被压迫🡪先看到**pupil involved, fixed dilated pupil**
>
> **<u>Internal carotid artery</u> 或 <u>ACom aneurysm</u> → optic nerve / optic chiasm compression可导致**
>
> **<span class="mark">ACom / ICA 🡪 optic apparatus</span>**

**单眼视力下降**（optic nerve compression）

**双颞侧偏盲**（optic chiasm compression）

> Patient **right lower** face - **<span class="mark">left UMN</span>**
>
> **Right half** of **face** - <span class="mark">**CN 7** (bell's Palsy: **ipsilateral**)</span>

<img src="images/media/image19.jpeg" style="width:3.05764in;height:3.22292in" /><img src="images/media/image20.png" style="width:3.29167in;height:2.65625in" />

> **Midbrain**

CN: 3,4

Vessels: Posterior communicating artery

Problem: vision problem but macular sparing, hallucination, agnosia - Median Midbrain Syndrome

> **Pons**

CN: 5,6,7,8

Vessels: Anterior inferior communicating artery and basilar artery

Problem: hearing problem - Lateral Pontine Syndrome

> **Medulla**

CN: 9,10,11,12

Vessels: Posterior inferior communicating artery, basilar artery, and vertebral artery

Problem: vertigo, ataxia, ipsilateral face, contralateral body - Lateral Medullary Syndrome

> **Medulla**

CN: 9,10,11,12

Vessels: Vertebral artery, anterior spinal artery

Problem: Medial Medullary Syndrome

**Spinal Tracts**

> Dorsal column: vibration, sensation, consciousness; sensory

Originate from dorsal root ganglia and go through thalamus and end up in parietal lobe

> Corticospinal tract: motor

Originates from prefrontal gyrus → goes down → passes internal capsule (can cause **atonic seizures**) → medullary

> Spinocerebellar tract: depth perception; sensory

Originates in dorsal root → thalamus → cerebellum

Problem: depth perception, proprioception, ataxia

> Spinothalamic tract: pain, balance, temperature; sensory

Originates in dorsal root ganglia → in and out of thalamus → parietal

100% contralateral

(Image of Spinothalamic Tract pathway)

> Internal capsule: motor going in and out

Internal capsule has lenticulate striate arteries which are first affected by hypertension

> Thalamus: sensory goes in

Depolarized by calcium

**Parts of the Brain**

> Frontal lobe: broca’s speech area, early Alzheimer disease, atonic seizures, Schizophrenia
>
> Temporal lobe: sensory, hearing, balance, speech center: Wernicke’s

Problem: hallucination, seizures, Wernicke’s affected = “word salad”

> Parietal Lobe: lesion on non-dominant right side: hemineglect of left side

Dominant lobe is left side: long term memory (childhood memory)

Problem: late Alzheimer's

> Hippocampus: watershed area, similar to splenic flexure
>
> Corpus callosum

The fibers are ipsilateral if a person is left handed

The fibers are contralateral if the person is right handed

In the utero, by 8 weeks, you can determine if the fetus is left or right handed.

> Reticular activating system is for focus

Uses **norepinephrine** and **serotonin**

Lesion to the region: true ADD

Treatment: increase dopamine by exercise

**Hematomas**

> Epidural Hematoma

Characteristic: short interval, lucid interval immediately after getting hit on the side of the head

Vessel: **middle meningeal artery**

> Subdural Hematoma

Characteristic:

**older patient** who has fallen

**teenager on roller coaster**

**shaken baby** syndrome

**Lucid interval 2 weeks** after trauma

Vessel: **bridging veins**

> Subarachnoid Hemorrhage

Characteristic: “**worst headache of my life**”

**Nuchal rigidity, photophobia, fever**

Vessel: **anterior communicating artery**

If patient has **polycystic kidney disease**: **posterior communicating artery**

**Pathologies**

> ADD and ADHD

For diagnosis, the child has to be affected at 2 settings and have symptoms for more than 6 months

Treatment: stimulants

> Parkinson's Disease

Characteristic: 55-60 year old with resting tremor, cogwheel rigidity, bradykinesia

**TRAP**: **t**ardive dyskinesia, **r**esting tremor, **a**kinesia/bradykinesia, **p**ostural rigidity

Neurotransmitter: low dopamine

Substantia nigra

Treatment: levodopa/carbidopa

> Huntington Disease

Characteristic: 40-50 year old with psychosis, dementia, personality changes, and chorea like movements

Neurotransmitter: high dopamine, low GABA

Caudate nucleus/putamen

Genetic: autosomal dominant; trinucleotide repeats → anticipation

> Alzheimer's Disease

Characteristic: slow and progressive memory loss, anomia (difficulty naming objects), depression, confusion, psychosis and apraxia (inability to perform tasks), acalculia

Imaging: CT - diffuse atrophy of the brain

> Lewy Body Dementia

Characteristic: Presentation looks like alzheimer's (slow progressive memory loss) and they start to fall (ataxia) and visual hallucinations

Treatment: donepezil, levodopa, carbidopa

> Vascular Dementia (Multi infarct dementia)

Characteristic: stepwise decline; every time there is a stroke → function declines → another stroke → function declines

Cause: due to **atherosclerosis** and **HTN**

> Frontotemporal Dementia (Pick’s Disease)

Characteristic: fast onset, hyper arousability, hypersexuality, violent, mood swings began earlier than Alzheimer's, movement disorder comes later

> Pseudodementia

Characteristic: patient claims they have memory issues, they say “I don’t know” for every question, and they do not make eye contact

> Creutzfeldt-Jakob Disease

Characteristic: younger patient with emotional disturbance, rapid decline (week to months), myoclonus, jerky movements, dementia, seizures

Fast demyelination

Someone who has HIV: **JC virus** with fast progressive demyelination

> **<u>Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis (ALS)</u>**

Characteristic: patient in their **30s-40s** with **motor deficit**, no sensory, **upper motor neuron and lower motor neuron loss**

**Tongue fasciculations, dysphagia, facial weakness, inappropriate and persistent laughing**

**Most urgent** step/test: **<span class="mark">PFT</span>** (worried about the diaphragm)

**Best initial** diagnostic: **<span class="mark">EMG</span>**

Treatment if **diaphragm not affected**: **<span class="mark">riluzole</span>**

Treatment if **diaphragm affected**: **<span class="mark">intubate</span>**

> Myasthenia Gravis

Characteristic: 20-40 year with muscle weakness at the end of day, weakness in eyes with repetitive activity

Pathophysiology: postsynaptic ACh antibody

Best initial test: check for antibody

**EMG**: amplitude **goes down** with movement

Treatment: steroids, physostigmine, neostigmine

> Multiple Sclerosis

Characteristic: 20-40 year with waxing and waning of eye issues, muscle issues, urinary incontinence

Episodic comes and goes

Antibodies: anti-myelin

Best initial imaging: MRI

> Lambert Eaton

Characteristic: older than 50 year old patient, muscle gets better with movement, can't get out of chair

Antibodies: presynaptic calcium channel blocker antibodies

**EMG**: amplitude **goes up** with movement

Associated with **small cell carcinoma**

Releases PTH, ACTH, ADH, TSH

Treatment: treat underlying issue, neostigmine, pyridostigmine

> Wilson's Disease

Characteristic: patient in their 20s; too much copper so act similar to being intoxicated: confusion, altered mental status, gait issues shuffling

Flesher rings in eyes

Affected area of the brain: lenticular nucleus

findings</td>

<p><strong>Hepatic</strong> (acute liver failure, chronic hepatitis, cirrhosis)</p>
<p><strong>Neurologic</strong> (parkinsonism, gait disturbance, dysarthria)</p>
<p><strong>Psychiatric</strong> (depression, personality changes, psychosis)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;">Diagnosis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>↓ Ceruloplasmin</strong> &amp; <strong>↑ urinary copper excretion</strong></p>
<p><strong>Kayser-Fleischer rings</strong> on <strong><mark>slit-lamp examination</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>↑ Copper content on liver biopsy</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Chelators (eg, D-penicillamine, trientine)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Zinc (interferes with copper absorption)</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**Sleep**

> **Alpha waves**: when awake with eyes closed
>
> **Beta waves**: when awake with eyes open and in REM sleep
>
> **Delta waves**: night terrors, sleep walking, teeth grinding
>
> **Night Terrors vs Nightmares**

| **特征** | **夜惊 (Night Terrors)** | **梦魇 (Nightmares)** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **睡眠阶段** | **NREM (深睡期)** | **REM (快速眼动期)** |
| **发生时间** | 入睡后早期 (1-3小时) | 入睡后后期 (凌晨) |
| **意识状态** | **无法被唤醒/安抚** | 容易被唤醒 |
| **事后记忆** | **完全遗忘** | 能清晰记得梦境 |
| **处理** | **<span class="mark">Reassurance</span>**属于发育过程中的良性现象，通常在青春期前自行消失 | 心理支持/减轻压力 |

**Increased Intracranial Pressure**

> First sign: papillary edema → symptom of **headache**
>
> Second sign: esotropia → symptoms of **blurry vision** (eye inward)
>
> Third sign: anisocoria → no symptoms but **pupil sizes are different**

**Red Nucleus and Brain Herniation**

> Decorticate: Patient is herniated **up to the red nucleus**

Arms are flexed, legs are extended

> Decerebrate: patient is herniated **past the red nucleus**

Arms and legs are extended

**Headaches**

> Migraine Headache

Characteristic: photophobia, phonophobia, nausea, vomiting, aura, unilateral

Lasts more than 4 hours

Cause: Due to vasodilation effect that is caused by estrogen or high intracranial pressure

Diagnosis: CT

Treatment: NSAIDs, triptans

If in the ER, abort one with triptan

> Cluster Headache

Characteristic: rhinorrhea, lacrimation, worse when they lay down, unilateral - on eye

Can last from 15 minutes to 3 hours

Treatment: 100% oxygen, triptan

Prophylaxis: verapamil

> Tension Headache

Characteristic: band-like headache around the head that comes with stress

No photophobia, phonophobia

Greater than 30 minutes

Treatment: NSAIDs

**<u>Types of Vertigos</u>**

> **2 vertigos with hearing loss**

**<u>Meniere's disease</u> (episodic)**

Characteristic: **endolymphatic hydrops** (an accumulation within the membranous labyrinth)

**Mnemonic**: <span class="mark">men wear **VEST**</span>: **ve**rtigo, **s**ensorineural hearing loss, **t**innitus

Treatment:

**<span class="mark">lower the salt</span>**

**<span class="mark">急性🡪meclizine</span>第一代抗组胺药**

**surgery**

**<u>Labyrinthitis</u> (after a <span class="mark">viral infection)</span>** 迷路**同时累及<span class="mark">前庭+耳蜗</span>**

Treatment

**<span class="mark">treat the bug</span>**

**<span class="mark">meclizine</span>**

> **2 vertigo without hearing loss**

**<u>BPVV</u>**

Characteristic: brief episodes of vertigo provoked by changes in head position

**<span class="mark">Lasts less than 1 minute</span>**

With **nausea and nystagmus**

**Diagnosis: <span class="mark">Dicks Halpike Maneuver</span>**

**Treatment**

**initial treatment with <span class="mark">Epley’s maneuver</span>**

**<span class="mark">meclizine</span>**

**<u>Vestibular neuritis</u> (after <span class="mark">viral infection</span>)** **<span class="mark">CN VIII 前庭支炎症</span>**

> **一场大晕好几天，听力没掉是前庭炎**

Treatment:

**<span class="mark">treat the bug</span>**

**<span class="mark">meclizine</span>**

<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>Central vertigo</strong></th>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>常见病因</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>BPPV, vestibular neuritis</strong></p>
<p><strong>Ménière, Labyrinthitis</strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>stroke, MS, migraine</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><mark>眼震</mark></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p>多为<strong>水平</strong>/旋转、<strong>单向</strong></p>
<p><strong>凝视固定可抑制</strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p>可<strong>垂直</strong>、变向/<strong>双向</strong></p>
<p><strong>Not fatigable</strong></p>
<p><strong>凝视固定不能抑制</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>不稳但多能走</strong></td>

<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: center;"></th>
<th style="text-align: center;"><strong>Peripheral vertigo</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: center;"><strong>Central vertigo</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Etiologies</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>BPPV</p>
<p>Ménière disease</p>
<p>Vestibular neuritis</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Stroke (eg, cerebellar)</p>
<p>Multiple sclerosis</p>
<p>Migraine</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Nystagmus<br />
characteristics</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Never purely vertical</p>
<p>Inhibited by fixation of gaze</p>
<p>Fatigable (&lt;1-min duration)</p>
<p>Latency period (2-40 sec)</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>May have any trajectory</p>
<p>Not inhibited by fixation of gaze</p>
<p>Not fatigable (&gt;1-min duration)</p>
<p>No latency period</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Other possible<br />
neurologic signs</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Hearing loss/tinnitus may be present</p>
<p>Walking usually preserved</p>
<p>No other CNS symptoms</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Hearing loss/tinnitus absent</p>
<p>Severe postural instability</p>
<p>Other CNS symptoms (eg, headache, diplopia, weakness/numbness of face or limbs, dysarthria) often present</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="3" style="text-align: left;">BPPV = benign paroxysmal positional vertigo.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**Central vertigo needed to be <span class="mark">evaluated for cerebellar stroke or hemorrhage</span> if:**

> **prominent stroke risk factors (eg, hyperlipidemia, hypertension, diabetes mellitus).**
>
> **new-onset headache.**
>
> **neurologic signs/symptoms (eg, weakness/numbness of the face or limbs, dysarthria).**

<span class="mark">**Peripheral眼震🡪unidirectional**，眼震方向不会随左右看的方向改变</span>

<span class="mark">**Central眼震🡪bi-directional**，眼震方向随左右看的方向改变（前庭神经核以上调节出问题，**眼震方向不固定，垂直眼震down-beating）**</span>

**Seizures**

> Partial - part of brain

Frontal

> Generalized - entire brain

Temporal

> Simple Partial seizure (focal aware seizure) - no loss of consciousness

Characteristic: don't lose consciousness

Treatment first line: carbamazepine, phenytoin

Treatment second line: valproic acid, lamotrigine

> Complex Partial seizure (focal seizure with impaired awareness)

Characteristic: lose consciousness but don't hit ground

Sitting at table, zones out, lip smacking - complex partial seizure

Treatment first line: carbamazepine, phenytoin

Treatment second line: valproic acid, lamotrigine

> Atonic Seizures - Generalized

Characteristic: lose tone → drop to the floor

Treatment first line: valproic acid, lamotrigine

Treatment second line: carbamazepine, phenytoin

> Tonic seizure - Generalized

Characteristic: stiffness and urinary incontinence

Treatment first line: valproic acid, lamotrigine

Treatment second line: carbamazepine, phenytoin

> Absence Seizure

Characteristic: Kid zones out in class, teacher has to repeat stuff

Treatment: ethosuximide

> **<u>Status Epilepticus</u>**

Characteristic: seizure, seizure, seizure (one on top of the other); talk about it in minutes

Treatment:

**<span class="mark">Check airway, breathing, circulation</span>**

**<span class="mark">IV lorezapam</span>**

If doesn't work, **<span class="mark">fosphenytoin or phenytoin</span>**

> Difference between syncope vs seizure

Syncope - recover consciousness and no loss of urinary incontinence

Seizure - disoriented, bite tongue, or urinary incontinence

**<u>Brainstem lesion localization</u>**

**脑神经核在脑干的位置：**

> **CN III, IV → midbrain（中脑）**
>
> **CN V, VI, VII, VIII → pons（脑桥）**
>
> **CN IX, X, XI, XII → medulla（延髓）**
>
> Lowest number = cranial nerve
>
> Highest level = spinal level

(Visual relationships of CNs and brain areas)

> **<span class="mark">no response to light on right side = CN 3</span> ———— @ Mid brain on right**
>
> **CN III 带有副交感纤维，支配：**
>
> **sphincter pupillae**
>
> **ciliary muscle**
>
> **所以右侧 CN III 受损可导致：**
>
> **右眼瞳孔散大**
>
> **对光反射消失**
>
> **还可合并：**

**ptosis**

**“down and out” eye**

> **<span class="mark">looks double - CN 4</span> ———— Mid brain on left side**
>
> **CN IV = trochlear nerve（滑车神经）支配 superior oblique muscle（上斜肌）**
>
> **上斜肌主要功能：**
>
> **使眼球 向下**
>
> **内旋**
>
> **在内收位帮助向下看**
>
> **所以 CN IV 麻痹时会出现：**
>
> **vertical diplopia（垂直复视）**
>
> **下楼、看书时更明显**
>
> **病人会头向对侧倾斜来代偿**
>
> **<span class="mark">eye towards nose = CN 6</span> ———— In pons**
>
> **CN VI = abducens nerve（外展神经）**
>
> **功能：支配 lateral rectus**
>
> **作用：让眼球 外展**
>
> **受损后,如果右侧 CN VI 损伤：**
>
> **右眼不能外展**
>
> **右眼在静息时会被内直肌拉向内侧**
>
> **所以表现为：eye is pulled toward the nose, 同时出现 horizontal diplopia**
>
> **<span class="mark">dysphagia = CN 9,10</span> ———— In medulla**
>
> **CN IX、X 都参与：9 吞咽起始，10 咽喉运动与发声**
>
> **吞咽**
>
> **咽反射**
>
> **软腭/咽喉协调**
>
> **所以出现：**
>
> **dysphagia**
>
> **gag reflex 异常**
>
> **palate droop**
>
> **声音变化**
>
> **更该想到 medulla lesion**
>
> **<span class="mark">hoarseness voice = CN 10</span> —————————————— @ medulla on right**
>
> **迷走神经支配：**
>
> **喉肌**
>
> **咽部肌肉**
>
> **软腭部分运动**
>
> **所以 CN X 受损会出现：**
>
> **hoarseness**
>
> **dysphagia**
>
> **uvula 偏斜**
>
> **palate droop**
>
> **<span class="mark">tongue deviated left - CN 12</span> ———— Medulla on left side 舌偏向病变侧**

** CN III → midbrain 开眼缩瞳看上内下**

> **ptosis, blown pupil, no light reflex**

** CN IV → midbrain 看楼梯会重影**

> **vertical diplopia, worse looking down**

** CN VI → pons 外展，坏了眼内斜**

> **cannot abduct eye, eye pulled toward nose**

** CN IX → medulla 9吞，10说，12伸舌偏**

> **dysphagia, impaired gag**

** CN X → medulla**

> **hoarseness, dysphagia, uvula deviation**

** CN XII → medulla**

> **tongue deviates toward lesion**

**Pathogens**

> **<u>Botulism</u>**

Characteristic: **descending paralysis, hypotonia**

**Under 6 months** of age: **honey**

**4-year-old:** **improperly canned food**

Treatment: **<span class="mark">antitoxin</span>** and/or **<u>intubate</u>**

> **<u>Guillan Barre</u>**

Characteristic: **ascending paralysis**

**2 weeks** after GI or respiratory infection

Antibody: **anti-ganglioside**

Lumbar puncture shows **high protein**, no bugs

**Nerve lesions**

> Erb’s Duchenne

Characteristic:

Baby: due to lateral traction of the neck in delivery

Adult: trauma leading to neck traction

Cranial Nerves: C₅ - C₇

Presentation: Arm is extended, adducted and medially rotated

Treatment: keep a close eye on it

> Klumpke’s Palsy

Characteristic:

Baby: upward force on arm during delivery

Adult: trauma from grabbing a tree branch

Cranial Nerves: C₈ - T₁

Can also injure the sympathetic cord of cervicals → Horner’s Syndrome (ptosis, miosis, anhydrosis)

Presentation: claw hand

Treatment: resolves on its own

> Carpal Tunnel Syndrome

Characteristic: Pain in digits 1, 2, 3 with numbness and tingling

Worse with use

Damage to the superior condyle distal 1/3 rd

Nerve: median nerve

Treatment: brace and NSAIDs

> Winged Scapula

Characteristic: inability to attach scapula to thoracic cage → cannot abduct arm in horizontal position

Nerve:

Long Thoracic = medial

<img src="images/media/image21.jpeg" style="width:2.31389in;height:1.4in" />MCC: mastectomy

Accessory Nerve = lateral

Leads to trapezius muscle paralysis

> Damage to **humerus**

Nerve: **<span class="mark">axillary nerve</span>** 🡪**shoulder abduction weakness**

Cause: **anterior shoulder dislocation**

> Damage to **mid shaft of humerus**

Nerve: **<span class="mark">radial nerve</span> → wrist drop**

> The **<span class="mark">ulnar nerve</span>** is commonly injured at the **elbow or wrist (Guyon Canal)**

Characteristic: sensory loss over the medial 1 ½ digits

Trauma to the **hook of hamate**

> Injured at **elbow**🡪**<span class="mark">ulnar symptoms</span>** + **weak wrist flexion**
>
> **<u>Cauda Equina Syndrome</u>**

Characteristic: Pt presents with **severe back pain** and **urinary retention** and **cannot feel their wipe**

**LMN**

Saddle anesthesia and urinary retention, decreased anal tone

Cause: Due to **disc herniation, trauma, tumor**

**Asymmetrical**

**Gradual development**

**<span class="mark">Hyporeflexia</span>**

Levels: **S₃-S₅**

> **<u>Conus Medullaris</u>**

Characteristic: back pain, radicular pain, distal paresis, perianal numbness, urinary incontinence

**Symmetrical**

**Sudden onset**

**<span class="mark">Hyperreflexia</span>**

Levels: **L₁-S₂**

**<u>STROKE</u>**

**Stroke Basics**

**Most Common Type**

> **<span class="mark">Ischemic stroke</span>** is **more common** than hemorrhagic stroke

**Definitions**

> **Ischemic stroke** = clot blocks blood flow
>
> **Hemorrhagic stroke** = vessel rupture

**Greatest Risk Factor**

> **<span class="mark">Hypertension</span>**

**<span class="mark">Initial Test</span> for Suspected Stroke or TIA**

> **<span class="mark">Non-contrast CT head</span>**

**<span class="mark">Most Accurate</span> Imaging**

> **<span class="mark">MRI</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Emergent CTA of head and neck</span>**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> First question in stroke management:

Is there blood?

Get the non-contrast CT

**<u>Transient ischemic attack/TIA</u>**

> **局灶性神经功能缺损**
>
> **持续时间短（20 分钟）**
>
> **完全恢复**

**接下来关键不是只停留在“TIA”，而是要<span class="mark">找 栓子来源</span>。**

**题干特意给了一个很重要的高危线索：bioprosthetic mitral valve**

**虽然 机械瓣 更容易血栓，但 bioprosthetic valve 也仍然可能发生血栓。\
如果瓣膜上形成血栓，<u>左心系统的血栓</u>就可以脱落进入体循环，引起：**

> **TIA**
>
> **stroke**
>
> **limb ischemia**
>
> **其他动脉栓塞**

**而 mitral valve 因为血流动力学特点，也比较容易形成这类问题。**

**TIA + prosthetic valve = 先查心源性栓塞来源🡪echocardiography**

**<span class="mark">TIA or stroke causes</span>**

**<u>Under 50</u>**

**Autoimmune**

**Cardiolipin**

**cocaine**

**VDRL 筛查梅毒**

**hypercoagulable state**

**<u>Stroke Syndromes by Vessel</u>**

**<u>ACA Stroke</u>**

> **Contralateral lower extremity weakness 对侧（单侧！）; 若双侧下肢🡪spinal cord**
>
> **<span class="mark">Urinary incontinence</span>**

**<u>Basilar Artery Stroke</u>**

> Patient can only blink their eyes **“l<span class="mark">ocked-in syndrome</span>”**
>
> **保留理解、意识、眼上下，损害四面、颈肩、不讲话**

**<u>MCA Stroke</u>**

> Contralateral hemiparesis--face/arm
>
> Major **<span class="mark">speech</span>** findings
>
> **Broca and Wernicke** involvement

优势半球（通常左）：**aphasia**

**Broca aphasia—frontal lobe**

**Wernicke aphasia—temporal lobe**

或 **global aphasia**

非优势半球：

**hemineglect**

可有 gaze preference

**<u>superior division</u>** 更偏 **Broca/face-arm weakness**

**<u>inferior division</u>** 更偏 **Wernicke/visual field symptoms**

**<u>大范围 MCA</u>** 才可能 **global aphasia**

**<u>PICA Stroke</u>**

> **Vertigo**
>
> **Ataxia**
>
> **Ipsilateral face findings**
>
> **Contralateral body findings**

**<u>PCA Stroke</u>**

> **Agnosia (can't recognize things)**
>
> **Hallucinations**
>
> **<span class="mark">Contralateral homonymous hemianopsia对侧同向偏盲</span>**
>
> **Macular sparing**

**Step 2 Vessel Memory**

> **<span class="mark">ACA = leg</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">MCA = face/arm/language</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">PCA = vision</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">PICA = crossed brainstem findings</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Basilar = locked-in type picture</span>**

<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical characteristics of major stroke subtypes</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Ischemic<br />
(thrombotic)</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Atherosclerotic risk factors (eg,<strong> uncontrolled hypertension, diabetes mellitus</strong>),</p>
<p>± history of <strong>transient ischemic attack</strong></p>
<p>Local obstruction of an artery (eg, carotid, cerebral, vertebral)</p>
<p>Symptoms may alternate with periods of improvement (<strong><mark>stuttering progression</mark></strong>)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Ischemic<br />
(embolic)</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>History of <mark><strong>cardiac disease</strong> (eg, <strong>atrial fibrillation, endocarditis</strong>) or <strong>carotid atherosclerosis</strong></mark></p>
<p>Onset of symptoms is <strong>abrupt &amp; usually maximal at the start</strong></p>
<p>Multiple infarcts in <strong>different vascular territories</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Intracerebral<br />
hemorrhage</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>History of <strong>uncontrolled hypertension, coagulopathy, illicit drug use (eg, amphetamines, cocaine)</strong></p>
<p>Symptom progression over <strong>minutes to hours</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Focal neurologic symptoms</mark> that appear early</strong>, followed by features of <strong>increased intracranial pressure</strong> (eg, <strong>vomiting, headache, <mark>bradycardia</mark>, reduced alertness</strong>)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Cushing triad</mark>: hypertension, bradycardia, irregular respirations</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Spontaneous<br />
subarachnoid<br />
hemorrhage</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Bleeding from arterial <strong>saccular ("berry") aneurysm</strong> or <strong>arteriovenous malformation</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Severe headache</mark> at onset</strong></p>
<p>Meningeal irritation (eg, <strong><mark>neck stiffness</mark></strong>)</p>
<p>Focal deficits uncommon</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table style="width:100%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 19%" />
<col style="width: 29%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="3" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Common <mark>lacunar stroke</mark> syndromes*</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Syndrome</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Typical location</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Clinical features</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Pure motor<br />
hemiparesis</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Posterior limb<br />
of internal capsule</strong></p>
<p><strong>corticospinal tract</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Contralateral weakness (face, arm, leg)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>No sensory deficits</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Ataxic<br />
hemiparesis</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Posterior limb<br />
of internal capsule</strong></p>
<p><strong>与小脑协调有关的深部纤维连接</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Contralateral weakness &amp; limb ataxia (leg &gt; arm)</strong></p>
<p><strong>No sensory deficits</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Pure sensory stroke</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Posterior thalamus</strong></p>
<p><strong>丘脑是感觉传入的重要中继站</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Contralateral hemisensory loss (face, arm, leg)</strong></p>
<p><strong>No motor deficits</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Dysarthria–clumsy hand syndrome</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Basis pontis</strong></p>
<p><strong>corticobulbar fibers</strong></p>
<p><strong>corticospinal fibers</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Facial weakness &amp; dysarthria</strong></p>
<p><strong>Contralateral hand weakness &amp; clumsiness</strong></p>
<p><strong>No sensory deficits</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="3" style="text-align: left;">*These syndromes typically lack cortical signs (eg, aphasia, agnosia, neglect, apraxia, hemianopia), seizures, and mental status changes.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

lacunar stroke: 深部小穿通动脉闭塞，常见于长期：高血压、糖尿病🡪小血管病变（lipohyalinosis / microatheroma）

梗死发生在：内囊、丘脑、脑桥等深部结构。 会影响传导束、感觉通路、运动通路

腔隙性卒中的最大特点：有明确的“纯运动”或“纯感觉”缺损，但没有 **<span class="mark">cortical signs = 对侧偏瘫 + 高级功能异常</span>**

**<span class="mark">aphasia（失语）</span>🡪多见左半球优势侧**

**<span class="mark">neglect（忽略）</span>🡪多见右顶叶**

**apraxia（失用），agnosia（失认）**

**<span class="mark">cortical sensory loss</span> (graphesthesia 书写觉/ stereognosis立体觉)**

**<span class="mark">hemianopia</span>（偏盲），gaze preference（凝视偏向）**

**seizures**

**mental status changes**

**内囊后肢里走的是非常密集的：**

**corticospinal tract**

**corticobulbar fibers**

所以这里一个小梗死就能造成：对侧面、臂、腿一起无力 **<span class="mark">internal capsule stroke = 纯运动性对侧face-arm-leg weakness</span>**

临床情景：一个长期高血压患者突然出现：右脸下垂、右上肢无力、右下肢无力，但感觉正常、没有失语、没有偏盲🡪内囊后肢腔隙梗死

2\. **<u>Ataxic hemiparesis</u>**（共济失调性偏瘫）

因为**病灶同时影响运动通路、与小脑协调有关的深部纤维连接**

所以会表现成像 weakness，又像 cerebellar incoordination

临床情景：病人说一边腿没力，走路“发飘”“不听使唤”，指鼻试验也笨拙

3\. **<u>Pure sensory stroke</u>**（纯感觉性卒中）

**丘脑是感觉传入的重要中继站，所以小梗死在这里会导致对侧半身感觉缺失**

临床情景：病人突然觉得半边脸麻、同侧手麻、同侧腿麻

4\. **<u>Dysarthria–clumsy hand syndrome</u>**（构音障碍-笨手综合征）

**Basis pontis（脑桥基底部），这里有corticobulbar fibers、corticospinal fibers**

临床情景：患者突然讲话含糊，一只手系扣子很笨，面部轻微无力

</blockquote></td>

</blockquote></td>

**<span class="mark"><u>Brainstem stroke</u>= 交叉体征</span> (<span class="mark">对侧身体偏瘫+同侧颅神经受损</span>)**

脑干里有两类重要结构挤在一起：

<span class="mark">长束（运动/感觉通路）</span>

<span class="mark">脑神经核</span>

最经典表现：**<span class="mark">对侧身体偏瘫+同侧颅神经受损</span>** (crossed findings / crossed neurologic deficits)

例如：

一侧面瘫 + 对侧肢体无力

一侧眼球运动障碍 + 对侧偏瘫

一侧舌偏 + 对侧偏瘫

**<u>Malignant hemispheric infarction (MHI)</u>**

life-threatening, <span class="mark">**ischemic stroke🡪massive cerebral edema** and/or **hemorrhagic transformation**:</span>

**Cerebral edema** results from endothelial dysfunction and breakdown of the blood-brain barrier.  The resulting mass effect and ↑ICP can cause brain herniation (eg, herniation of the temporal lobe onto the brainstem).

**Hemorrhagic transformation** occurs when blood extravasates from injured cerebral vessels into the brain parenchyma.  The **larger the infarct, the greater the risk** of hemorrhagic transformation.

occlusion of a **large vessel (eg, internal carotid, proximal MCA)**

initially present with **severe deficits** (eg, right-sided weakness, hemisensory loss, aphasia) due to the large affected area of the brain. 

occurs in the **first 48 hours** but can be more **gradual (up to a week)**.

**<span class="mark">Emergent noncontrast CT scan</span>** of the head🡪determine the extent of edema and/or hemorrhage

Treatment

**<span class="mark">Decompressive hemicraniectomy</span>**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 84%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong><u>Clinical features of brain herniation</u></strong></p>
<p>Brain herniation can rapidly lead to <strong>respiratory failure</strong></p>
<p>Best next step: <strong>intubation and mechanical ventilation</strong> (airway and breathing of the ABCs). </p>
<p><strong>preventing further bleeding</strong></p>
<p><strong>reversing anticoagulation</strong></p>
<p><strong>controlling blood pressure</strong></p>
<p><strong>lowering the intracranial pressure</strong></p>
<p><strong>hyperventilation</strong></p>
<p><strong>osmotic agents [eg, mannitol]</strong></p>
<p><strong>neurosurgical hematoma evacuation</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Herniation type</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Common features</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Subfalcine</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Herniation of cingulate gyrus underneath falx cerebri</p>
<p>No pupillary involvement, consciousness often preserved</p>
<p><strong><mark>Contralateral leg weakness</mark> (ipsilateral ACA compression)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Uncal</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Herniation of uncus (<strong>medial temporal lobe</strong>) under tentorium cerebelli</p>
<p><strong><mark>Ipsilateral dilated &amp; fixed pupil</mark> (ipsilateral <mark>oculomotor nerve [CN III]</mark> compression)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Early: <mark>contralateral hemiparesis</mark> (ipsilateral cerebral peduncle compression)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Late: <mark>ipsilateral hemiparesis</mark> (contralateral cerebral peduncle compression)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Central</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Caudal displacement of diencephalon &amp; brainstem</p>
<p>Rupture of paramedian basilar artery branches</p>
<p><strong>Bilateral midposition &amp; <mark>fixed pupils</mark> (loss of sympathetic &amp; parasympathetic innervation)</strong></p>
<p><strong>中央疝时，间脑和中脑向下移位，会损伤控制瞳孔的交感、副交感🡪midposition, fixed pupils</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Decorticate (flexor) → decerebrate (extensor) posturing</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Decorticate → decerebrate 表示脑损伤从红核以上进展到红核以下/脑干，常见于进行性脑疝，提示病情恶化</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>昏迷 + 高血压/缓脉/呼吸不规则（Cushing triad）+ 中位固定瞳孔 + 去大脑强直</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Tonsillar</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Herniation of cerebellar tonsils through foramen magnum</p>
<p><strong><mark>Coma, loss of CN reflexes, flaccid paralysis, respiratory arrest</mark> (brainstem compression)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>ACA</strong> = anterior cerebral artery; <strong>CN</strong> = cranial nerve.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<img src="images/media/image23.jpeg" style="width:2.87975in;height:2.87975in" /> <img src="images/media/image24.png" style="width:3.62782in;height:2.76361in" />

**<u>Cushing triad</u>** = **<span class="mark">increased ICP / impending herniation</span>🡪脑干受压**

**高血压**（常见脉压增大）

**心动过缓**

**呼吸不规则/呼吸减慢**

**<span class="mark">Temporal trauma</span> + lucid interval 🡪 epidural hematoma + Cushing triad → uncal herniation → CN III compression**

<img src="images/media/image25.png" style="width:5.14077in;height:3.53164in" />

**<u>Hemorrhagic Stroke Management</u>**

**If Blood Pressure Is Severely Elevated**

> **Lower BP gradually**

**Drugs Used**

> **<span class="mark">IV labetalol</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">IV nicardipine</span>**

**Why Gradual Reduction?**

> To **avoid loss of cerebral perfusion pressure**

**If BP Is Not in Extreme Range/lower than 220/120**

> **<span class="mark">Sit the patient up</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Hyperventilate</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Mannitol</span>-type measures**

**If BP higher than 220/120**

**<span class="mark">Labetalol</span>**

**<span class="mark">IV nitroprusside</span>**

**Drop it no more than 25%**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> Lowering BP too aggressively can worsen ischemia by dropping brain perfusion

**<u><span class="mark">Ischemic Stroke</span> Management</u>**

**Non-Hemorrhagic Stroke <span class="mark">Within 4 Hours溶栓！</span>**

> **<span class="mark">tPA （IV alteplase）</span>**

**What tPA Lyses**

> **Arterial clots**
>
> **Venous clots**

<table style="width:100%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 24%" />
<col style="width: 75%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Criteria for <strong><mark>thrombolytics</mark> in stroke</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Inclusion criteria</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Ischemic stroke</strong> with <strong>disabling neurodeficits</strong></p>
<p>Symptom onset <strong>&lt;3-4.5 hr </strong>before treatment initiation</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Strict exclusion criteria</strong>*</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>ICH</strong> on CT scan, history of ICH, suspected SAH</p>
<p><strong><mark>Ischemic stroke in the past 3 months</mark></strong></p>
<p>Intraaxial neoplasm, recent intracranial or intraspinal surgery</p>
<p>Blood pressure &gt;185/110 mm Hg</p>
<p>Current anticoagulant use with <strong>INR &gt;1.7, PT &gt;15 sec, or ↑ active PTT</strong></p>
<p>Glucose &lt;60 mg/dL or platelets &lt;100,000 mm<sup>3</sup></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p>*Careful consideration given for patients with recent major surgery, MI, or GI/GU bleeding.</p>
<p>GI/GU = gastrointestinal/genitourinary; ICH = intracranial hemorrhage; MI = myocardial infarction; SAH = subarachnoid hemorrhage.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**Non-Hemorrhagic Stroke <span class="mark">After 4 Hours</span> <span class="mark">抗板！</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Aspirin</span>**

**If Already <span class="mark">on Aspirin</span> and Still Has Stroke**

**<span class="mark">Add dipyridamole</span>**

> **Dipyridamole = 抗血小板药 + 血管扩张药，常用于预防血栓，尤其常和 aspirin 联合用于中风二级预防**

<img src="images/media/image26.png" style="width:5.12346in;height:1.0804in" />

**Or <span class="mark">Stop aspirin🡪</span>give <span class="mark">clopidogrel</span>**

<img src="images/media/image27.png" style="width:5.0251in;height:1.19118in" />

**In This Teaching Framework**

> **Do not use aspirin and clopidogrel together for stroke**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> Time window matters
>
> **<span class="mark">CT must first exclude hemorrhage</span>**

**<u>Determining the Cause of Stroke</u>**

**In a Patient Over 50, Consider**

> **<span class="mark">Emboli</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Carotid stenosis</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Atrial fibrillation</span>**

**If <span class="mark">Carotid Stenosis</span> Suspected**

> **<span class="mark">Doppler ultrasound</span>**

**When to <span class="mark">Operate</span> <span class="mark">(endarectomy)</span>**

> **Greater than 70% occlusion**
>
> **Less than 100%**

**If <span class="mark">AFib</span> Suspected**

> First test = **<span class="mark">EKG</span>**

**AFib on EKG**

> **No P waves**

**If EKG Is Normal but AFib Still Suspected**

> **<span class="mark">Holter monitor / ambulatory monitor</span>**

**Teaching Pearl from This Framework**

> If stroke is thought to be **<span class="mark">due to AFib</span>**, **<span class="mark">start anticoagulation early</span> even before confirmatory testing**

**If <span class="mark">Vegetation</span> Source Suspected**

> **<span class="mark">Echocardiogram</span>**

**Teaching Pearl from This Framework**

> If stroke is suspected from a **<span class="mark">vegetation</span>, <span class="mark">anticoagulation</span> is still started in this system**

**In Patients <span class="mark">Under 50</span>, Important Causes Include**

> **Cocaine**
>
> **Hypercoagulable states**
>
> **Tumors**
>
> **Autoimmune disease**
>
> **Syphilis**

**Secondary Prevention**

> **Stop smoking**
>
> **Lower blood pressure**
>
> **Lower LDL**
>
> **Raise HDL**
>
> **Control diabetes**

**DELIRIUM VS DEMENTIA**

**<u>Delirium</u>**

> **Reversible**
>
> **Acute**
>
> **Hyperactivity (agitation), hypoactive (lethargy, somnolence)**
>
> Commonly has **<span class="mark">hallucinations</span>**

**<u>Dementia</u>**

> **Irreversible**
>
> **Chronic**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Acute mental status change with reversibility = think delirium**
>
> **Gradual chronic decline = think dementia**

<p>Electrolyte disturbances (eg, hyponatremia, hypercalcemia)</p>
<p>Metabolic derangements (eg, volume depletion, vitamin B<sub>12</sub> deficiency, hyperglycemia)</p>
<p>Systemic illnesses (eg, congestive heart failure, hepatic failure, malignancy)</p>
<p>CNS conditions (eg, seizure, stroke, head injury, subdural hematoma)</p>
</blockquote></td>

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>Management of hospital delirium</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Reduce noise, improve room lighting, open window blinds during the day &amp; avoid frequent room changes</p>
<p>Constant observation by a familiar person at the bedside, preferably a family member </p>
<p>Nonpharmacologic sleep aids for insomnia</p>
<p>Early mobilization &amp; minimal use of physical restraints</p>
<p>Visual &amp; hearing aids when appropriate</p>
<p>Early volume repletion for dehydrated patients</p>
<p>Adequate pain control</p>
<p>Aggressive chronic disease management (eg, diabetes mellitus, COPD)</p>
<p>Reduce polypharmacy</p>
<p>Monitor &amp; treat for metabolic disturbances, infections &amp; drug toxicity</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 22%" />
<col style="width: 77%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Delirium symptom management*</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Nonpharmacologic</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Environment: noise reduction, intervention grouping</p>
<p>Sleep facilitation: bright day/dim night lighting</p>
<p>Personal interaction: reassurance, physical touch</p>
<p>Constant observation: family, professional sitters</p>
<p>Mobilization: out of bed, restraint avoidance</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Pharmacologic</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Pain management: nonopioid</mark></strong> when possible</p>
<p><strong><mark>Antipsychotics</mark></strong>: <strong><mark>low-dose haloperidol</mark></strong> (off-label indication)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Benzodiazepines</mark></strong>: <strong>antipsychotic failure/withdrawal</strong> syndromes</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">*Definitive management is identification and treatment of the underlying cause(s).</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<span class="mark">**<u>Benzodiazepines</u>** 🡪 **agitation in young**</span> patients

Typically **contraindicated in older patients**

at increased risk for adverse events (eg, withdrawal, dependence, motor impairment)

**worsening agitation (paradoxic effect)**

metabolize benzodiazepines slowly, making their effects very long-lasting.

<table style="width:68%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />
<col style="width: 54%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Common complications of <strong>delirium</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Short term</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Disorientation, falls</p>
<p>Immobility, pressure ulcers</p>
<p>Poor intake, dehydration</p>
<p>Aspiration pneumonia</p>
<p>Prolonged hospitalization</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Long term</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Persistent delirium</p>
<p>Nursing home placement</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Permanent</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Cognitive decline/dementia</strong></p>
<p><strong>Death</strong>: ~20% mortality at 6 months</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>PARKINSON DISEASE</u>**

**Typical Age Group**

> Older patients
>
> Classically **over 50**

**Classic Features**

> **Mask-like facies**
>
> **Resting tremor**
>
> **Rigidity**
>
> **Akinesia**
>
> **Postural instability**

**Treatment by Age / Severity**

**<span class="mark">Mild</span> Disease, <span class="mark">Under 50</span>🡪抗胆碱药🡪震颤为主，年轻人**

> **<span class="mark">Benztropine</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Trihexyphenidyl</span>**

**Mild Disease, <span class="mark">Older Than 60</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Amantadine</span>**

**<span class="mark">Severe</span> Disease Regardless of Age**

> **<span class="mark">Levodopa</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Carbidopa</span>**

**Complication of Carbidopa/Levodopa**

> **On-off phenomenon**

**Parkinson Plus Pattern**

> **Parkinson disease + ataxia + orthostatic hypotension** = **<span class="mark"><u>Shy-Drager syndrome</u></span>**

**Underlying Issue Mentioned in This Teaching**

> Problem with the **carotid sinus**

**Antipsychotic-Induced Parkinson-Like Symptoms**

> Due to **dopamine inhibition**

**Term Used in This Session**

> **akinesia**

**Management in This Session**

> **<span class="mark">Lower the dose</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Add diphenhydramine</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Add benztropine</span>**
>
> Usually **do not need to change the drug entirely**

**Tremor Type**

> **Resting tremor**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Parkinson tremor = at rest**
>
> **Essential tremor = with action**
>
> **Intention tremor = worsens as target is approached**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 14%" />
<col style="width: 51%" />

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Acute<br />

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Sudden, sustained contraction of the <strong>neck, mouth, tongue &amp; eye</strong> muscles</p>
<p>脖子歪向一边, 舌头伸出, 说话困难, 眼睛向上翻</p>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>

</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Val<strong>benazine (VMAT inhibitor)</strong></p>
<p>Deutetrabenazine</p>
</blockquote></td>

</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Idiopathic Parkinson disease</u>**: loss of dopaminergic neurons in the substantia nigra

**<u>drug-induced parkinsonism</u>**: dopamine receptor blockade where the neurons project into the striatum.

**antipsychotics (eg, haloperidol, risperidone)**

**antiemetics (eg, metoclopramide, prochlorperazine)**

**TREMORS**

**<u>BENIGN ESSENTIAL TREMOR</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Worse with action**
>
> Worse under **physical stress**
>
> Worse under **mental stress**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Beta blockers</span>**

**Classic Clue**

> Tremor worsens while **trying to pour coffee into a cup**

</blockquote></td>

<p><strong>Improves with alcohol</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
