**<u>Cerebellar Tremor / Intention Tremor</u>**

**Presentation**

> Tremor worsens when reaching for something意向性震颤，越接近目标越抖

**Causes Mentioned**

> **<span class="mark">Myasthenia gravis</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Multiple sclerosis</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Stroke</span>**

**Classic Clue**

> Tremor worsens when **reaching for the coffee pot**

**<u>Functional tremor</u>震颤表现与已知神经疾病模式不一致，并且会受注意力/分散影响而改变**

**1. Distractibility分散注意时减轻或消失**

**2. Variability频率、幅度、部位、出现时机变化大**

**3. Inconsistency和已知器质性震颤模式不一致**

**4. Abrupt onset / abrupt remission突然开始、突然停止**

| **类型** | **什么时候最明显** | **典型特点** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Functional tremor** | 可静止可动作，不固定 | 突然起病, 分散注意后减轻/消失，表现不一致 |
| **Essential tremor** | 姿势/动作时 | 双手，逐渐起病，可家族性，饮酒可缓解 |
| **Parkinson tremor** | 静止时 | 搓丸样 tremor，运动迟缓、肌强直 |
| **Cerebellar tremor** | 接近目标时 | intention tremor，伴共济失调 |
| **Physiologic tremor** | 轻微动作/紧张时 | 高频低振幅，咖啡因焦虑甲亢加重 |

**<u>RESTLESS LEG SYNDROME</u>**

dopamine dysfunction + iron deficiency🡪感觉-运动障碍，病人会有：

> 腿里不舒服
>
> 发痒、爬行感、酸胀、拉扯感
>
> 强烈想动腿

**<span class="mark">at rest worse + night worse + movement relieves</span>**

**Presentation**

> **Urge to move the legs**
>
> Usually at **night**

**Most Common Cause / Risk Factor Mentioned**

> **Iron deficiency (月经过多女性，孕妇，透析/CKD，反复献血后腿不舒服)**

**Other Risk Factors**

> **Diabetes**
>
> **Pregnancy**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">轻中度先查铁、补铁，避免诱因</span>**
>
> **Mild：<span class="mark">Dopamine agonists (carbidopa-levodopa)</span>**
>
> **Frequent: <span class="mark">Gabapentin, pregabalin</span>**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Restless legs + nighttime symptoms + iron deficiency association**

<p><strong>Multiple sclerosis, Parkinson disease</strong></p>

<p><strong>Limit caffeine &amp; alcohol</strong></p>
<p><strong>Regular, moderate exercise</strong></p>
<p><strong>Warm &amp;/or cold soaks or compresses</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Medications</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Supplemental iron</mark></strong> (if <strong>serum ferritin ≤75</strong> ng/mL)</p>
<p><strong>Mild</strong> intermittent symptoms: <strong><mark>carbidopa-levodopa</mark></strong> as needed</p>
<p><strong>Frequent/daily</strong> symptoms: <strong>α2δ calcium channel ligand</strong> (eg, <strong><mark>gabapentin, pregabalin</mark></strong>)</p>
<p>Dopamine agonists (eg, pramipexole, ropinirole) not preferred</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>HUNTINGTON DISEASE</u>**

中年起病、**AD**、**CAG** 重复扩增、**<span class="mark">caudate+putamen 萎缩🡪GABA↓</span>🡪chorea,早期dopamin↑🡪tetrabenazine, Achi↓🡪dementia**、舞蹈样动作合并精神症状和痴呆，就是 Huntington disease；考题最爱加 anticipation 和家族史

**Classic Age Group**

> Age **40 to 50**

**Presentation**

> **Chorea**
>
> **Dementia** （cognitive decline, personality change, depression）
>
> **Psychosis**

**Inheritance**

> **<span class="mark">Autosomal dominant，HTT gene CAG repeat expansion</span>**

**Diagnosis**

> **<span class="mark">Genetic Concept</span>**
>
> Anticipation
>
> **Imaging🡪<span class="mark">CT/MRI</span>**
>
> **Atrophy of the <span class="mark">caudate and putamen</span>**

**Management**

> **<span class="mark">Tetrabenazine</span> for movements** （**VMAT2 inhibitor**，可减少多巴胺相关活动，从而减轻 chorea；可能增加**抑郁和自杀意念**风险）
>
> **<span class="mark">Antipsychotics</span>**
>
> **Genetic counseling**

**Disease Course**

> **Progressive**
>
> **Terminal**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> Huntington = chorea + psychiatric disease + dementia + AD inheritance + anticipation

Huntington ：GABA↓，dopamine↑，Ach相对↓

> hyperkinetic 运动过多
>
> chorea 为主

Parkinson ：dopamine↓，Ach相对↑

> hypokinetic 运动过少
>
> tremor/rigidity/bradykinesia 为主

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 17%" />
<col style="width: 82%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Huntington disease</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Motor</strong>: chorea, delayed saccade</p>
<p><strong>Psychiatric</strong>: depression, irritability, psychosis, obsessive-compulsive symptoms</p>
<p><strong>Cognitive</strong>: executive dysfunction</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Findings</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Genetic</strong>: autosomal dominant <strong>CAG trinucleotide repeat</strong> expansion disorder</p>
<p><strong>Neuropathology</strong>: <strong>loss of GABA-ergic neurons</strong></p>
<p><strong>Imaging</strong>: <strong>caudate nucleus &amp; putamen atrophy</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Management &amp; prognosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Treatment: <strong><mark>supportive</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Survival: 10-20 years</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>MYASTHENIA GRAVIS</u>**

**MG 是 postsynaptic AChR 自身免疫病，表现为越用越差的疲劳性无力，最常累及眼肌和球部肌**

**Presentation**

> Usually age **20 to 30**
>
> **Weakness that worsens with repeated movement越用越没力**
>
> **<span class="mark">Diplopia, ptosis</span>** may develop

**<span class="mark">Best Initial</span> Test**

> **<span class="mark">Antibody testing</span>**
>
> Antibodies against **<span class="mark">post</span>synaptic <span class="mark">acetylcholine receptors</span>**

**<span class="mark">Most Accurate</span> Test**

> **<span class="mark">Electromyogram🡪</span>Decreased amplitude with repeated use**

**Why <span class="mark">Chest CT</span> Is Performed**

> **To evaluate for <span class="mark">thymoma</span>**

**<span class="mark">Most Urgent</span> Step**

> **<span class="mark">Pulmonary function testing</span>**

如果累及吞咽肌、构音肌、呼吸肌/膈肌，就会变成myasthenic crisis

**If Pulmonary Function Is Involved🡪<span class="mark"><u>myasthenic crisis</u></span>快速免疫治疗+气道/呼吸支持**

> **<span class="mark">IVIG</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Plasmapheresis</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Ventilator support</span> after reducing antibody burden**

**Important Teaching Pearl**

> **Reduce antibody burden before just ventilating**
>
> **Moving the diaphragm without addressing the antibodies can worsen the situation**

**If Diaphragm Is Not Involved**

> **<span class="mark">Pyridostigmine</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Neostigmine</span>**

**After Stabilization**

> **<span class="mark">Treat associated thymoma</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Under 60🡪take it out</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Over 60🡪give prednisone, keep it under control</span>**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Myasthenia = worse with use**
>
> **Lambert-Eaton = better with use**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 14%" />
<col style="width: 85%" />

</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Treatment</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>AChE inhibitors (eg, pyridostigmine) ± immunotherapy (eg, corticosteroids, azathioprine)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Thymectomy</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>AChE = acetylcholinesterase; <strong>AChR-Ab = acetylcholine receptor antibodies</strong>; BBs = beta blockers; MgSO<sub>4</sub> = magnesium sulfate.</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table style="width:55%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 55%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: left;">Medications to avoid in myasthenia gravis</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Magnesium sulfate</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Fluoroquinolones, aminoglycosides</strong></p>
<p><strong>Neuromuscular blocking agents</strong></p>
<p>CNS depressants</p>
<p>Muscle relaxants</p>
<p><strong>Calcium channel blockers</strong></p>
<p><strong>Beta blockers</strong></p>
<p><strong>Opioids</strong></p>
<p><strong>Statins</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<span class="mark">硫酸镁</span>**是一种钙离子通道阻滞剂，会抑制突触前膜乙酰胆碱的释放 。需要**预防子痫**发作时用**<span class="mark">Valproic acid</span>**替代

**重症肌无力 (MG) 患者禁用的产科相关药物**

| **药物类别** | **具体药物** | **潜在风险** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **子痫预防** | **硫酸镁 (Magnesium sulfate)** | **诱发重症肌无力危象** |
| **抗生素** | **氨基糖苷类（庆大霉素）、氟喹诺酮类（环丙沙星）** | **加重骨骼肌无力** |
| **降压药** | **beta-受体阻滞剂、钙通道阻滞剂 (CCB)** | **干扰神经肌肉传导** |
| **麻醉辅助** | **神经肌肉阻滞剂（琥珀胆碱等）** | **导致长时间呼吸麻痹** |

**新生儿影响： 患有 MG 的母亲，其抗体可通过胎盘导致新生儿一过性重症肌无力。考试中若看到新生儿出生后哭声细弱、吸吮无力，要考虑此诊断。**

**<u>LAMBERT-EATON MYASTHENIC SYNDROME</u>**

**LEMS 是 presynaptic 钙通道抗体病，表现为越用越好、近端无力并常伴小细胞肺癌**

**Presentation**

> Usually age **35 to 45**
>
> **Muscle weakness that improves with use**
>
> **Feels better throughout the day**
>
> **<span class="mark">dry mouth、ED 等自主神经症状</span>**

**Strong Association**

> **<span class="mark">Small cell lung cancer</span>**

**Antibody**

> **Antibodies against <span class="mark">pre</span>synaptic <span class="mark">calcium channels</span>**

**Most accurate test**

**<span class="mark">EMG</span>-the more stimulate, the higher the amplitude**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Treat underlying cause</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Treat the small cell lung cancer</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Pyridostigmine</span>**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Proximal weakness that improves with use + malignancy association = Lambert-Eaton**

**<u>DEMENTIA</u>**

**Dementia Workup**

Before diagnosing dementia, **<span class="mark">rule out</span>**:可逆原因

> **TSH/T4 abnormality**
>
> **B12 deficiency**
>
> **B3 deficiency** (pellagra: diarrhea, dementia, dermatitis忘皮泻)
>
> **Syphilis**
>
> **Structural process with <span class="mark"><u>head CT</u></span>**

<table style="width:100%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 12%" />
<col style="width: 87%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p>I<u>nitial workup of <strong>suspected cognitive impairment</strong></u></p>
<p>before a definitive AD dx is made, all patients should undergo a <strong>workup</strong> for <mark>potentially <strong>reversible causes</strong></mark> of cognitive impairment.</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Cognitive<br />
testing</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>MMSE (score &lt;24/30 suggestive of MCI/dementia)</p>
<p>Montreal Cognitive Assessment (score &lt;26/30)</p>
<p>Mini-Cog (abnormal 3-word recall &amp;/or clock-drawing test)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Laboratory<br />
testing</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Routine</strong>: <strong><mark>CBC, vitamin B<sub>12</sub>, TSH, complete metabolic panel</mark></strong></p>
<p>Selective (<strong>specific risk factors</strong>): <strong>folate, syphilis, vitamin D level</strong></p>
<p>Atypical (<strong>early onset</strong>): <strong>CSF</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Imaging</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Routine</strong>: <mark><strong>CT scan</strong> or <strong>MRI</strong></mark> of the brain</p>
<p><strong>Atypical: EEG</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">CBC = complete blood count; CMP = complete metabolic panel; CSF = cerebrospinal fluid; EEG = electroencephalogram; MCI = mild cognitive impairment; MMSE = Mini-Mental State Examination.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"></td>

**<u>Alzheimer Disease</u>**

**Neurotransmitter**

> **<span class="mark">Acetylcholine low</span>**

**Presentation**

> **Slow progressive** forgetfulness

**CT Finding**

> **Diffuse atrophy**

**Treatment**

> **First-line** in this session = **<span class="mark">Donepezil</span>**
>
> **More advanced** dementia = **<span class="mark">Memantine</span>**

<img src="images/media/image28.png" style="width:4.97566in;height:1.26575in" />

**Vitamin / Supplement Mentioned都不是标准预防方法**

> **Vitamin E**
>
> **Ginkgo**

**Monitoring With Ginkgo**

> **Bleeding time**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> Progressive memory loss + diffuse atrophy + cholinergic deficit = Alzheimer disease

有 Alzheimer 家族史的患者，最重要的干预不是补 充剂或基因检测，而是**积极控制中年期可改变危险因素，如高血压、糖尿病、肥胖和缺乏运动。**

**<u>Vascular Dementia/</u>Multi-infarct dementia**

**Presentation**

> **Stepwise decline**
>
> **可伴局灶性神经体征**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Treat vascular risk factors</span>** such as:

**diabetes**

**hypertension**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> Stepwise decline strongly suggests vascular dementia

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 17%" />
<col style="width: 82%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Vascular dementia</strong></p>
<p><strong>卒中后数月内出现快速认知下降、执行功能障碍和人格/行为改变🡪 strategic infarct, ACA🡪额叶🡪执行功能</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Pathophysiology</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p>Ischemia and/or infarcts due to:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Large-vessel atherosclerosis</p>
<p>Small-vessel disease (eg, arteriolosclerosis)</p>
<p>Cerebral amyloid angiopathy</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical<br />
manifestations</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Early, <strong>prominent executive dysfunction</strong></p>
<p>Subtypes:</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Multi-infarct</strong>: often with <strong>stepwise decline</strong></p>
<p><strong>Strategic infarct</strong>: associated with <strong>localizing cortical deficits (frontal lobe, thalamus)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Subcortical vascular encephalopathy</strong>: associated with <strong>subcortical signs (eg, urinary incontinence, gait disturbances)</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Imaging<br />
findings</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Cortical infarcts</p>
<p>Subcortical lacunar infarcts</p>
<p><strong>White matter hyperintensities</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Treatment</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Risk factor modification</strong> (eg, hypertension, diabetes)</p>
<p><strong>± Antiplatelet therapy</strong></p>
<p><strong>Cholinesterase inhibitor/Achi (Donepezil, Rivastigmine, Galantamine)症状治疗，改善认知</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Frontotemporal Dementia / Pick Disease</u>**

**中年人，记忆还行，但突然变“没礼貌、没分寸、乱吃、性格大变**

**Presentation**

> **Memory loss**
>
> **Personality changes first**
>
> **Rapid mood swings**
>
> **可有 primary progressive aphasia**

**Imaging**

> **<span class="mark">CT</span>** can be used
>
> **<span class="mark">MRI</span>** is better for **frontal and temporal atrophy**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Same as Alzheimer disease</span>**
>
> **Donepezil/memantine**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **<span class="mark">Early personality and behavioral change</span>** points toward frontotemporal dementia

**<u>Creutzfeldt-Jakob Disease</u>**

**Disease Type**

> **Prion disease**

**Presentation**

> **Rapid neuro decline**
>
> **<span class="mark">Jerky movements (myoclonus)</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Seizures</span>**
>
> **Dementia**

**Imaging Mentioned in This Session**

> **<span class="mark">CT</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">MRI</span>**

**Increased signal intensity in putamen and the head of the caudate**

**<span class="mark">LP</span> Finding—most accurate**

> **<span class="mark">14-3-3 protein</span>**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Supportive care</span>**
>
> **Seizure management**

**<span class="mark">Clonazepam</span> （benzo）**

**<span class="mark">Valproic acid</span>**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Rapid dementia + myoclonus-like jerky movements** = think CJD

**CJD**

> **<span class="mark">Prion</span>** disease
>
> Rapidly progressive dementia
>
> Myoclonus
>
> EEG periodic sharp waves

**PML**

> **<span class="mark">JC virus</span>** in **HIV/immunocompromised patients**
>
> Progressive multifocal **white matter demyelination**
>
> Focal neurologic deficits
>
> MRI white matter lesions

**<u>Lewy Body Dementia</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Memory loss 认知症状在 parkinsonism 出现的同年或 1 年内就会出现**
>
> **Falls**
>
> **<span class="mark">Visual hallucinations</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Parkinsonism</span>**
>
> **REM sleep behavior disorder**

**Treatment in This Session**

> **<span class="mark">Donepezil</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Carbidopa-levodopa</span>**
>
> **~~Haloperidol~~**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> Hallucinations plus parkinsonian features support Lewy body dementia

**<u>HEADACHES</u>**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 84%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Characteristics of chronic headache</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Headache subtype</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: center;"><strong>Clinical presentation</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Migraine</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Female predominance</strong></p>
<p><strong>Unilateral, throbbing</strong></p>
<p><strong>Nausea/vomiting, photophobia</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Tension-type</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Gradual onset, bilateral pressure</strong></p>
<p><strong>Mild to moderate without pericranial muscle tenderness</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Cluster</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Male predominance</strong></p>
<p><strong>Unilateral, trigeminal distribution with ipsilateral autonomic symptoms</strong></p>
<p><strong>Duration 15 min to 3 hr, circadian periodicity</strong></p>
<p><strong>Improves with <mark>oxygen therapy</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Medication overuse</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Develops or worsens with daily medication use</strong></p>
<p><strong>Similar pattern to chronic migraine or tension-type headache</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>medication-overuse headache (MOH)</u>**

**near-daily headache** **≥3 months** in the setting of **regular use of acute headache medications** (eg, acetaminophen, opioids, butalbital).

preexisting headache disorder (eg, migraine, tension headache)

slow development, more **constant**, often daily headaches

symptoms can mimic prior headaches, or develop an entirely new headache pattern

Analgesics provide relief for only short periods

Because analgesics wear off during the night while patients are sleeping, MOH is often present on awakening晚上没补止痛药，药效退了，**早晨反跳性头痛**

Management

**<span class="mark">cessation analgesic</span>**🡪may cause transiently ↑headaches

**<span class="mark">initiation (or escalation) of preventive therapy</span>**

**<u>MIGRAINE</u>**

**偏头痛主要是 trigeminovascular system activation（三叉神经-血管系统激活），伴随神经炎症和痛觉传导异常，相关的恶心和呕吐与脑干和中枢头痛网络参与有关**

**Presentation**

> Usually **unilateral, throbbing单侧、搏动样头痛**
>
> **Nausea**
>
> **Vomiting**
>
> **畏光、畏声**

**常见先兆<span class="mark">aura</span>类型**

**visual aura**：闪光、锯齿、视野缺损

**sensory aura**：麻木、刺痛

**language aura**：说话困难

**Why Nausea/Vomiting Occur in This Teaching**

> **Vasodilation activates the CTZ**

**Proportion Described as Vasodilatory**

> About 90%

**Vasoconstrictive Migraine Subtype Mentioned**

> **<span class="mark">Tingling in the finger</span>s—preceding aura**

**Acute ER Abortive If No Cardiovascular Disease**

> **<span class="mark">Sumatriptan</span>**

**Acute DNTa**

**Dihydroergotamine**

**NSAIDs**

**Triptan**

**Antiemetics (prochlorperazine, metoclopramide)**

**Why Sumatriptan Is <span class="mark">Avoided in Cardiovascular Disease</span>**

> **Vasoconstriction** can **worsen cardiac disease**

**Alternative Mentioned in This Session**

> A non-coronary-affecting alternative was taught as **<span class="mark">ergotamine</span>**

**When to <span class="mark">Start Prophylaxis</span>发作频繁、致残、急性药效果差或不能用时考虑预防治疗**

> **≥4 episodes per month**

<u>**preventive**</u> medication should be considered in patients who:

> have frequent (eg, **<span class="mark">\>4/month) or long-lasting (eg, \>12 hr)</span>** episodes.
>
> experience **disabling symptoms** that prevent regular activities.
>
> are unable to take or have had **limited relief with abortive medications.**
>
> **overuse abortive medications** (eg, NSAIDs).

**Prophylaxis Options**

> **<span class="mark">Beta blockers</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">topiramate</span>**
>
> **Valproic acid**
>
> **TCAs (amitriptyline)**
>
> **Botox**

<table style="width:97%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 81%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">Migraine therapies</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Abortives</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Simple analgesics (eg, <strong>NSAIDs, acetaminophen)</strong></p>
<p>Antiemetics (eg, <strong>metoclopramide, prochlorperazine</strong>)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Triptans (eg, sumatriptan)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Ergotamine, dihydroergotamine</mark></strong>—for coronary artery disease</p>
<p>CGRP receptor antagonists (eg, rimegepant)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Preventives</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Antiepileptics</strong> (eg, <strong><mark>topiramate,</mark></strong> divalproex sodium)</p>
<p><strong>Tricyclic antidepressants</strong> (eg, amitriptyline)</p>
<p><strong><mark>β Blockers</mark></strong> (eg, propranolol)</p>
<p>CGRP monoclonal antibodies (eg, erenumab)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">CGRP = calcitonin gene-related peptide; NSAIDs = nonsteroidal anti-inflammatory drugs.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**migraine with aura + combined OCP🡪<span class="mark">change contraceptive method</span>**

migraine with aura 本身就和 ischemic stroke risk 增加有关；\
如果再加上 estrogen-containing contraceptives，卒中风险会进一步增加。AHA/ASA 卒中预防指南指出，偏头痛，尤其是有先兆者，是女性卒中的危险因素，而使用含雌激素口服避孕药会增加卒中风险。

所以管理上最优先的是：

> 停用/更换含雌激素避孕方式
>
> 改为 non-estrogen 方案，比如 IUD 或 progestin-only methods。CDC 美国避孕适用标准把 **<span class="mark">migraine with aura 归为combined hormonal contraceptives 的禁忌</span>**（Category 4）

**<u>CLUSTER HEADACHE</u>**

单侧眶周/颞部剧痛, 持续**时间短但重suicide headache**, **autonomic symptoms**流泪、流鼻涕、结膜充血、鼻塞, 病人常**坐立不安**

**Presentation似allergy**

> **Lacrimation, miosis (autonomic symptoms)**
>
> **Rhinorrhea**
>
> Often at **<span class="mark">night, last 90 min</span>**
>
> **Worse when they lay down**

**Abortive Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">100% oxygen</span>**
>
> May add a **<span class="mark">triptan</span>**

**Prophylaxis**

**<span class="mark">verapamil</span>**

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Cluster headaches are <span class="mark">short, severe, and autonomic</span>**

**<u>Tension Headache</u>**

非搏动、双侧、压迫样、与压力(压力、睡眠差、情绪紧张)相关, 无明显恶心呕吐, 日常活动一般不明显加重

**Presentation**

> **Band-like headache**
>
> **Often stress related**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">NSAIDs</span>**

**For Frequent Tension Headaches**

> **<span class="mark">Amitriptyline</span>** may sometimes be used

**<u>Amitriptyline</u>**

inhibiting the reuptake of norepinephrine and serotonin

副作用：interaction with other receptors: anti-HAM

> **Histamine receptors🡪<span class="mark">sedation/lethargy</span>**
>
> **Alpha-adrenergic receptors🡪<span class="mark">orthostatic hypotension</span>**
>
> **Muscarinic receptors🡪anticholinergic symptoms (dry mouth, constipation, urinary retention)**

**<u>Pseudotumor Cerebri</u>**

**Definition**

> **Excess CSF** 🡪 **↑ICP without a mass lesion**

**Vitamin A Association**

> Can be associated with **<span class="mark">vitamin A excess or derivatives</span>**
>
> Does not have to be

**Herniation Risk**

> **No**

**CT Finding**

> **Normal CT**

**LP Finding**

> **Increased opening pressure**

**Why Headache Occurs**

> Too much fluid with nowhere for it to go because the brain is not atrophying

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Acetazolamide</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Therapeutic lumbar puncture</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Remove offending drugs</span>** if possible

**Medication Contributors Mentioned**

> Some **chemotherapy drugs** because of vitamin A derivatives

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **Increased ICP symptoms with normal imaging and high opening pressure** = pseudotumor cerebri

**INTRACRANIAL HEMORRHAGES**

**<u>Epidural Hematoma</u>**

Presentation

> **Trauma to the side of the head**
>
> **Lucid interval (minutes)**

Vessel

> **Middle meningeal <span class="mark">artery</span>🡪急症**

Diagnosis

> **<span class="mark">CT without contrast</span>**

Treatment

> **<span class="mark">Surgery</span>**

Step 2 Pearl

> Epidural = **<span class="mark">arterial bleed + lucid interval</span>**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 12%" />
<col style="width: 87%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Epidural hematoma</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Pathogenesis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">Trauma to sphenoid bone with tearing of <strong>middle meningeal artery</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical features</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Brief loss of consciousness</strong> followed by <strong>lucid interval</strong></p>
<p>Hematoma expansion leads to:</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>↑ Intracranial pressure</strong> (impaired consciousness, headache, nausea/vomiting)</p>
<p><strong>Uncal herniation</strong> (CNIII🡪ipsilateral pupillary dilation &amp; contralateral hemiparesis)</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Diagnosis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>CT scan</strong> of the head: <strong>biconvex (lens-shaped)</strong> hyperdensity that does <strong>not cross suture lines</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Treatment</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Urgent surgical evacuation</mark></strong> for symptomatic patients</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Subdural Hematoma</u>**

Classic Presentation

> Often **<span class="mark">older patient after a fall</span>**
>
> **Lucid interval** may appear **<span class="mark">2 to 3 weeks later</span>**
>
> **Focal neurologic deficits**

Vessel

**Bridging veins/subdural <span class="mark">veins</span>**

Other Causes Mentioned

> **Head trauma in young adults**
>
> **Football head injury**
>
> **Repetitive head movement**
>
> **Roller coaster type injury**
>
> **<span class="mark">Shaken baby</span> mechanism🡪seizures, ↑head circumference, bulging/tense anterior fontanelle, papilleadema, AMS**

Diagnosis

> **<span class="mark">CT without contrast</span>**

**If Midline Shift Is Present**

> **<span class="mark">Surgery</span>**

**If No Midline Shift**

> **<span class="mark">Hyperventilation</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Mannitol</span>**

Step 2 Pearl

> **Subdural can present later and may be more delayed than epidural**

<table style="width:97%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 82%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Subdural hematoma</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Pathogenesis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Rupture of <strong><mark>bridging veins</mark></strong> (head trauma)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Risk factors</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Elderly</strong> &amp; <strong>alcohol use disorder</strong> (cerebral atrophy, ↑ fall risk)</p>
<p><strong>Infants</strong> (thin-walled vessels)</p>
<p><strong>Anticoagulant use</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical features</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Acute</mark></strong>: <strong>gradual onset 1-2 days</strong> after injury</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Impaired consciousness (eg, coma), confusion</strong></p>
<p><strong>Headache, nausea &amp; vomiting</strong> (<strong>↑ intracranial pressure</strong>)</p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Chronic</mark></strong>: <strong>insidious onset weeks</strong> after injury</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Headache, somnolence, confusion, light-headedness</strong></p>
<p><strong>Focal neurologic deficits</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Diagnosis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>CT scan</mark></strong> of the head: <strong>crescent-shaped hyperdensity (acute)</strong> or <strong>hypodensity (chronic)</strong> <strong>crossing suture lines</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Treatment</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Reverse/discontinue anticoagulants</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Surgical evacuation of symptomatic or large bleeds</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

| 特征       | **Epidural hematoma**   | **Subdural hematoma**      |
|:-----------|:------------------------|:---------------------------|
| 出血来源   | middle meningeal artery | bridging veins             |
| 进展       | 快                      | 较慢                       |
| 典型病史   | lucid interval          | 渐进性 headache/confusion  |
| CT         | biconvex/lens-shaped    | crescent-shaped            |
| 是否跨缝线 | **不跨**                | 可跨缝线                   |
| 常见人群   | **头外伤，年轻人/儿童** | **老年人、婴儿、酒精依赖** |

**<u>Subarachnoid Hemorrhage</u>**

Classic Presentation

> **Worst headache of life**

Additional Vignette Clue Emphasized

> **Younger patient** presenting to the ER in the **middle of the night** with a **severe headache**

**Most Common** Vessel Overall

> **Anterior communicating artery**

Aneurysm Location Associated With **<span class="mark">Polycystic Kidney Disease</span>**

> **Posterior communicating artery**

**Initial Test**

> **<span class="mark">Non-contrast CT</span>**

Important **Early Pearl**

> **<span class="mark">CT may be normal early</span>**

If **CT Is Normal** but Suspicion Remains High

> **<span class="mark">Lumbar puncture</span>**

LP Finding

> **<span class="mark">Xanthochromia</span>**

If Blood Is Seen Only in the First Tube

> Suggests **<span class="mark">traumatic tap</span>**

如果腰穿（LP）时只有第1管脑脊液里见到血，而后面几管越来越清或没有血，提示是 traumatic tap（穿刺时碰到血管）

**Most Accurate** **Test After Confirmation** in This Teaching

> **<span class="mark">MRA or angiographer to check which vessel</span>**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Surgical clipping</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Calcium channel blocker</span> to prevent vasospasm and stroke**
>
> **<span class="mark">Magnesium sulfate</span> for seizure prophylaxis**

Step 2 Pearl

> For suspected SAH:

**CT first**

**LP if CT is negative and suspicion remains high**

**57岁男性 + sudden onset severe occipital headache：<span class="mark">这种Thunderclap headache，在排除其他原因前，必须默认是 SAH</span>**。**血压 180/98 mmHg + 轻度嗜睡：** 提示可能存在颅内压增高。

**SAH 的诊断与管理流程**

| 步骤 | 行动 | 说明 |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 第一步 | **<span class="mark">Noncontrast CT</span>** | 首选，速度快，急性期极其敏感。 |
| 第二步 (若CT阴性) | **<span class="mark">腰椎穿刺 (LP)</span>** | 寻找黄变或持续高红细胞计数。 |
| 确认解剖原因 | **<span class="mark">CTA 或 DSA (造影)</span>** | 确定动脉瘤的位置（用于手术或介入准备）。 |
| 预防并发症 | **<span class="mark">尼莫地平 (Nimodipine)</span>** | 预防出血后 3-10 天发生的脑血管痉挛。 |

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 19%" />
<col style="width: 80%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Overview of subarachnoid hemorrhage</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Ruptured arterial <strong>saccular (berry) aneurysm</strong> (most common)</p>
<p><strong>Severe headache</strong> at onset of neurologic symptoms</p>
<p><strong>Meningeal irritation (eg, neck stiffness)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Focal deficits</strong> can be present</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Complications</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Rebleeding (first 24 hr)</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Delayed cerebral ischemia</strong> due to <strong><mark>vasospasm (after 3 days)🡪stroke-like symptoms</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Obstructive hydrocephalus/increased ICP</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Seizures</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Hyponatremia</mark> (usually from SIADH)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Noncontrast CT</mark> scan of the head initially</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Lumbar puncture</mark> required to definitively rule out SAH if CT scan is negative</strong></p>
<p><strong>Xanthochromia in CSF confirms diagnosis</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Cerebral angiography</mark> to identify bleeding source</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Angiographic procedure</mark> to stabilize aneurysm</strong> (<strong>coiling or clipping</strong>)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Nimodipine &amp; euvolemia</mark></strong> to reduce <strong>delayed cerebral ischemia</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>CSF</strong> = cerebrospinal fluid; <strong>ICP</strong> = intracranial pressure; <strong>SAH</strong> = subarachnoid hemorrhage; <strong>SIADH</strong> = syndrome of inappropriate antidiuretic hormone secretion.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

| **SAH并发症** | **时间** | **典型表现** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Rebleeding** | **前24小时最常见** | 突然再次剧烈恶化、意识下降 |
| **Cerebral vasospasm** | **3–14天** | 新发局灶性神经缺损、stroke-like symptoms |
| **Hydrocephalus** | 可早可晚 | 头痛、嗜睡、意识改变、ICP增高 |
| **Seizure** | 可发生 | 抽搐、发作后意识障碍 |
| **Hyponatremia/SIADH** | 住院期可见 | confusion, lethargy |

**<span class="mark">Cocaine use</span>🡪 intracranial hemorrhage** (ICH):

> **Young age**:  Most patients who sustain stroke are age \>60.
>
> **Absence** of typical risk factors (**chronic hypertension)**
>
> **<span class="mark">Sympathetic activation</span>**:

acute hypertension

tachycardia

**mydriasis** (normal **2-4mm**)

**hyperthermia** (cocaine-induced vasoconstriction preventing heat dissipation)

> **Location**: **subcortical** locations (eg, **thalamus**)🡪**intraventricular hemorrhage**

**VERTIGO**

**Vertigo With Hearing Loss**

> Labyrinthitis
>
> Meniere disease

**Meniere Disease Treatment**

> Dietary sodium modification
>
> Meclizine
>
> Surgery if needed

**Vertigo Without Hearing Loss**

> Benign positional vertigo
>
> Vestibular neuritis

**Benign Positional Vertigo**

> Diagnosis = Dix-Hallpike maneuver
>
> Treatment = Epley maneuver

Step 2 Pearl

> Hearing loss helps separate peripheral vertigo etiologies

**<u>ALS</u>**

<img src="images/media/image29.png" style="width:6.75276in;height:1.25155in" />

Presentation

> Usually around the **40s**
>
> Weakness
>
> **Upper motor neuron** findings
>
> **Lower motor neuron** findings
>
> No sensory loss
>
> **tongue fasciculations** due to the denervation of cranial nerve XII
>
> **dysarthria, facial weakness, dysphagia, inappropriate and persistent laughing, crying or yawning**
>
> **hypersecretion** 🡪 mucus build up in the pharynx (halitosis) and lungs -\> inability to manage secretions and loss of gag reflux - **aspiration pneumonia** (MCC of death with ALS)

**Most Urgent** Step

> **<span class="mark">Pulmonary function tests</span>**

**Best Initial** Diagnostic Test

> **<span class="mark">EMG</span>**

**If Pulmonary Function Is Not Yet Affected**

> **<span class="mark">Riluzole</span> (Glutamate antagonist)**

**If Pulmonary Function Is Affected**

> **<span class="mark">Intubation / ventilatory support</span>**

Step 2 Pearl

> **<span class="mark">Mixed UMN and LMN signs without sensory loss = ALS</span>**

**<u>MULTIPLE SCLEROSIS</u>**

**<span class="mark">Autoimmune🡪demyelination of CNS (brain, spinal cord)</span>**

年轻患者出现相隔时间和空间的中枢神经缺损，伴UMN体征，要考虑MS；CSF最典型为 oligoclonal IgG bands

年轻成人，尤其女性，出现反复发作、可部分恢复的神经系统症状，比如：

> **视力模糊、眼痛、颜色变淡，提示 <span class="mark">optic neuritis</span>**
>
> **一侧肢体无力、麻木**
>
> **共济失调、步态不稳**
>
> **尿急、尿潴留或痉挛**
>
> **热天** (move from Oregon to Arizona)、发烧、洗热水澡后症状短暂加重，提示 **<u>Uhthoff phenomenon</u>**

**Presentation**

> **Waxing and waning symptoms**
>
> **Eye complaints**
>
> <img src="images/media/image30.png" style="width:3.14097in;height:4.31597in" />**constitutional symptoms** (fatigure, poor sleep)
>
> **↑risk of <span class="mark">ischemic stroke</span>**
>
> **Symptoms separated in time**

**<span class="mark">Best Initial</span> Test**

> **<span class="mark">MRI</span>**

**If <span class="mark">MRI Is Normal</span> but Suspicion Remains**

> **<span class="mark">Lumbar puncture</span>🡪<span class="mark">Oligoclonal bands</span>** (not specific)

**Antibody Mentioned in Session**

> **<span class="mark">Anti-myelin</span>**

**<span class="mark">Acute Exacerbation</span> Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">High-dose steroids</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Or plasmapheresis</span>**

**<span class="mark">Relapsing-Remitting</span> Treatment Options**

> **<span class="mark">Interferon beta</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Glatiramer</span>**一种合成多肽混合物，类似 myelin basic protein，假装自己是髓鞘，诱导免疫系统别再打真髓鞘

**Symptom Control**

> **Daytime spasticity = <span class="mark">Baclofen</span>** GABA-B receptor agonist🡪抑制脊髓反射🡪减轻痉挛
>
> **Nighttime spasticity = <span class="mark">Tizanidine</span>** 中枢性 α2-adrenergic agonist🡪减少兴奋性神经递质释放🡪减轻痉挛
>
> **Urinary <span class="mark">retention</span> = <span class="mark">Bethanechol</span>** muscarinic agonist🡪刺激逼尿肌收缩🡪帮助排尿

**Step 2 Pearl**

> **MS requires lesions separated in time and often clinically in space**

Features concerning for **ischemia** rather than MS include:

> **deficits that localize to a classic arterial distribution**
>
> **<span class="mark">hyperacute onset (minutes)</span>**
>
> prominent **<span class="mark">cortical signs</span>** (**<span class="mark">Visual \[hemianopia, gaze preference\], Aphasia, Neglect, Sensory</span> \["<span class="mark">VANS</span>"\]**)
>
> **headache, meningeal signs, signs of increased intracranial pressure**

**<u>Acute inflammatory demyelinating polyneuropathy/GUILLAIN-BARRE SYNDROME</u>**

**Autoimmune destroy <span class="mark">schwann cell🡪demyelination</span> of motor fiber, sensory fiber, peripheral nerves (CNIII-XII)**

Presentation

> **<span class="mark">Bilateral ascending paralysis</span>**
>
> Often about **2 weeks** after an infection
>
> Patient may say they **<span class="mark">cannot walk</span> because they <span class="mark">cannot feel their feet</span>**

Infectious Triggers Mentioned

> Viral
>
> Bacterial
>
> Other infectious triggers

**Most Urgent Step**

> **<span class="mark">Pulmonary function tests</span>**

**Best Initial Test**

> **<span class="mark">Lumbar puncture</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Albuminocytologic dissociation</span>**
>
> **High protein**
>
> **No white blood cells**

**Antibody** Mentioned

> **<span class="mark">Anti-ganglioside antibody</span>**

**<span class="mark">EMG</span>** Finding

> **Diffuse demyelination**

If P**ulmonary Function Is Involved**

> **<span class="mark">Ventilator</span> first**
>
> **Then <span class="mark">IVIG</span>**
>
> **Then <span class="mark">plasmapheresis</span>**

**If Pulmonary Function Is Not Involved**

> **<span class="mark">IVIG</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Plasmapheresis</span>**

Key Management Pearl

> Some patients may need **<span class="mark">early ventilation</span>** because paralysis may reach the diaphragm before medical therapy takes effect

Step 2 Pearl

> **<span class="mark">Ascending weakness + recent infection + albuminocytologic dissociation = Guillain-Barre</span>**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 14%" />
<col style="width: 85%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Guillain-Barré syndrome急性感染后诱发的免疫介导性<mark>周围神经脱髓鞘</mark></strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>对称性进行性上行性无力</mark></strong>，<strong><mark>反射减弱/消失</mark>，感觉多正常或轻微异常，运动受累更明显</strong>，可有<strong>背痛</strong></p>
<p><strong>神经传导检查nerve conduction studies / 肌电图</strong>：可见<strong>demyelination</strong>，如神经传导速度下降</p>
<p>CSF可见蛋白高细胞正常（albuminocytologic dissociation）</p>
</blockquote></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Immune-mediated <strong>acute demyelinating polyneuropathy</strong></p>
<p>Preceding <strong>gastrointestinal (<em>Campylobacter</em>), respiratory infection, acute HIV infection</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Initial: paresthesia（tingling） of fingers and toes</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>neuropathic pain</mark> （back pain without spinal tenderness）</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Symmetric, ascending weakness</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>hyporeflexia</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Autonomic dysfunction</mark> (eg, <mark>bradycardia</mark>, arrhythmia, ileus)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Respiratory compromise</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Clinical</strong></p>
<p>Supportive findings</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Cerebrospinal fluid: ↑ protein, normal leukocytes</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Abnormal electromyography &amp; nerve conduction</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>MRI: normal or enhancement of anterior nerve roots/cauda equina</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Management</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Monitoring of autonomic &amp; respiratory function</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Intravenous immunoglobulin or plasmapheresis</mark> </strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Miller Fisher syndrome (MFS)</u>** **腹泻之后眼先花，走路不稳反射塌；MFS 三联记住它：眼麻、共济差、腱反射下**

after a gastrointestinal illness 1-2w, a variant of **Guillain-Barré syndrome (GBS)**

**<span class="mark">Anti-GQ1b</span>**—highly sensitive for MFS

**<span class="mark">ophthalmoplegia</span> 眼肌麻痹，复视，ptosis**

**cerebellar-like <span class="mark">ataxia</span>** (eg, dysmetria)**周围神经/本体感觉传导异常,以及运动协调相关通路受影响**

**<span class="mark">areflexia</span>**

**lower-extremity weakness** may occur, paralysis is less common. 

**diagnosis**

**cerebrospinal fluid: albuminocytologic dissociation **

**Management**

**<span class="mark">intravenous immunoglobulin</span>**

**<span class="mark">plasmapheresis</span>**

**经典 GBS**

> 主要是 **ascending weakness**
>
> 反射减弱/消失
>
> 可有自主神经异常
>
> 常见呼吸肌受累风险

**Miller Fisher syndrome**

> 更经典的是：

**ophthalmoplegia**

**ataxia**

**areflexia**

> 肢体瘫痪可轻，甚至不明显
>
> 和 **anti-GQ1b** 关联更强

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 19%" />
<col style="width: 80%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Chronic inflammatory demyelinating polyneuropathy</strong></p>
<p><strong>慢性进展的近端+远端无力、低反射、振动觉/本体觉下降</strong></p>
<p><strong>典型检查是<mark>周围神经</mark>传导速度下降</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Immune-mediated</strong> <strong>demyelination</strong> of <strong>peripheral nerves and nerve roots</strong></p>
<p><strong>Non–length dependent🡪近端、远端均受累</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Progression <strong>&gt;8 weeks，可反复或持续恶化</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Motor &gt;&gt; sensory</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Symmetric proximal &amp; distal muscle weakness</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>LMN signs</mark></strong> (eg, hyporeflexia, atrophy)</p>
<p><strong>Distal sensory loss</strong> can occur, 尤振动觉、本体觉受损</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>CSF: ↑ protein</strong>, normal white blood cells</p>
<p><strong><mark>NCS: decreased conduction velocity</mark></strong> (ie, demyelination)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Nerve biopsy: segmental demyelination</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Glucocorticoids</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Intravenous immunoglobulin</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Plasmapheresis</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>CSF</strong> = cerebrospinal fluid; <strong>LMN</strong> = lower motor neuron; <strong>NCS</strong> = nerve conduction studies.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>TRANSVERSE MYELITIS</u>有感觉平面 + UMN体征 + 膀胱功能障碍**

**immune-mediated disorder** characterized by the infiltration of inflammatory cells into a segment of the spinal cord.  Inflammation localizes to **≥1 contiguous spinal cord segments🡪rapidly progressive myelopathy** characterized by motor weakness, autonomic dysfunction (eg, bowel/bladder dysfunction), and sensory deficits with a **distinct sensory level.**

Clinical Clue

> **<span class="mark">Ascending paralysis</span>**
>
> **Back pain**
>
> **Chest tightness (band-like chest/abdominal tightness)**
>
> **Bowel/bladder dysfunction**

Description in This Session

> **Inflammation of the spinal cord**

Infectious Cause Mentioned

> **CMV**

Diagnosis

> **<span class="mark">MRI</span>**

LP Pearl

> **LP will not show anything useful here**

Treatment

> **<span class="mark">Steroids</span>**

Differentiation From Guillain-Barre

> Transverse myelitis has:

back pain

chest tightness

> Guillain-Barre just rises upward without that back finding

Step 2 Pearl

> **Back pain** plus **ascending deficits** should make you think spinal cord process

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 84%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Idiopathic transverse myelitis</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Immune-mediated destruction of spinal cord</strong></p>
<p>Often <strong><mark>postinfectious</mark> (molecular mimicry): gastroenteritis, upper respiratory infection</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Rapidly progressive bilateral weakness, early flaccid (LMN)🡪 late spastic (UMN)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Bilateral sensory dysfunction (all somatosensory systems), <mark>distinct sensory level</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Band-like chest/abdominal tightness</strong></p>
<p><strong>Autonomic dysfunction (<mark>bowel &amp;/or bladder</mark> dysfunction)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>MRI of spine</mark>: no compressive lesion, <mark>T2 hyperintensity</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Lumbar puncture</mark>: <mark>↑ WBCs, ↑ IgG index</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>High-dose intravenous glucocorticoids</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Plasmapheresis</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>LMN</strong> = lower motor neuron; <strong>UMN</strong> = upper motor neuron; <strong>WBCs</strong> = white blood cells.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**TM（transverse myelitis）是“脊髓病”**，\
**GBS 是“周围神经/神经根病”**。

所以鉴别重点就是看：**有没有脊髓定位体征**

 TM: **sensory level + bladder/bowel dysfunction + spinal cord findings**

 GBS: **ascending weakness + areflexia**, usually **no sensory level**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 34%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>特征</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>Transverse myelitis (TM)</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>Guillain-Barré syndrome (GBS)</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">病变部位</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>脊髓 (LMN🡪UMN)</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>周围神经/神经根 (LMN)</mark></strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">无力类型</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">双下肢常见，可逐渐上行</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>对称性上行性无力</strong>更典型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">反射</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p>早期可正常/低 <strong>(LMN)</strong></p>
<p>但很快常变成<strong>亢进 (UMN)</strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>减弱或消失</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Babinski</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>阳性</strong>（UMN）</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>阴性</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">肌张力</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">常增高（后期痉挛）</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">低张、弛缓</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">感觉异常分布</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>有明确 sensory level</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>无明确感觉平面</strong>，多为手套袜套样或远端感觉异常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">感觉受累类型</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">可同时累及<strong>痛温觉 + 振动觉/本体觉</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">感觉症状通常较轻，常见麻木/刺痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">膀胱肠道功能</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>常见</strong>，尿潴留/便秘/失禁</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">可有自主神经异常，但<strong>明确尿潴留+感觉平面更支持TM</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">背痛</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">可有</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">也可有，但通常是根性疼痛或腰背痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">脑神经受累</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">少见</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>常见</strong>，如面瘫、吞咽困难</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">呼吸肌受累</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">可有，但不如GBS经典</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>常见且重要</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">脊髓MRI</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>异常</strong>，脊髓T2高信号</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">通常无脊髓实质病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">CSF</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">可有<strong>WBC↑、IgG index↑</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">经典是<strong>蛋白高、细胞正常</strong>（albuminocytologic dissociation）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">神经传导</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">不是主要诊断依据</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>nerve conduction study</mark>🡪脱髓鞘改变</strong>很重要</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**更支持 TM 🡪有感觉平面 + UMN体征 + 膀胱功能障碍**

> <span class="mark">**sensory level（感觉平面）**</span>
>
> **hyperreflexia**
>
> **Babinski positive**
>
> **Chest tightness**
>
> **urinary retention / bowel dysfunction**
>
> MRI 显示**脊髓病变**
>
> 各种感觉都受损：痛温觉、振动觉、本体觉一起受累

**更支持 GBS 🡪上行性无力 + 反射消失**

> **ascending symmetric weakness**
>
> **areflexia / hyporeflexia**
>
> 感觉异常轻，主要是**paresthesia**
>
> 近期感染后出现
>
> 可有**面瘫、呼吸肌无力、自主神经不稳**
>
> CSF：**高蛋白、正常细胞数**
>
> **nerve conduction study**提示脱髓鞘

GBS 也可以有：

> 自主神经异常
>
> 腰背痛
>
> 感觉异常

所以不要被这些带偏。\
**真正拉开差距的，是：**

> **反射方向**：TM 常亢进，GBS 消失
>
> **是否有 sensory level**
>
> **是否有 Babinski/其他 UMN signs**

**<u>BOTULISM</u> = 把副交感和神经肌接头都“关掉”，所以更偏向干、停、瘫、压低**

Presentation

> **<span class="mark">Descending</span> paralysis**
>
> **Constipation**
>
> **Hypotonia**
>
> **Hypotension**

Treatment**高度怀疑 <span class="mark">wound botulism</span>，且已有呼吸衰竭, 立刻给予**

**<span class="mark">equine botulinum antitoxin</span>**

> **<span class="mark">Intubation</span> Respiratory support** and **wound debridement also required**

Step 2 Pearl

> Descending paralysis is a major differentiator from Guillain-Barre

**<u>infant botulism</u>：ingested spores**

**<u>foodborne botulism</u>：ingested preformed botulinum toxin**

**<u>Wound botulism</u>**

***Clostridium botulinum* spores contaminate a puncture wound** (eg, injection drug use), germinate in the anaerobic environment, and **generate botulinum toxin *in vivo***.

**clostridium botulinum** 产生的毒素会**抑制突触前膜 acetylcholine 释放**

**<span class="mark">注射毒品 + 脓肿/污染伤口 + 脑神经受累 + 对称性下降性麻痹 + 呼吸衰竭</span>**

**10 days** (rather than within hours) after transmission

**Fever, leukocytosis**

作用部位在：

> **周围胆碱能神经末梢**
>
> **神经肌接头**
>
> 也可影响**自主神经**

所以表现为：

**<span class="mark">1. 脑神经受累先出现</span>beginning with CNs**

> **CN III, CN IV, and CN VI (diplopia, ptosis, mydriasis)**
>
> **CN IX and CN X (dysphagia,** suppressed gag，**dysarthria** 构音障碍**)**

**<span class="mark">2. 对称性下降性弛缓性麻痹</span>**

> 先**头颈**
>
> 再上**肢/呼吸肌**
>
> 最后**下肢**

**<span class="mark">3. 呼吸肌麻痹</span>**Progressive respiratory compromise due to **diaphragmatic paralysis**

> **浅呼吸**
>
> hypoxemia
>
> **acute respiratory acidosis**

4\. **<span class="mark">Autonomic dysfunction</span>** (eg, **ileus, orthostatic hypotension, urinary retention**)

**SEIZURES**

General **Seizure Workup** After a seizure, do:

> **CT scan**：**排急性出血或占位；MRI 比 CT 更敏感，后续更适合看小病灶或癫痫灶**
>
> **EEG：判断是否存在癫痫样放电并帮助评估复发风险**
>
> **Electrolytes：找代谢原因**
>
> **Toxicology screen：怀疑聚会、毒品、药物相关时帮助确认诱因**

Automatically **<span class="mark">Start Treatment After a First Seizure If</span>**—**由复发风险决定**

> **Family history**
>
> **Any abnormality on seizure workup**
>
> **First seizure was status epilepticus**

**<u>Focal / Partial Seizures</u>**

放电起源于一个局部皮层区，所以症状常有“定位性”。

意识保留🡪focal aware；意识受损🡪focal impaired awareness

**First-Line** Treatment

> **<span class="mark">Carbamazepine</span>**

Applies To

> **Partial seizures**
>
> **Focal aware/simple partial seizures**
>
> **Focal impaired/complex partial seizures**

**Second-Line** Options

> **<span class="mark">Valproic acid</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Lamotrigine</span>**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 10%" />
<col style="width: 89%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Focal seizure</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Onset</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Neuronal discharge begins in 1 cerebral hemisphere</p>
<p>Symptoms may be <strong>motor, sensory, or autonomic</strong></p>
<p>Underlying structural abnormality (eg, tumor) more likely than with a generalized seizure</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Categories</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><u>No impairment of awareness</u></strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>Occurs when seizure remains l<strong>ocalized to 1 hemisphere</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong><u>Impairment of awareness</u></strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>Occurs when seizure <strong>spreads to the other hemisphere</strong></p>
<p>Often associated with <strong>automatisms (eg, chewing)</strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Postictal confusion and lethargy, transient postictal paresis or paralysis (Todd paralysis)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Diagnosis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>EEG</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Brain MRI</mark></strong> (may identify a triggering, structural lesion)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">EEG = electroencephalography.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Complex Partial / Focal Impaired Seizure</u>**

病人突然**发呆**，摸衣角、**咂嘴**、重复吞咽，1 分钟后迷糊（**意识受损**）。

Presentation

> Loss of consciousness
>
> Zoning out
>
> Lip smacking

**<u>Absence Seizure</u>**

**短暂意识中断**，通常<span class="mark">几秒到十几秒</span>，常见于儿童；发作后**<span class="mark">立刻恢复</span>**，常能接着刚才的话继续说。

经典 EEG 是 **<span class="mark">3-Hz spike-and-wave</span>**

Presentation

> Usually in a child
>
> Zoning out
>
> Returns and repeats what was said--**no postictal period**.
>
> easily **<span class="mark">provoked by hyperventilation</span>**

Treatment

> **<span class="mark">Ethosuximide</span>**

**<u>Myoclonic seizure</u>**

**Quick, repetitive jerks, no loss of consciousness**

**特发性全身性癫痫，是突然、短暂、像被电了一下的肌肉抽动，可累及单个肌群、双上肢、全身短暂抽动，病人通常意识保留。常见于<u>juvenile myoclonic epilepsy</u>，病人常描述为**

> **手突然一抖**
>
> **端东西突然掉了**
>
> **刷牙、拿杯子时猛地一弹**
>
> **早晨或睡眠不足最明显**

**a/w Creutzfeldt**

**Treatment**

> **First line**

**<span class="mark">Valproate</span>**

**<span class="mark">Levetiracetam</span>**

> **Alternative / caution**

**Lamotrigine**

**may worsen myoclonic seizures**

> **Add-on / refractory**

**<span class="mark">Clonazepam</span>**

**<u>Atonic Seizure</u>**

突然丢失肌张力，所以人像“断线木偶”一样塌下去，最怕摔伤。常见于某些广泛性癫痫综合征

孩子走着走着突然膝盖一软摔地，几秒后醒

Presentation

> Sudden loss of tone
>
> Rag-doll collapse
>
> Falls to the floor

**First-Line** Treatment

> **<span class="mark">Valproic acid</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Lamotrigine</span>**

**Second-Line** Treatment

> **<span class="mark">Carbamazepine</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Phenytoin</span>**

**<u>Tonic Seizure</u>**

突然全身或部分肌群强直收缩，所以表现成“僵住、绷住”。病人突然全身发硬、不能动，随后恢复

Presentation

> Patient freezes up

**First-Line Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Valproic acid</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Lamotrigine</span>**

**Second-Line Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Carbamazepine</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Phenytoin</span>**

**<u>Generalized tonic-clonic seizure</u>先硬后抽，postictal confusion**

双侧大脑半球广泛同步异常放电，先强直后阵挛，常伴意识丧失、跌倒、发作后困倦混乱。

病人突然倒地、全身先硬后抽，醒后迷糊 20 分钟。

**EEG: fast spike-and-wave activity at 4–5 Hz**

** 持续放电 → tonic (强直期)**

** 兴奋/抑制交替 → clonic (阵挛期)**

 **absence = 3 Hz，像“发呆，慢一点”**

 **tonic-clonic = 更猛、更快，4–5 Hz🡪每秒4–5次广泛同步异常放电**

与晕厥区分:\
**尿失禁** 可以支持 seizure，但不绝对, 任何严重 collapse 都可能出现失禁。

更有帮助的是 **发作后意识混乱、舌咬伤、明显强直-阵挛动作**

**Tonic-Clonic vs Syncope**

Distinguishing Feature in a Patient Who Lives Alone

> **Urinary incontinence** suggests **tonic-clonic seizure**

Important Session Pearl

> **Any seizure type can have some degree of incontinence**

If Unclear Whether Collapse Was Atonic Seizure or Syncope

> **EEG**
>
> **Full seizure workup**

**<span class="mark">Treat 41min</span>**

<th style="text-align: center;">Seizure</th>
<th style="text-align: center;">Vasovagal syncope</th>

<p>Physical/emotional stress</p>
<p>Heat</p>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Preceding aura (eg, olfactory hallucinations)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Can occur with sleeping/sitting</strong></p>
<p><strong>Tonic/clonic movements</strong></p>
<p><strong>Rapid, strong pulses</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Tongue biting</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Incontinence</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Preceding lightheadedness (ie, presyncope)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Unlikely to occur while sleeping/sitting</strong></p>
<p><strong>Uncommon to have clonic jerks (can occur with prolonged cerebral hypoperfusion)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Weak, slow pulses</strong></p>
<p><strong>Pallor &amp; diaphoresis</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Sequelae</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Delayed return to baseline</strong> (postictal drowsiness or confusion)</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Immediate return to baseline</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Status Epilepticus</u>**

**持续抽搐**或**反复发作而未恢复基线**，会导致持续缺氧、乳酸堆积、脑损伤，属于神经急症。现代处理强调 **不要等太久**

Treatment

> Maintain **<span class="mark">ABCs</span> （airway, oxygenation, circulation）**
>
> **<span class="mark">Lorazepam</span>**

Step 2 Pearl

> **Stabilize airway first, then benzodiazepine**

<table style="width:100%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 11%" />
<col style="width: 88%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong><u>Generalized convulsive status epilepticus</u></strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Risk factors</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Nonadherence to AEDs</p>
<p>Structural brain abnormalities (eg, brain tumor)</p>
<p>Metabolic abnormalities</p>
<p>Infection</p>
<p>Drug withdrawal</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Diagnosis</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>≥5 minutes of generalized convulsive seizure<br />
</strong>OR</p>
<p><strong>≥2 generalized convulsive seizures without interval recovery of consciousness</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Treatment</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Stabilize circulation, airway &amp; breathing</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Benzodiazepines</mark> (repeat administration until termination of seizure activity)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Begin antiepileptic drugs</strong></p>
<p><strong>EEG monitoring for refractory status epilepticus or failure to regain consciousness</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>AEDs = antiepileptic drugs; EEG = electroencephalography.</strong></p>
<p><strong>BZD先止抽，长效防再抽，意识不恢复再上EEG</strong></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<span class="mark">ABC</span>，<span class="mark">建立IV，查fingerstick glucose</span>**🡪先保命，排低血糖

**<span class="mark">IV benzodiazepine</span>🡪终止当前发作**

**lorazepam**

**diazepam (还可rectum)**

**midazolam (还可IM)**

**<span class="mark">IV longer-acting antiseizure medication</span>🡪防止再次发作** 因为苯二氮卓类 **起效快但维持短**

**levetiracetam**

**fosphenytoin**

**valproic acid**

若仍<span class="mark">**持续发作**🡪**麻醉药持续输注**</span>**（midazolam, pentobarbital, propofol**）

若抽搐停止后，**<span class="mark">意识不恢复🡪continuous EEG</span>🡪查** **nonconvulsive status epilepticus**

**<span class="mark">稳定后</span>做<span class="mark">CT/MRI、感染代谢</span>评估🡪找病因**

若怀疑<span class="mark">meningitis,encephalitis🡪**lumbar puncture**</span>

Following proper therapy, patients with GCSE typically **regain responsiveness in 10-20 minutes**. 

<u>**<span class="mark">Persistent unresponsive state</span>**</u> may be due to:

> **<span class="mark">Sedation</span>** due to persistent effects of **benzodiazepines**
>
> **<span class="mark">ongoing seizure activity</span> without physical manifestations (ie, nonconvulsive status epilepticus)**. 

**To differentiate between these 2 states, <span class="mark">electroencephalography</span> should be performed. **

**If <span class="mark">electrographic seizure activity continues</span> despite benzodiazepines and AED, a <span class="mark">continuous infusion of benzodiazepines</span> can be initiated, and <span class="mark">propofol or pentobarbital</span> can be used in refractory cases.**

<img src="images/media/image33.png" style="width:4.01426in;height:4.08021in" />

<table style="width:81%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 65%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Myoclonus status epilepticus</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Etiology</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Severe neurologic injury (eg, cardiac arrest)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical<br />
features</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Comatose patient</p>
<p>Appears <strong>within 72 hr of injury</strong></p>
<p><strong>Involuntary muscle contraction</strong> in a joint or limb</p>
<p>Generalized, symmetric</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Management</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Electroencephalography</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Antiepileptic medications</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**心跳骤停后仍昏迷 + 全身短促反复抽动，病因: prolonged cerebral hypoxia**

**myoclonus 不是典型 UMN 或 LMN 体征。它本质是脑缺氧后的异常神经放电/去抑制，不一定马上改变腱反射。后期才可能出现 hyperreflexia**

⚠️ **Myoclonus 6 大成因鉴别**（USMLE 高频）：
- **Serotonin Syndrome**（SSRI / MDMA / Tramadol / Triptan 等 5-HT 类合用）— 伴 hyperreflexia + clonus + 高热 + AMS（见 [[mistakes/uworld-mistakes#^Q11853]]）
- **缺氧后脑病**（心跳骤停后 72h 内）— 伴昏迷，预后差
- **代谢性**（尿毒症 asterixis / 肝衰 / 低钠 / 低钙 / 低血糖）
- **感染性**（CJD = prion / 脑炎 / SSPE = 麻疹后亚急性硬化性脑炎）
- **退行性**（CJD / Alzheimer 晚期 / Lewy body 痴呆 / Multiple System Atrophy）
- **抗胆碱中毒**（DPH / TCA / atropine）— 伴 "干红怒热" + bizarre 谵妄

→ SS 三联完整对照见 [[完整笔记/专题笔记/psych_物质急性中毒鉴别表]] §2 / §5

<p>± <mark>Lumbar puncture</mark> (for <strong>fever or nuchal rigidity</strong>)</p>
<p><mark>EEG</mark> (<strong>no etiology is identified且病人恢复基线</strong>, nonurgent routine)</p></td>

<p><strong>Focal neurologic examination</strong></p></td>

**<u>Psychogenic nonepileptic seizure (PNES)</u>** 心因性非癫痫发作

a type of **conversion disorder**

**forceful eye closure** vs **seizure**: **眼睛睁开**或不自主凝视

**side-to-side head or body movements**

rapid alerting and reorienting

**快速恢复，没有 postictal confusion**

memory recall of the event

**typically occur in front of witnesses**

may model their behavior after a friend or relative with epilepsy.

**not associated with abnormal cortical activity** during the episode

**<span class="mark">Video-EEG monitoring</span>**🡪lack of associated epileptiform activity

**psychiatric assessment** is crucial: have comorbid psychiatric disorders and/or a history of trauma

<img src="images/media/image34.png" style="width:2.4284in;height:1.06243in" />

**Alprazolam** 是 **benzodiazepine**。\
在老年人，尤其本来就有 **baseline cognitive impairment** 的人，苯二氮卓类可导致：

> **confusion**
>
> **disinhibition**
>
> **paradoxical agitation/aggression** (本来应该“镇静/抗焦虑”的药，反而让患者变得更激动、易怒、更攻击性、更混乱)
>
> 跌倒风险增加

下一步处理

**<span class="mark">Taper and discontinue alprazolam</span>**

**BRAIN TUMORS**

Most Common Brain Cancer Overall

> Metastasis

Most Common Primary Malignant Brain Tumor Mentioned

> Glioblastoma

**Specific Tumor Associations**

Acoustic Neuroma

> Brain tumor with episodic deafness

**<u>Ependymoma</u>**

> Child with **communicating hydrocephalus**, possibly later **noncommunicating hydrocephalus**

**<u>Meningioma</u>**

> Benign brain tumor that the brain can grow around
>
> Sometimes associated with genetics

**<u>Medulloblastoma</u>**

> Arises from the floor of the fourth ventricle
>
> Can cause morning vomiting

**<u>Craniopharyngioma</u>**

> Brain tumor causing **headaches** and **panhypopituitarism**
>
> **Bilateral hemianopia**
>
> Originates from **Rathke pouch**

**<u>Pinealoma</u>**

> Child with:

bitemporal hemianopia

loss of upward gaze

> Can also cause precocious puberty

**Step 2 Pearl**

> Match the tumor to the anatomic clue and endocrine/neurologic syndrome

**CAUDA EQUINA VS CONUS MEDULLARIS**

**Cauda Equina**

Lesion Type

> Lower motor neuron lesion

Symmetry

> Asymmetrical

Spinal Level Emphasized

> S3 to S5

Reflexes

> Hyporeflexia

**Conus Medullaris**

Reflex Pattern Emphasized

> Hyperreflexia pattern

Symmetry

> Symmetrical

Spinal Level Emphasized

> L1 to L2

Step 2 Pearl

> Cauda equina = LMN, asymmetric
>
> Conus medullaris = more symmetric pattern

<span class="mark">36min managment</span>

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 16%" />
<col style="width: 40%" />
<col style="width: 43%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: center;"></th>
<th style="text-align: center;"><p><strong>Conus medullaris syndrome</strong></p>
<p><strong>终末脊髓本体受压，带“脊髓征”</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>对称，高反射</mark>，早尿便</strong></p></th>
<th style="text-align: center;"><p><strong>Cauda equina syndrome</strong></p>
<p><strong>腰骶神经根束受压，带“神经根征”</strong></p>
<p><strong>根痛，<mark>低反射</mark>，<mark>不对称</mark>腿麻痛</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Vertebral level</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>L1-L2</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>L2-sacrum</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Spinal level</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>UMN:</mark> tracts of lumbosacral cord</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>LMN</mark>: lumbosacral spinal roots</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Presentation</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><mark>Severe <strong>low back pain</strong></mark></p>
<p>Mild or absent radicular pain</p>
<p><strong>Bowel/bladder dysfunction</strong></p>
<p><strong>更早、更明显</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Mild or absent low back pain</p>
<p><mark>Severe <strong>radicular pain</strong></mark></p>
<p><strong>Bowel/bladder dysfunction</strong></p>
<p><strong>常较晚或逐渐出现</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Physical<br />
examination</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Motor weakness usually <strong><mark>symmetric</mark></strong></p>
<p><mark><strong>Hyperreflexia</strong>, UMN signs</mark></p>
<p><strong>Symmetric</strong> perianal/saddle numbness</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Motor weakness usually <strong><mark>asymmetric</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Areflexia/hyporeflexia</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Asymmetric patchy</strong> saddle numbness that may <mark>extend to the leg</mark></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

| 特征 | 圆锥综合征 (Conus) | 马尾综合征 (Cauda Equina) |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 受损平面 | L1 - L2 (脊髓末端) | L2 以下 (神经根) |
| 无力程度 | **<span class="mark">对称性</span>** | **<span class="mark">非对称性</span>** |
| 腱反射 | **活跃/增强 (UMN)** | **消失/减弱 (LMN)** |
| 大小便障碍 | **早期且严重** | 相对后期出现 |
| 感觉缺失 | 局限于围肛区 | 鞍区感觉缺失 (Saddle anesthesia) |

<u>**Spinal epidural hematoma** (SEH)</u>

complication of **neuraxial anesthesia (eg, epidural block), lumbar puncture, or spinal surgery**

risk factors:

older adults taking **antithrombotic medications**

coagulopathies (eg, thrombocytopenia)

**spinal structural abnormalities**

**osteoporosis**

cord compression🡪**progressive motor and sensory dysfunction**🡪**<span class="mark">cauda equina syndrome</span>** with **bowel and bladder dysfunction**

**localized back pain** and **point tenderness**

may also develop **radicular pain**

**venous**🡪**slowly progressive** (ie, **<span class="mark">days</span>**)

Management

<span class="mark">urgent **MRI of the spine**</span> to evaluate for blood within the canal

**surgical emergency**, requires **<span class="mark">urgent decompression (eg, laminectomy)</span>**

**<u>Spinal epidural abscess</u>**

**Trauma🡪hematoma🡪abscess **

Risk factors:

**糖尿病**

**IV drug use**

**免疫抑制**

**近期脊柱操作** (**Epidural analgesia)**

**菌血症**

**外伤**

The classic triad:

**<span class="mark">Focal spinal pain</span>** 🡪 **radiculopathic pain**

> typically progress in the following fashion:

**Focal back pain** →

**Nerve root pain** (eg, **shooting, electric-shock sensation**) →

Motor **weakness**, **sensory changes, bowel/bladder dysregulation** →

**Paralysis**

**<span class="mark">Neurologic deficits</span>** (eg, weakness, sensory changes, bowel/bladder dysregulation)

**<span class="mark">Fever</span>** (~50% of patients), **leukocytosis**, **↑ESR**

**如果是颈椎硬膜外脓肿，炎症/脓肿可向前波及retropharyngeal space（咽后间隙），出现：**

**咽痛**

**颈痛僵硬**

**<span class="mark">Urgent MRI with contrast</span>**

Management

**broad-spectrum IV antibiotics**

常常需要 **紧急引流/减压**

| **项目** | **Spinal epidural hematoma (SEH)** | **Spinal epidural abscess (SEA)** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 本质 | 硬膜外**积血**压迫脊髓/神经根 | 硬膜外**脓肿**压迫脊髓/神经根 |
| 常见诱因 | **外伤、抗凝/溶栓、出血体质、椎管操作** | **糖尿病、菌血症、皮肤/牙源感染、椎体骨髓炎、免疫抑制、IVDU**，也可**外伤后继发感染** |
| 起病速度 | <span class="mark">**急**，常在**分钟到数小时**</span>内进展 | 常较<span class="mark">**亚急性**，多在**数天到数周**进展</span> |
| 疼痛特点 | **<span class="mark">突发剧烈</span>背/颈痛**，局部叩痛明显 | **<span class="mark">进行性</span>背/颈痛**，可有局灶压痛，后期可出现根性痛 |
| 发热/感染指标 | **通常没有发热** | **常有<span class="mark">发热、白细胞升高、ESR/CRP高</span>**，但不是每例都有发热 |
| 神经缺损 | 可迅速出现**无力、感觉缺失、大小便功能障碍** | 也会有神经缺损，但通常是**随着感染扩展逐渐加重** |
| 最佳检查 | **<span class="mark">MRI</span> spine** | **<span class="mark">MRI</span> spine with gadolinium contrast** |
| 治疗 | **紧急外科减压/引流血肿** | **立即抗生素** ± **外科引流/减压** |
| 考试题眼 | “**突然**痛 + 抗凝/外伤/腰穿后 + 快速瘫” | “**发热** + 背痛/颈痛 + 神经缺损 + DM/IVDU/感染史” |

**ULTRA-HIGH-YIELD RAPID REVIEW**

Must-Memorize Numbers and Patterns

Diabetes

> A1C 6.5 or greater on 2 occasions
>
> Fasting glucose 126 or greater on 2 occasions
>
> Random glucose greater than 200 with symptoms once
>
> GTT greater than 200 once

Subacute Thyroiditis

> Viral illness 2 to 3 weeks earlier
>
> Low TSH
>
> High ESR
>
> Low uptake

Thyroid Nodule

> First step = TSH + ultrasound
>
> Low TSH = scan
>
> Normal/high TSH = FNA

Primary Hyperparathyroidism

> High PTH
>
> High calcium
>
> Low phosphate

Secondary Hyperparathyroidism

> High PTH
>
> Low calcium
>
> High phosphorus

Addison Labs

> Low sodium
>
> High potassium
>
> Acidosis
>
> Low glucose

Conn Syndrome Labs

> High sodium
>
> Low potassium
>
> Alkalosis

Cushing Disease Pattern

> Low-dose dex no suppression
>
> High-dose dex suppression
>
> Pituitary source

Stroke

> Initial test = non-contrast CT
>
> Most accurate test = MRI

Vessel Syndromes

> ACA = leg weakness + incontinence
>
> MCA = speech + face/arm findings
>
> PICA = vertigo + ataxia + ipsilateral face + contralateral body
>
> PCA = visual loss with macular sparing

Ischemic Stroke Treatment

> Within 4 hours = tPA
>
> After 4 hours = aspirin

Tremors

> Parkinson = resting
>
> Essential = action/stress
>
> Intention = worse as target approached

Restless Leg Syndrome

> Most common cause = iron deficiency

Huntington

> Autosomal dominant
>
> Anticipation

Myasthenia vs Lambert-Eaton

> MG = worse with use
>
> LEMS = better with use

MS

> Waxing and waning
>
> Symptoms separated in time

Alzheimer

> Diffuse atrophy

Vascular Dementia

> Stepwise decline

NPH

> Ataxia
>
> Incontinence
>
> Dementia

Migraine

> Acute abortive if no heart disease = sumatriptan

Cluster Headache

> Abortive = 100% oxygen

Benign Positional Vertigo

> Diagnose with Dix-Hallpike
>
> Treat with Epley

ALS

> No sensory loss

Guillain-Barre

> LP = high protein, no white blood cells

Transverse Myelitis

> Back pain and chest tightness

Botulism

> Descending paralysis

Absence Seizure

> Ethosuximide

Status Epilepticus

> Lorazepam

Brain Tumors

> Most common overall = metastasis
>
> Most common primary malignant in this lecture = glioblastoma

【补充】

**LEAD POISONING🡪<span class="mark">acquired sideroblastic anemia</span>**

**Symptoms<span class="mark">腹痛+神经症状</span>**

> Episodic **abdominal pain**, gum bleeding
>
> Fatigue, irritability
>
> **AMS (altered mental status), wrist drop**

**Enzymes**

> **<span class="mark">ALA dehydratase</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Ferrochelatase</span>**

**Diagnosis**

> **骨髓：ring sideroblasts （Prussian blue stain）**
>
> **外周血：basophilic stippling**

**Treatment**

> **<span class="mark">Succimer🡪GI</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Dimercaprol🡪BM</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">2+=penicillamine🡪plasma</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">EDTA🡪2+ out of everywhere</span>**

**<u>Alpha-synuclein neurodegenerative disorders</u>**

**<u>rapid eye movement (REM) sleep behavior disorder</u>**

常是 α-synuclein 相关神经退行性病变的**早期表现**

正常 REM 睡眠时肌肉应该“瘫痪”（atonia），人不会把梦做出来**\
RBD 是 REM atonia 消失 → 病人会拳打脚踢、喊叫、梦境表演**

**<u>Parkinson disease</u>**

> **substantia nigra dopaminergic neuron loss**
>
> **Lewy bodies：α-synuclein**

**<u>dementia with Lewy bodies</u>**

**早期 dementia + visual hallucinations + parkinsonism**

**Lewy bodies：α-synuclein**

**<u>multiple system atrophy</u>**

**Parkinsonism + autonomic dysfunction + cerebellar signs**

**glial cytoplasmic inclusions：α-synuclein**

<img src="images/media/image35.png" style="width:3.12519in;height:3.33999in" />

**Alcohol withdrawal 时间轴**

| **时间** | **表现** |
|:---|:---|
| 6–24小时 | tremor, anxiety, nausea, insomnia, **tachycardia** |
| 12–48小时 | withdrawal **seizures** |
| 12–48小时 | alcoholic **hallucinosis**，常见昆虫/动物视幻 |
| 48–96小时 | **delirium tremens**：delirium + **<span class="mark">autonomic instability</span>** |

治疗：**long acting <span class="mark">benzodiazepines</span>**

⚠️ **AWS seizure 用药陷阱**：BZD 一线（GABA-A 激动）；**Phenytoin 无效**（Na 通道阻断，不针对 GABA-A 脱敏机制）；status epilepticus 时加 **Phenobarbital**（也作用 GABA-A）。

→ 完整对照见 [[完整笔记/专题笔记/psych_物质急诊速查]] §15.1（AWS seizure 用药对比，Q3187 触发）

**<u>Todd paralysis</u>**：postictal Todd paralysis due to seizure activity

> **Seizure🡪突然倒地 + 短暂意识丧失**
>
> **醒来后 confusion**
>
> **一侧肢体瘫痪**
>
> **脑影像正常**
>
> **几小时内完全恢复**
