**IE🡪brain abscess**, next step:

**<span class="mark">3 sets blood cultures from 3 different venipuncture sites</span>**

**<span class="mark">Transthoracic echocardiography</span>**

发热 + 亚急性不适 + 新发心杂音 + 结膜出血 + 脑脓肿样病灶，先想感染性心内膜炎并 septic emboli；最佳下一步是 **echocardiography**（并做**3 组 blood cultures**）

<img src="images/media/image36.png" style="width:6.03468in;height:5.07609in" />

**<u>Riley-Day syndrome</u>**

不是单纯颈动脉窦本身坏了，而是来自 carotid sinus 的 baroreceptor 传入反射通路先天异常，所以站立时不能正常触发升压反应，导致 orthostatic hypotension。\
**familial dysautonomia → afferent baroreflex failure → carotid sinus pressure signals can’t be transmitted normally → orthostatic hypotension**\
 **baby/child**

 自主神经异常

 喂养困难

 肌张力低

 泪液少

 温度调节差

 血压不稳

 以后出现明显 **orthostatic hypotension**

 Riley-Day syndrome

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 16%" />
<col style="width: 83%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Malignant hyperthermia</strong></p>
<p><strong>麻醉后短时间内出现心动过速、呼吸急促、全身肌强直和棕色尿，即使尚未高热，也要首先考虑</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Epidemiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Genetic mutation alters control of intracellular calcium遗传性钙离子调节异常</strong></p>
<p>Triggered by <strong><mark>volatile inhaled anesthetics, succinylcholine</mark></strong>, excessive heat</p>
</blockquote>
<p>🡪导致骨骼肌细胞内<strong>ryanodine receptor 异常,Ca²⁺ 大量释放</strong></p>
<p>🡪全身骨骼肌持续收缩, 代谢率暴增, 耗氧增加, CO₂大量产生</p>
<p> 肌肉坏死 → <strong>rhabdomyolysis，高K</strong></p>
<p> 肌红蛋白尿 → <strong>dark/brown urine</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Manifestations</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>术后极短时间（15min）</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Masseter muscle</mark>/<mark>generalized rigidity</mark>咬肌僵硬，浑身僵硬</strong></p>
<p><strong>Rhabdomyolysis, myoglobinuria, <mark>hyperkalemia</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Sinus <mark>tachycardia，hypercarbia</mark></strong> resistant to increased minute ventilation<strong>高代谢</strong></p>
<p><strong>Hyperthermia (<mark>late</mark> manifestation)体温不高不能排除</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>R<mark>espiratory/ventilatory support</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Immediate cessation of causative anesthetic</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Dantrolene</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

| **特征** | **Malignant hyperthermia (MH)** | **Neuroleptic malignant syndrome (NMS)** | **Serotonin syndrome (SS)** ⭐ |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 诱因 | **<span class="mark">麻醉药 / succinylcholine</span>** | **<span class="mark">抗精神病药、dopamine blockade</span>** | **<span class="mark">5-HT 类合用</span>**（SSRI / MDMA / Triptan / Tramadol / MAOI / Linezolid / DXM）|
| 起病 | **<span class="mark">分钟到数小时</span>**（术中）| **<span class="mark">数天</span>** | **<span class="mark">小时</span>**（加药 / 换药 / MDMA 后）|
| 场景 | 术中 / 术后 | 长期用抗精神病药 | 加药 / SSRI + MDMA 派对 |
| 肌张力 | 肌僵硬 + **masseter rigidity**（早期）| **lead-pipe rigidity（铅管样）+ bradyreflexia** | **Hyperreflexia + Myoclonus + Clonus** ⭐（指纹）|
| AMS | 高热相关 | 有 | 有（激越 → 昏迷）|
| 自主神经 | 亢进 + **高 ETCO₂** ⭐ | 亢进 | 亢进（出汗 / HR↑ / BP↑）|
| CK / myoglobinuria | 有（↑↑↑）| 有（↑↑↑）| 可↑（较轻）|
| 治疗 | **Dantrolene** + 停麻醉药 + 降温 | 停药 + 支持 + **Dantrolene + Bromocriptine**（D2 激动）| 停药 + 支持 + BZD + **Cyproheptadine**（5-HT2A 拮抗）|

> [!tip] 三联速记决策（USMLE 高频）
> - **起病速度**：术中（MH）/ 小时（SS）/ 天（NMS）
> - **反射**：↑ 亢进（SS）/ 铅管 ↓（NMS）/ 僵硬（MH）
> - **触发药**：麻醉 + Succinylcholine（MH）/ 抗精神病药（NMS）/ 5-HT 类（SS）
> - **三药角色**：Dantrolene = MH + NMS / Bromocriptine = NMS only / Cyproheptadine = SS

→ 完整对照见 [[完整笔记/专题笔记/psych_物质急性中毒鉴别表]] §5（Q11853 触发本表加 SS 列）

**<u>Autonomic dysreflexia（自主神经反射异常）</u>**

经典场景：

> **脊髓损伤在 <span class="mark">T6</span> 以上**
>
> lesion 以下出现 **noxious stimulus**（最常见就是**尿潴留/导尿管堵塞**）
>
> 引发 **严重高血压 + 头痛 + 出汗 + 面部潮红 + 反射性心动过缓**

**2️⃣ 机制理解**

**正常情况下，**身体下部如果有刺激（比如膀胱过度充盈），会激活交感神经。\
但正常人脑干和高位中枢可以把这股交感冲动“压下去”，维持平衡。

**脊髓损伤后，**如果损伤在 **T6以上**，来自高位中枢的抑制信号传不过去。\
于是 lesion 以下的刺激会导致

**lesion以上，**因为颈动脉窦/主动脉弓感受到高血压，会启动**副交感反射**：

> **心动过缓**
>
> **面部潮红**
>
> 出汗（多在病灶以上）

**lesion以下，失控的交感兴奋**

> 广泛血管收缩
>
> **严重高血压**

所以会形成一个很典型的组合：**severe hypertension + bradycardia + headache + diaphoresis/flushing**

**一个高位截瘫患者出现上述症状，先查：**

> **导尿管堵没堵**
>
> **膀胱是不是胀**
>
> **有没有便秘**
>
> **有没有压疮/刺激物**

<img src="images/media/image37.jpeg" style="width:3.89583in;height:4.4525in" />

<td style="text-align: left;">常见场景</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>leaning on elbow</strong></p>
<p><strong>dialysis positioning</strong></p>
<p><strong>cubital tunnel</strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>handlebar palsy</strong></p>
<p><strong>hamate hook injury</strong></p>
<p><strong>Guyon canal compression</strong></p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

FCU = Flexor carpi ulnaris尺侧腕屈肌，FDP = Flexor digitorum profundus指深屈肌

<img src="images/media/image38.jpeg" style="width:1.27569in;height:2.87153in" />

<img src="images/media/image39.png" style="width:3.09583in;height:1.88542in" /><img src="images/media/image40.jpeg" style="width:3.22778in;height:2.37222in" />

**Median**

> **elbow**：前臂屈肌、旋前也受损
>
> **wrist**：主要 **thenar**🡪**<span class="mark">对掌/OK sign</span>** + 手指感觉症状

**Ulnar**

> **elbow**：**<span class="mark">wrist flexion weakness</span> + grip weakness**
>
> **wrist**：**手内在肌**症状为主🡪**<span class="mark">分指/夹纸/4-5指</span>**，**不影响腕屈**

**Radial**

> **high lesion**：**肘伸**也受影响
>
> **radial groove**：**<span class="mark">伸腕/ wrist drop</span>**
>
> **PIN**：**纯运动多**，感觉少

| **神经** | **主要动作** | **主要感觉区** | **最经典损伤表现** | **高频关键词** |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **Median** | 屈腕、旋前、拇对掌 | 拇/食/中/半个无名指 | thenar weakness, ape hand, carpal tunnel | OK sign, opposition |
| **Ulnar** | 指外展内收、握力、部分屈腕 | 小指+半个无名指、手内侧 | ulnar claw, hand clumsiness | interossei, Froment |
| **Radial** | 伸腕、伸指、伸肘 | 手背桡侧 | **wrist drop** | humeral shaft, Saturday night palsy |

**<u>Primary VZV infection (chickenpox)</u>**

latent VZV in the **geniculate ganglion**, disrupting **facial nerve function**

**diffuse, vesicular rash**

**fever, malaise, and pharyngitis**

then migrates via sensory nerves to cranial nerve and dorsal spinal ganglia

**<u>Reactivation</u>**

**painful, vesicular rash** in a dermatomal distribution🡪**crust**

occurs commonly in adults, and can rarely occur in children

**<u>Herpes zoster oticus/Ramsay Hunt syndrome</u>**--latent VZV reactivation

> **<span class="mark">Ear pain</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Facial weakness</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Vesicular rash</span>** <span class="mark">in **external auditory canal**</span>—facial nerve

spread to the vestibulocochlear nerve (CN VIII)

auditory🡪hearing loss, hyperacusis, tinnitus

vestibular 🡪vertigo, nausea/vomiting

Treatment

**<span class="mark">corticosteroids</span>**

**<span class="mark">antiviral medications</span>**

**Early initiation (\<3 days)** a/w improved recovery of facial nerve function; however, even with treatment many patients have **residual facial weakness**. 

If facial nerve paralysis, **<span class="mark">protection of the eye</span>** (**artificial tears, lubricating ointment**) is of paramount importance.

**<u>Alcohol-related toxic distal polyneuropathy</u>**

**Impair axonal function** 🡪reduction in the number of **small myelinated and unmyelinated fibers**🡪 **<span class="mark">symmetric distal polyneuropathy (ie, stocking and glove pattern)</span>**:

**Distal polyneuropathy** (burning pain in both fee)

**<span class="mark">Length-dependent</span>** pattern **(<span class="mark">toes🡪whole foot gradually</span>**)

paresthesia, burning pain, and numbness

**<span class="mark">areflexia</span>**, begins with **<span class="mark">bilateral ankle reflex loss</span> (周围神经病常见)**

loss of light touch and vibratory sense （大纤维受累）

**gait ataxia**

Treatment:

**Cessation of alcohol**

**<span class="mark">thiamine supplementation</span>**

**Gabapentin, TCA for refractory pain**

**<u>HORNER SYNDROME 颈交感神经通路（三级神经元通路）受损</u>**

Ipsilateral ptosis**上睑下垂**：交感神经受损导致上睑板肌无力

Miosis**瞳孔缩小**：瞳孔开大肌麻痹，副交感（缩瞳）占优势

Anhidrosis**面部无汗**：交感神经纤维受损导致汗腺失去支配

Dilation lag**散瞳延迟**：在暗处瞳孔扩大缓慢（诊断特征）

<img src="images/media/image41.jpeg" style="width:3.78897in;height:4.60127in" />

| **症状组合** | **诊断方向** | **排除逻辑** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **Horner + 肩痛 + 吸烟史** | **Pancoast Tumor** | **肿瘤压迫星状神经节。** |
| **Horner + 剧烈头痛** | **Carotid Dissection** | **血管壁撕裂影响其表面的交感丛。** |
| **Horner + 昏迷 + 瞳孔固定** | **Brain Herniation** | **通常表现为散瞳（CN III 受压），而非缩瞳。** |
| **仅有 Ptosis + 易疲劳** | **重症肌无力** | **不会有瞳孔改变。** |

**<u>local anesthetic systemic toxicity</u>误入血管**

早期：先阻断 抑制性神经通路🡪**<span class="mark">中枢神经兴奋</span>**

**Perioral numbness口周麻木**

**Metallic taste金属味**

**tinnitus耳鸣**

焦虑、激动、震颤

随后可进展为**<span class="mark">严重癫痫/心血管毒性</span>**

**generalized tonic-clonic seizure**

嗜睡

呼吸抑制

心律失常

心血管崩溃

Treatment：

**立刻停药**

处理气道、氧合、循环

**benzodiazepine 控制癫痫**

严重者用 **lipid emulsion therapy**。

<table style="width:95%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />
<col style="width: 82%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Narcolepsy发作性睡病</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>DSM-5<br />
diagnostic<br />
criteria</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Recurrent lapses into sleep or naps (≥3×/week for 3 months)</p>
<p>≥1 of the following:</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Cataplexy猝倒</strong>: brief loss of muscle tone precipitated by <strong>strong emotion (eg, laughter, excitement)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Low cerebrospinal fluid levels of hypocretin-1</strong></p>
<p><strong>Shortened REM sleep latency</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Associated<br />
features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Hypnagogic入睡前 or hypnopompic醒前 hallucinations</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Sleep paralysis</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Sleep hygiene (eg, scheduled sleep, caffeine &amp; alcohol avoidance)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Modafinil</mark> (first-line)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Amphetamines</mark> (refractory cases)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**年轻、苗条且睡眠质量好的患者出现日间不可抗拒的嗜睡**尤其是在无聊或餐后（上课、看电影时）**，应高度怀疑Narcolepsy，首选多项小睡潜伏期试验（MSLT）进行诊断。**

> **核心缺陷：** 下丘脑中产生下丘脑分泌素（Hypocretin/Orexin）的神经元丢失。
>
> **后果：** 睡眠与觉醒的开关失灵。患者会直接从清醒状态跳入 **REM 睡眠**（快速眼动期）。这就是为什么患者可能会有入睡前幻觉（Hypnagogic hallucinations）或猝倒（Cataplexy）。
>
> **诊断：<span class="mark">Multiple Sleep Latency Test</span> (MSLT)：**确诊发作性睡病的“金标准”

**方法：** 在白天的不同时间点让患者小睡。

**诊断标准：** 1. 平均入睡潜伏期（Sleep latency）**\< 8 分钟**；2. 出现至少 2 次**入睡期 REM（SOREMPs）**。

**发作性睡病（Narcolepsy）的典型四联征**

| **症状** | **描述** | **机制** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| **日间过度嗜睡 (EDS)** | 最早且最恒定的症状。 | 觉醒调节失灵。 |
| **猝倒 (Cataplexy)** | 情绪激动时突然肌肉无力，但意识清醒。 | **清醒时突然发生 REM 期肌张力丧失。** |
| **睡眠瘫痪 (Sleep Paralysis)** | 刚醒或入睡时无法动弹。 | REM 残余。 |
| **入睡前幻觉** | 视觉或听觉幻觉。 | 进入 REM 太快。 |

> **日间嗜睡：** 首选**<span class="mark">Modafinil</span>**（非苯丙胺类兴奋剂）。
>
> **猝倒：** 首选 **羟考酸钠（<span class="mark">Sodium oxybate</span>）**，也可使用 **<span class="mark">REM 抑制剂（如 SSRI/SNRI）</span>**。

**避坑指南：** 看到“日间嗜睡”先看 **BMI** 和 **打鼾史**。

> 肥胖 + 打鼾 = **<span class="mark">OSA</span>** → 首选 **<span class="mark">Polysomnography (PSG)</span>**。
>
> 苗条 + 情绪激动后摔倒 = **<span class="mark">Narcolepsy</span>** → 首选 **<span class="mark">PSG + MSLT</span>**。
>
> **Overnight pulse oximetry🡪**筛查 OSA

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>

</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Paroxysmal attacks of unilateral, severe, stabbing pain lasting <mark>seconds</mark> to 2 min</strong></p>
<p><strong>Limited to CN V distribution (mainly V2 &amp; V3)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Triggered by innocuous stimuli (eg, chewing, talking, brushing teeth, light touch)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Work-up</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>MRI/MRA of the brain with contrast</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Nerve conduction</mark></strong> (eg, trigeminal reflex) testing <strong>if unable to obtain MRI</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Carbamazepine</mark></strong> or <strong><mark>oxcarbazepine</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Surgery (eg, decompression</mark></strong>) only for <strong>severe, medically refractory</strong> cases</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>MRA</strong> = MR angiography.</td>
</tr>

<img src="images/media/image42.jpeg" style="width:3.84375in;height:2.47014in" /><img src="images/media/image43.jpeg" style="width:4.25417in;height:2.47083in" />

<u>**Bilateral** **trigeminal neuralgia**</u>

**<span class="mark">multiple sclerosis</span>** inflammatory plaques 🡪 **bilateral** **trigeminal neuralgia,** also occur with **internuclear ophthalmoplegia** （**<span class="mark">INO：病侧眼不内收，对侧眼外展震</span>**）

trigeminal sensory nuclei are relatively close to the midline

medial longitudinal fasciculus is also close to the midline

Treatment:

**<span class="mark">high-dose glucocorticoids</span>**, as with an **MS exacerbation**

typical treatments for TN (eg, carbamazepine, surgery) ineffective

<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Abnormal gait patterns</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Parkinsonian</strong><br />
(PD, MSA, DLB, VD)</p>
<p><strong>窄、小、碎</strong></p>
<p><strong>启动最费劲</strong></p></td>

<p><strong><mark>Narrow</mark> based</strong></p>
<p><strong>Shuffling (<mark>small-stride gait</mark>)</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>基底节多巴胺不足后，运动程序启动和放大都变差，导致 <strong>hypokinesia / bradykinesia</strong>。病人不是“不会走”，而是 <strong>步子发不出去、迈不开、越走越碎</strong>。因为姿势反射也差，所以转身特别慢，容易慌张步态</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Weakness with spasticity</strong><br />
(myelopathy)</p>
<p><strong>锥体束一紧</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>两腿像剪刀</mark></strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Narrow</mark> based</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Scissoring</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Toes scrape the floor</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>这是 <strong><mark>上运动神经元/锥体束损伤</mark></strong> 的步态。肌张力增高，尤其髋内收肌和伸肌群张力高，腿会 <strong>内收交叉</strong>，像剪刀；踝跖屈、膝伸直，脚尖容易擦地。脊髓病（myelopathy）很典型</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Myopathic</strong><br />
(myopathies, MG)</p>
<p><strong>骨盆带无力</strong></p>
<p><strong>走路像<mark>鸭子</mark></strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Waddling</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Abnormal pelvic tilt (limb girdle weakness)</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>近端肌无力</mark></strong>，尤其 <strong>臀中肌/臀小肌</strong> 和骨盆带肌无力，单脚站立时骨盆撑不住，所以身体要左右摆、躯干向支撑侧倾来代偿，形成<strong>“鸭步”</strong>。MG 也可表现近端无力，但更常是波动性疲劳</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Magnetic</strong><br />
(<mark>NPH)</mark></p>
<p>想走走不出</p>
<p><mark>脚底像带磁</mark></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Difficulty initiating steps</mark> + 尿失禁 + 认知下降</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>额叶-皮质下步态程序受损，不是力量不够，而是 <strong>“<mark>脚抬不起来</mark>”</strong>。所以病人想走，但脚像黏在地上，小步、拖步、启动困难特别明显</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Vestibular</strong><br />
(BPPV, Ménière disease)</p>
<p><mark>前庭坏一边</mark></p>
<p><mark>走路歪一边</mark></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Stumbling or veering to one side (usually the affected side)偏向患侧</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>前庭系统负责头位和空间平衡。单侧前庭输入失衡时，大脑会误以为身体在转，病人就会 <strong>向患侧偏、歪、摔</strong>。这不是肌力问题，也不是深感觉问题，所以黑暗不一定明显加重到像 sensory ataxia 那么典型</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Cerebellar ataxia</strong><br />
(stroke, drug toxicity,</p>
<p>alcohol, hereditary)</p>
<p><mark>小脑像<strong>醉汉</strong></mark></p>
<p>站得宽，走得晃</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Wide</mark> based</strong></p>
<p><strong>Stumbling, lurching</strong></p>
<p><strong>May be one sided or bilateral depending on etiology</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>小脑负责动作校准、时序和误差修正。小脑坏了后，身体不能把重心连续稳定地转移，所以只能 <mark><strong>把双脚分开站宽一点</strong>增加稳定性</mark>；同时步伐摇晃、忽左忽右，像喝醉。<strong>酒精、小脑卒中、药物毒性</strong>都常见</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Sensory ataxia</strong><br />
(sensory neuropathy,</p>
<p>VB<sub>12</sub> deficiency)</p>
<p>深感觉一丢，<mark>高抬腿猛踩地；灯一关，走更差</mark></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Wide based</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>High stepping/stamping</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Worse in the dark</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>深感觉/本体觉坏了，病人不知道脚落在哪里，只能靠 <strong>视觉补偿</strong>。所以会把腿抬很高，再重重踩下去，用“震动反馈”帮助确认地面位置；一到黑暗里，视觉补偿没了，马上更不稳，这一点特别有鉴别价值</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>BPPV</strong> = benign positional paroxysmal vertigo; <strong>DLB =</strong> dementia with Lewy bodies; <strong>MG</strong> = myasthenia gravis; <strong>MSA</strong> = multiple system atrophy; <strong>NPH</strong> = normal pressure hydrocephalus; <strong>PD</strong> = Parkinson disease; <strong>VD</strong> = vascular dementia.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

 **窄 + 小碎步** → **帕金森**

 **窄 + 剪刀步** → **痉挛 / 脊髓** （**<span class="mark">UMN lesion</span>** → spasticity → hip adductors 张力过高 → 内收肌太紧，把腿夹成剪刀）

 **左右摇摆像鸭子** → **肌病**

 **脚像粘地** → **NPH / magnetic**

 **总往一边歪** → **前庭**

 **宽基底 + 像醉酒** → **小脑**

 **宽基底 + 高抬腿猛踩 + 黑暗更差** → **深感觉缺失**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 24%" />

</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Frontal (apraxic) gait</strong></p>
<p>(frontal lobe degeneration</p>
<p>NPH)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">Magnetic (freezing): start &amp; turn hesitation</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">Dementia, incontinence, frontal lobe signs</td>

<tr>

<p>(PD, DLB)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">Short steps, shuffling, narrow based</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">Bradykinesia, resting tremor, postural instability, ↓ arm swing</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Vestibular gait</strong><br />

<td style="text-align: left;">Dysdiadochokinesia, dysmetria, nystagmus, − Romberg</td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Weakness with footdrop</strong><br />

<p><strong>fibular head or neck</strong> due to the nerve superficial.  Injury is associated with sensory loss over the dorsum of the foot and impaired dorsiflexion and eversion.</p></td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Sensory ataxia</strong><br />
(vitamin B<sub>12</sub> deficiency,<br />
compressive myelopathy)</td>

<p>often wide based, <strong>worse in the dark</strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>↓ Proprioception of toes, ↓ vibration sense</strong>, <strong><mark>+ Romberg</mark></strong></td>

</tr>

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 17%" />

<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Sydenham chorea</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Preceding GAS infection, months after</p>
<p>Molecular mimicry between <strong>anti-GAS antibodies</strong> &amp; <strong>neuronal antigens in basal ganglia</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Bilateral, progressive involuntary, jerky movements (<mark>worse while awake</mark> &amp; with action, <mark>disappear during sleep</mark>)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Hypotonia</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Behavior changes (emotional lability, obsessive-compulsive behaviors)</strong></p>
<p><strong>± Symptoms of acute rheumatic fever</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Evaluation</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>GAS testing: throat culture, <mark>ASO &amp; anti-DNAse B titers</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Cardiac testing: echocardiography, ECG</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Chronic antibiotics (eg, <mark>penicillin G</mark>)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Symptomatic (antidopaminergics [eg, <mark>haloperidol</mark>])</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Prognosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Spontaneous remission</p>
<p><strong>Recurrence</strong> common</p>
<p>↑ Risk of <strong>rheumatic heart disease</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>anti-DNAse</strong> = antideoxyribonuclease; <strong>ASO</strong> = antistreptolysin O; <strong>GAS</strong> = group A <em>Streptococcus</em>.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<u>**Paroxysmal sympathetic hyperactivity** (PSH)</u> 阵发性交感神经过度兴奋

**<span class="mark">严重脑外伤后</span>，受到护理或体位改变刺激时反复出现高血压、心动过速、呼吸急促、发热和出汗，要首先想到PSH**

<span class="mark">**severe** **traumatic brain injury**</span>🡪**damage to cortical areas** (responsible for modulating and **inhibiting lower sympathetic centers** (eg, in the hypothalamus, brainstem, and spinal cord))🡪**<span class="mark">sympathetic hyperactivity</span>**

**<span class="mark">rapid-onset</span> episodes** of **tachycardia, hypertension, tachypnea**

**fever**, **diaphoresis**

last up to **20-30 minutes**

**triggered by external stimuli** (eg, bathing, repositioning) but may occur **spontaneously**

**clinical diagnosis** with **no confirmatory tests**

Treatment

**<span class="mark">supportive care</span>** (eg, avoiding triggers, treating fever)

medication (eg, opioids, GABA-agonists, α<sub>2</sub>-agonists)—abort/prevent

<img src="images/media/image44.jpeg" style="width:3.3094in;height:2.90272in" /> <img src="images/media/image45.jpeg" style="width:3.10961in;height:2.17564in" />

> **右脸颊虫咬**🡪**蜂窝织炎/局部感染** cellulitis (eg, swelling, erythema of right cheek)，发热
>
> 面部与眼静脉系统 **缺乏静脉瓣**🡪感染逆行扩散到 **cavernous sinus🡪** <u>**septic cavernous sinus thrombosis**</u>

海绵窦内局部神经受累：

> **CN III, IV, VI** → 双侧眼外肌无力🡪眼球运动障碍 / 复视 / 眼肌麻痹
>
> **V1, V2** → 前额、中面部感觉下降
>
> **静脉回流受阻** → **proptosis、periorbital edema**
>
> **颅压增高** → **头痛、平躺加重、呕吐、papilledema**

Diagnosis

**MRI with MR venography**

Treatment:

**<span class="mark">broad-spectrum IV antibiotics</span>**

**<span class="mark">management of increased ICP</span>**

anticoagulation is controversial

**Thiazide 利尿剂（HCTZ）🡪 hypokalemia**

<img src="images/media/image46.png" style="width:2.17639in;height:1.92014in" />**低钾** 会使骨骼肌和心肌细胞膜电活动异常，导致：

> **近端为主的肌无力，走路困难**
>
> **肌痛/肌痉挛**
>
> 严重时可有**弛缓性瘫痪、低反射**
>
> Tetany, rhabdomyolysis
>
> 心电图可见：

**Flat T waves**

**ST depression**

**U waves**

**PVCs/其他心律失常**

**近端肌无力 + 低反射 + HCTZ 使用史 + flat T waves/PVCs = 低钾性电解质紊乱**

<img src="images/media/image47.png" style="width:6.16924in;height:1.45977in" />

**Descending (type B) aortic dissection🡪 <u>Thoracic anterior cord ischemia</u>**

greatest risk at T10-T12 levels (blood flow is lowest)

**diminished reflexes** (reflexes are increased after days or weeks but are diminished initially)

**lower extremities paresis**

**acute bladder paresis** (eg, urinary retention)

loss of **crude touch/pain** sensation (carried in anterior/lateral spinothalamic tracts)

<u>**Anterior cord syndrome**:</u>

> damage **lateral corticospinal tracts** and **anterior horn cells🡪bilateral paralysis**
>
> damage **lateral and anterior spinothalamic tracts🡪loss of pain/temperature and crude touch sensation**
>
> damage **descending autonomic tracts**🡪**urinary retention**

<img src="images/media/image48.jpeg" style="width:4.27692in;height:3.1152in" />

**<u>Subclavian steal syndrome（锁骨下动脉盗血综合征）</u>**

**proximal subclavian artery stenosis（椎动脉起始近端的锁骨下动脉狭窄）**

**手臂用力诱发眩晕（椎基底动脉供血不足）**

**同侧手臂缺血症状：arm pain, fatigue, heaviness**

**两臂收缩压差 \>15–20 mmHg**

**锁骨上杂音supraclavicular systolic bruit**

**诊断：**

**Duplex Doppler ultrasound:** **ipsilateral vertebral flow reversal**

**MRA / CTA**

In major trauma, **bedside CXR/pelvic x-ray/FAST** are common adjuncts, esp **unstable patients**

**<span class="mark"><u>Cervical spine imaging</u></span>**：high-energy trauma + any 1 of the following

> **Neurologic deficit**
>
> **Spinal tenderness**
>
> **Altered mental status**
>
> **Intoxication**
>
> **<span class="mark">Distracting injury</span>**

**Single vertebral fracture in a patient with blunt trauma 🡪 <span class="mark">CT scan entire spine</span>**

**一旦发现一个椎体骨折，要继续筛查整个脊柱，尤其胸腰椎**

<td style="text-align: left;">Red flags</td>

</blockquote></td>

features</td>

<p><strong>Burns</strong>: linear, well demarcated</p>
<p><strong>Fractures</strong>:</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Multiple &amp; in various stages</strong> of healing</p>
<p>Femur fracture in nonambulatory child</p>
<p><strong>Posterior rib fractures</strong></p>

<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Closed spinal dysraphism隐性脊柱裂谱系：小孩 + 新发尿失禁 + 进行性步态变差 + 背痛 + 足畸形</strong></th>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Failure of posterior vertebral arch fusion</p>
<p>± Spinal cord anomalies (eg, lipoma, cyst)</p>
<p>Stretch-induced distal spinal cord dysfunction (tethered cord脊髓栓系)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>May be asymptomatic</p>
<p>Cutaneous, lumbosacral anomalies (eg, hair tuft, mass)</p>
<p><strong><u>Tethered cord syndrome*</u></strong>:</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Neurologic</mark>: LMN signs (weakness, hyporeflexia)</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Urologic</mark>: incontinence/retention; recurrent UTI</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Orthopedic</mark>: back pain, scoliosis, foot deformities</strong></p>
<p><strong>high arches of the feet/pes cavus，hammer toes</strong>慢性足部畸形提示长期神经支配异常</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Management</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>MRI of the spine</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Surgical detethering</mark></strong> of cord if symptomatic</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">*Age of onset &amp; organ system involvement are variable.</td>
</tr>

</table>

<img src="images/media/image50.png" style="width:3.55833in;height:2.25139in" />

<img src="images/media/image51.jpeg" style="width:3.91378in;height:4.56962in" />

**Caput succedaneum**头皮水肿

> **出生即见**
>
> diffuse scalp swelling
>
> <img src="images/media/image52.png" style="width:1.69931in;height:1.65208in" />crosses suture lines
>
> benign, **resolves spontaneously**🡪**<span class="mark">reassurance + observation</span>**

**Cephalohematoma骨膜下出血**

> **subperiosteal vessel rupture🡪subperiosteal hemorrhage**
>
> does **not** cross sutures
>
> may cause **hyperbilirubinemia**
>
> **<span class="mark">reassurance + observation</span>**

**Subgaleal hemorrhage 帽状健膜下出血**🡪急症

**subgaleal vein shearing**

帽状腱膜下空间很大，可以积很多血，尤其见于**<span class="mark">vacuum-assisted delivery</span>**

> **头皮弥漫波动性肿胀**
>
> **进行性增大**
>
> **苍白、心率快、低血压**
>
> **Treatment:**

**<span class="mark">Serial hemoglobin monitoring</span>**

**<span class="mark">volume resuscitation</span>**

**<span class="mark">correction of coagulopathy</span>\**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />

<tr>
<th colspan="4" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Neonatal scalp swelling</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"></td>
<td style="text-align: center;"><strong>Caput succedaneum</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: center;"><strong>Cephalohematoma</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: center;"><strong>Subgaleal hemorrhage</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Location</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Subcutaneous</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Subperiosteal</strong> (between skull &amp; periosteum) </p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Between periosteum &amp; gala aponeurotica</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clinical features</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Present <mark>at birth</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Soft, boggy</strong></p>
<p><strong>Crosses</strong> sutures</p>
<p>Overlying skin is normal</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Forceps or vaccum</strong></p>
<p>Present <strong><mark>hours</mark> after birth</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Firm</mark>, nonfluctuant</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Does not cross sutures</mark></strong></p>
<p>Overlying skin is normal</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Vaccum-assisted deliveries</strong></p>
<p>Can <strong>expand over <mark>days</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>Soft, fluctuant</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Diffuse</mark>, crosses sutures</strong></p>
<p>± Overlying <strong>bruising</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Prognosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Self-resolves in days</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>↑ Hyperbilirubinemia risk</strong></p>
<p><strong>Resorbs within a month</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Can cause <strong>life-threatening blood loss</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 19%" />
<col style="width: 80%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Bilirubin-induced neurologic dysfunction</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathophysiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Excess free, unconjugated bilirubin crosses the blood-brain barrier</p>
<p>Deposition of bilirubin in basal ganglia &amp; brainstem nuclei</p>
<p>Neuronal damage, necrosis &amp; atrophy</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Risk factors</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Prematurity</p>
<p>Hemolysis (eg, <strong>G6PD deficiency</strong>)</p>
<p>Birth trauma (eg, <strong>cephalohematoma</strong>)</p>
<p>Exclusive breastfeeding with excessive weight loss</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Acute encephalopathy</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>± Reversible</strong> (treatment: <strong>phototherapy, exchange transfusion</strong>)</p>
<p>Clinical findings</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Lethargy or inconsolability</p>
<p><strong>Hypotonia (early) or hypertonia (late)</strong></p>
<p>Apnea/respiratory failure, feeding difficulties, <strong>seizures</strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Chronic encephalopathy</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Irreversible</strong></p>
<p>Clinical findings</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Developmental delay</p>
<p><strong>Sensorineural hearing loss</strong></p>
<p>Choreoathetoid movements</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

choroid plexus papilloma（脉络丛乳头状瘤）→ CSF 产生增多🡪婴儿 + 侧脑室肿块 + 脑积水

婴儿多见

侧脑室多见

**CSF production ↑**

**Ependymoma**

> 儿童常见
>
> **第四脑室**更常见
>
> 更偏**阻塞性脑积水**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 84%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Spinal cord compression</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Causes</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Mechanical (eg, disc herniation, spinal stenosis)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Malignancy (eg, lung, breast, prostate cancers)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Infection (eg, epidural abscess)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Symptoms</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Gradually worsening, severe back pain</strong></p>
<p><strong>Pain worse in <mark>recumbent position/at night</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Physical examination</strong></p>
<p>急性脊髓损伤</p>
<p>急性脊髓压迫</p>
<p>均为此表现</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Early</mark> signs早期spinal shock / acute cord dysfunction→ 反射暂时被压没了</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Symmetric extremity <mark>weakness</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Hyporeflexia</mark></strong></p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Late</mark> signs</strong> <strong>UMN tract injury fully declares itself→ 反射亢进、Babinski 阳性</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>↓ Rectal tone骶段通路/descending autonomic pathways 受影响，常提示病情更重</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Hyperreflexia</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>bilateral Babinski reflex</strong></p>
<p><strong>spasticity🡪<mark>paralysis</mark></strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Management</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Emergency MRI</mark> of the spine</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Emergency surgical</mark> ± radiation oncology consultation</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Intravenous glucocorticoids (eg, malignancy)</mark> or <mark>antibiotics (eg, infection)</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 16%" />
<col style="width: 83%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Cervical myelopathy 颈髓病= 颈段脊髓被压，是“长传导束 + 脊髓体征问题”</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Epidemiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Age &gt;55</p>
<p>Degenerative cervical spine/discs → <strong><mark><u>cervical spondylosis</u></mark></strong>🡪canal stenosis → <strong><u>spinal cord compression (myelopathy)</u></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Manifestations</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><mark><strong>Gait dysfunction(spastic, scissoring walk)</strong> - usually first</mark></p>
<p><strong>Extremity weakness &amp; numbness</strong></p>
<p><mark><strong>LMN signs</strong> (<strong>arms</strong>) – <strong>strength↓, hyporeflexia</strong>，<strong>muscle atrophy</strong></mark></p>
<p>病变在<strong>颈髓水平</strong>，累及<strong><mark>前角细胞/神经根</mark></strong>或该节段的下运动神经元</p>
<p><mark><strong>UMN signs</strong> (<strong>legs</strong>) - <strong>Babinski, hyperreflexia </strong></mark></p>
<p>病变在<strong>脊髓</strong>，并且影响了下行<strong><mark>皮质脊髓束</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong>↓ Proprioception/vibration/pain sensation</strong></p>
<p><strong>感觉异常</strong>进一步支持脊髓受压，不是单纯周围神经病</p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Lhermitte sign</mark> <mark>(electric shock-like sensation)</mark></strong></p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Diagnosis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>MRI</mark></strong> of cervical spine</p>
<p>CT myelogram</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Nonsurgical - <strong><mark>immobilization</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>Surgical decompression</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 84%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Clinical features of RA cervical myelopathy</strong></p>
<p><strong>RA + intubation后 + occipital headache + paresthesias + hyperreflexia/Hoffmann = atlantoaxial instability causing cervical myelopathy</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Symptoms</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Neck pain radiating to occipital region</strong></p>
<p><strong>Slowly progressive spastic quadriparesis</strong></p>
<p><strong>Painless sensory deficits in hands or feet</strong></p>
<p><strong>Respiratory dysfunction (eg, from vertebral artery compression)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Signs</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Protruding anterior arch of atlas</strong></p>
<p><strong>Scoliosis with loss of cervical lordosis</strong></p>
<p><strong>UMN signs (eg, spastic paresis, hyperreflexia, Babinski sign)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Hoffman sign</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<span class="mark">Hoffman</span>**：上肢 UMN sign，cervical myelopathy+

**Babinski**：下肢 UMN sign

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />
<col style="width: 22%" />
<col style="width: 22%" />
<col style="width: 41%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="4" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Features of cervical radiculopathy=颈神经根被压，是“<mark>单根神经分布问题</mark>”</strong></p>
<p>只要出现 <strong>疼痛 + 肌无力 + 反射改变</strong>，就要优先想 <strong>radiculopathy</strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>shoulder abduction relief test</mark></strong>（Bakody sign）：病人把手放在头上后，牵拉的神经根张力减轻，所以<strong>神经根性疼痛缓解</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Nerve root</strong></p>
<p>(disc space)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Reflex affected</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Sensory loss*</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Weakness</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>C5</strong></p>
<p>(C4-5)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Biceps</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Lateral upper arm</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Shoulder abduction (deltoid)</p>
<p>Elbow flexion (biceps)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>C6</strong></p>
<p>(C5-6)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Biceps</p>
<p>Brachioradialis</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Thumb</p>
<p>Index finger</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Elbow flexion (biceps)</p>
<p>Forearm pronation/supination (brachioradialis)</p>
<p>Wrist extension</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>C7</strong></p>
<p>(C6-7)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Triceps</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Dorsal forearm</p>
<p>Middle finger</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Elbow extension (triceps)</p>
<p>Wrist flexion</p>
<p>Finger extension</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>C8</strong></p>
<p>(C7-T1)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Finger flexors**</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Ring &amp; little fingers</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Finger flexion &amp; extension</p>
<p>Thumb flexion &amp; abduction</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>T1</strong></p>
<p>(T1-2)</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Finger flexors**</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Medial forearm</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Finger abduction &amp; adduction</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="4" style="text-align: left;"><p>*In addition to <strong>neck/shoulder pain</strong>, <strong>radicular pain</strong> typically has a <strong>similar distribution to sensory loss.</strong></p>
<p>**Not typically evaluated clinically.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**“五六二头，六桡骨，七三头”**

> **C5/C6 → biceps reflex**
>
> **C6 → brachioradialis reflex**
>
> **C7 → triceps reflex**

**“5抬肩，6弯腕，7伸肘，8抓手，1分叉”**

> **C5** → 抬肩（shoulder abduction）
>
> **C6** → 弯肘 + 腕背伸
>
> **C7** → 伸肘
>
> **C8** → 抓握、手指屈曲
>
> **T1** → 手指外展内收

**C8T1支配手部所有内在肌，损伤🡪爪形手**

**（感觉）“六拇七中八小”**

> C6 拇指
>
> C7 中指
>
> C8 小指

**神经根更像：**

> neck pain
>
> 放射痛
>
> dermatomal sensory loss
>
> reflex change

**周围神经更像：**

> 某单一神经支配区异常
>
> 不一定有颈痛
>
> 分布更“解剖性”

| **特点** | **Cervical radiculopathy** | **Cervical myelopathy** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 病变部位 | 颈神经根 | 颈段脊髓 |
| 常见原因 | 椎间盘突出、骨刺压迫<span class="mark">单个神经根</span> | 颈椎病/椎管狭窄压迫<span class="mark">脊髓</span> |
| 疼痛特点 | <span class="mark">**颈肩臂放射痛**明显</span> | 可有颈痛，但**<span class="mark">步态异常、肢体僵硬</span>**更突出 |
| 分布 | **皮节/肌节分布** | <span class="mark">**脊髓束征**，常双侧、下肢更明显</span> |
| 感觉异常 | 某一神经根分布区 | 更广泛，可**累及双手双脚** |
| 肌无力 | 对应某神经根支配肌群 | 四肢或双下肢无力，手也可笨拙 |
| 反射 | **受累根对应<span class="mark">反射下降</span>** | <span class="mark">**下肢反射亢进**常见</span> |
| UMN signs | **没有** | <span class="mark">**有**：Babinski、hyperreflexia、spasticity</span> |
| 步态 | 通常正常 | **<span class="mark">步态异常常是早期表现</span>** |
| 手功能 | 局部肌群弱 | <span class="mark">可有**手笨拙、扣扣子困难**</span> |
| 排尿功能 | 一般没有 | <span class="mark">严重时可有尿急/尿潴留</span> |
| 特殊体征 | **<span class="mark">Spurling 可诱发症状；手放头上可缓解</span>** | **<span class="mark">Lhermitte sign 可有；长束征阳性</span>** |
| 检查 | MRI颈椎，定位神经根 | MRI颈椎，看脊髓受压/髓内信号改变 |

<table style="width:89%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 29%" />
<col style="width: 17%" />
<col style="width: 42%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>体征</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>更支持谁</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: left;"><strong>怎么理解</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Spurling test阳性</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Radiculopathy</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>颈部侧屈后伸再加压，<mark>诱发手臂放射痛</mark></strong></p>
<p>提示颈神经根受压, 压窄椎间孔，挤到神经根</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>手放头上缓解（Bakody sign）</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Radiculopathy</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">减少神经根张力，根性痛减轻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Lhermitte sign阳性</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Myelopathy</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">屈颈牵拉受损颈髓，出现<mark>电击感</mark></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>长束征阳性</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Myelopathy</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">说明脊髓传导束受损，不是单根神经问题</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**<u>Lhermitte sign</u>：electric shock-like sensation in the spine🡪**颈髓后索/脊髓受累的经典提示

**<u>long tract signs（长束征）</u>：这些束一旦受损，表现往往不是“一个肌肉”或“一个反射”那么局部，而是出现：**

**<span class="mark">双侧</span>**

**<span class="mark">UMN signs</span>**

**<span class="mark">下肢明显</span>**

**<span class="mark">步态异常</span>**

**<span class="mark">感觉通路大片受影响</span>**

**运动长束受损/皮质脊髓束**受损：

> **双腿发硬stiff**
>
> **走路像剪刀步/痉挛步态**
>
> 肌张力增高spsticity, 反射亢进hyperreflexia
>
> Babinski 阳性

**感觉长束受损/后索**或**脊髓丘脑束**受损：

> 振动觉、本体觉差
>
> 痛温觉差
>
> **感觉平面**
>
> 走路不稳

**Cervical radiculopathy 病人会说**

> “脖子一歪、一压，胳膊就麻/疼”
>
> “把手放头上反而舒服一点”

**Cervical myelopathy 病人会说**

> “一低头像电流从背上窜下去”
>
> “最近走路发僵、容易绊”
>
> “手越来越笨”

神经查体体征

Romberg test (indicating normal proprioception);

**<span class="mark">Babinski / clonus / Hoffman / pronator drift → UMN lesion</span>**

**Pronator drift：** 双臂前伸、掌心向上、闭眼🡪一侧上肢旋前并下沉

提示UMN / corticospinal tract lesion

<u>**轻度急性 cervical radiculopathy**：</u>

> **只有疼痛和轻度感觉异常**
>
> **没有运动无力**
>
> **没有反射明显异常**
>
> **没有 myelopathy**
>
> **没有感染/肿瘤红旗征**

所以第一步处理应该是：**<span class="mark">保守治疗</span>,** 大多数这种急性颈神经根病会随着时间逐渐改善

包括：

> **<span class="mark">避免诱发动作</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">NSAIDs</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">维持适度活动</span>，不要长期卧床**
>
> **Severe pain: <span class="mark">oral glucocorticoids</span>**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 10%" />
<col style="width: 17%" />

<th colspan="4" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Features of lumbosacral radiculopathy</strong></th>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Nerve root</strong></td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Weakness</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>L2-L4**</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Patellar</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Anteromedial thigh</p>
<p>Medial shin</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Hip flexion (iliopsoas)</p>
<p>Hip adduction</p>
<p>Knee extension (quadriceps)</p>
</blockquote></td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>L5</strong></td>

<p>None</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Lateral shin</p>
<p>Dorsum of the foot</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Foot dorsiflexion &amp; inversion (tibialis anterior)</p>
<p>Foot eversion (peroneus)</p>
<p>Toe extension (extensor hallucis &amp; digitorum)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>S1</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Achilles</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Posterior calf</p>
<p>Sole &amp; lateral foot</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Hip extension (gluteus maximus)</p>
<p>Knee flexion (hamstrings)</p>
<p>Foot plantarflexion (gastrocnemius)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>S2-S4**</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Anocutaneous</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Perineum</p>
</blockquote></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Urinary or fecal incontinence</p>
<p>Sexual dysfunction</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="4" style="text-align: left;"><p>*Radicular pain typically has a similar distribution to sensory loss.</p>
<p>**Difficult to distinguish between individual nerve roots clinically.</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**Marfanoid body habitus**

> 高瘦
>
> 四肢细长
>
> 蜘蛛指
>
> 胸廓畸形
>
> 关节过度活动

<table style="width:91%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20%" />
<col style="width: 71%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Fragile X syndrome🡪normal life expectancy</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Pathogenesis</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Trinucleotide (CGG) repeat expansion of <em>FMR1</em></p>
<p>Gene methylation prevents transcription &amp; protein production</p>

<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Thiazide-induced hyponatremia</strong></p>
<p>老年女性使用 chlorthalidone 后出现慢性低钠血症，表现为 confusion、健忘和步态不稳；首要处理是停用 thiazide</p></th>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>↓ Water excretion (ADH-dependent &amp; ADH-independent mechanisms)</p>
<p>↑ Water intake (natural tendency to polydipsia)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Risk factors &amp; presentation</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Risk factor: advanced age (mean <strong>age &gt;75), female, low BMI</strong></p>
<p>Typically <strong>within few weeks of therapy</strong> or after <strong>acute event (eg, diarrhea)</strong></p>
<p>Patients often <strong>euvolemic with subtle symptoms (eg, confusion)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Chronic (&gt;48h) hyponatremia</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Subtle: nausea, fatigue</strong></p>
<p><strong>Severe: encephalopathy, gait disturbances, seizures</strong></p></td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Treatment</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Discontinue thiazide</strong></p>
<p><strong>Correct hyponatremia (eg, IV fluids)</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>

<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>ADH</strong> = antidiuretic hormone; <strong>IV</strong> = intravenous.</td>

**<span class="mark">Thiazide排K, Na, Cl; hypergluc（glycemia, lipidemia, uricemia, calcemia）</span>**

**<u>Phenytoin toxicity</u>服用 phenytoin 的患者在加用 TMP-SMX 后出现眼震、共济失调、指鼻不准和宽基步态**

long-acting antiepileptic medication🡪inhibits voltage-gated sodium channels. 

**↑risk of toxicity**

**p450 inhibitor (eg,TMP-SMX, fluconazole**)

displace phenytoin from plasma proteins (eg, **valproic acid**)

**renal or hepatic dysfunction**

**Acute toxicity🡪<span class="mark">cerebellar dysfunction</span>眼震 + 共济失调 + 指鼻不准 + 宽基步态**

**horizontal nystagmus (ie, nystagmus on lateral gaze)**

**ataxia (eg, wide-based gait)**

**dysmetria (eg, on finger-nose testing)**

**slurred speech**

nausea/vomiting

hyperreflexia may occur. 

**Severe toxicity**

altered mental status (eg, lethargy, confusion)

coma

paradoxical seizures

death

**Rapid IV phenytoin or fosphenytoin （prodrug ）**

**hypotension and bradyarrhythmia**

**Management**

**<span class="mark">supportive care</span>**

**<span class="mark">gastric decontamination</span>**

**<span class="mark">hemodialysis</span>**

**多年不发作，检查也正常；准备要怀孕，苯妥英慢慢停**

<span class="mark">**seizure-free for ≥2 years** can consider **<u>discontinuing their antiepileptic drug</u>**</span>**/AED**. 

**low risk** for future seizure recurrence:

lack of an identifiable structural etiology (eg, normal MRI)

normal electroencephalography

positive initial response to therapy (eg, no seizures on medication)

The highest risk for **seizure recurrence** is in the **first 6 months after AED discontinuation**

**<span class="mark">slow taper</span> and discontinue phenytoin**🡪allow for slow normalization of the receptors, minimization of the risk for seizure

**<u>fetal hydantoin syndrome</u>**

<img src="images/media/image53.png" style="width:1.97926in;height:2.15366in" />

<img src="images/media/image54.jpeg" style="width:4.75836in;height:5.72785in" />

<img src="images/media/image36.png" style="width:6.75316in;height:5.68045in" />

**Bell palsy面瘫累及额和眼，先想 Bell，给 prednisone**

 **急性** 单侧周围性面瘫

 可有**耳后痛、味觉改变、流泪异常**

peripheral neuropathy involving **CN VII**

**acute onset (within hours)** and **progressive** (maximal weakness within 3 weeks)

**<span class="mark">prodrome</span>** of **auricular pain** or **dysacusis** (distortion of sound)

**Unilateral facial paralysis**: **mouth drooping, disappearance of the nasolabial fold, <span class="mark">involvement of the upper face</span>** (eg, inability to close the eye, weakness raising the eyebrow), which ddx **<u>acute stroke</u>** (in **upper face spared**)

decreased tearing, hyperacusis, and a reduced sense of taste

Sensation is typically intact.

Treatment

<span class="mark">high-dose oral **glucocorticoids**</span> (eg, prednisone), started **within 72 hours**

**± valacyclovir or acyclovir** (caused by **reactivation of HSV**)

**corneal protection strategies** (eg, moisture chamber, lubricating drops or ointment, taping the eye closed at night)

**improve spontaneously within 3-4 months**

**palsies lasting longer suggest another diagnosis**

> **<u>cerebellopontine angle / internal auditory canal tumor (vestibular schwannoma)</u>**
>
> **progressive unilateral LMN facial weakness + hearing loss + facial spasm**
>
> 面神经 **CN VII** 和前庭蜗神经 **CN VIII** 在**内听道/小脑桥脑角**位置很近。如果这里长了肿瘤，就会同时压到：
>
> **CN VII** → 面瘫、面肌抽动
>
> **CN VIII** → 听力下降、耳鸣、平衡问题
>
> 慢性肿瘤压迫/刺激面神经，不一定一开始就是完全瘫，也可先出现：
>
> **twitching**
>
> hemifacial **spasm**
>
> 之后逐渐无力
>
> Diagnosis:

**<span class="mark">MRI</span>** of the head

<img src="images/media/image55.jpeg" style="width:4.07464in;height:3.78462in" />

**<u>Herpes zoster oticus/Ramsay Hunt syndrome</u>**--latent VZV reactivation

> **<span class="mark">Ear pain</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Facial weakness</span>**
>
> **<span class="mark">Vesicular rash</span>** <span class="mark">in **external auditory canal**</span>—facial nerve

spread to the vestibulocochlear nerve (CN VIII)

auditory🡪hearing loss, hyperacusis, tinnitus

vestibular 🡪vertigo, nausea/vomiting

Treatment

**<span class="mark">corticosteroids</span>**

**<span class="mark">antiviral medications</span>**

**Early initiation (\<3 days)** a/w improved recovery of facial nerve function; however, even with treatment many patients have **residual facial weakness**. 

If facial nerve paralysis, **<span class="mark">protection of the eye</span>** (**artificial tears, lubricating ointment**) is of paramount importance.

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Bell palsy</strong></td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>受累</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p>耳后痛、味觉改变、流泪异常</p>
<p>通常<strong>没有其他神经系统红旗</strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>isolated unilateral LMN facial palsy</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><mark>早期 <strong>steroids</strong></mark>；眼睛保护</td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>缓慢进展，数周到数月</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">可受累（若压迫 CN VII）</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>听力下降、耳鸣、平衡问题</strong></p>
<p>可有 facial twitch/spasm</p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>facial weakness + hearing loss</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>MRI</mark> brain/internal auditory canal</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Ramsay Hunt</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;">常较急性/亚急性</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>受累</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>耳痛 + 耳周/耳道/口腔疱疹</strong></p>
<p><strong>hearing loss/vertigo</strong></p></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>painful vesicular rash</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><p><strong><mark>steroids</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>antivirals</mark></strong></p>
<p>眼睛保护</p></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**题干关键词速抓**

> **“woke up this morning” / 48 hours** → Bell palsy。
>
> **“can still wrinkle forehead”** → stroke。
>
> **“ear vesicles / severe otalgia / hearing loss”** → Ramsay Hunt。
>
> **“6 weeks progressive / hearing loss / tinnitus / facial spasm”** → vestibular schwannoma。

**高频陷阱**

少数**脑干卒中**可以看起来像周围性面瘫，所以如果有任何其他神经系统异常、步态问题、复视、肢体症状，不能只按 Bell palsy 处理。

**最短版结论**

> **额头保留**：stroke
>
> **急性整侧面瘫**：Bell palsy
>
> **耳痛疱疹+听力下降**：Ramsay Hunt
>
> **缓慢进展+听力下降**：vestibular schwannoma

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 12%" />

<th colspan="3" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Clues to etiology of syncope</strong></th>

<td rowspan="3" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Reflex syncope</strong></td>

<p>Advanced age, carotid atherosclerosis</p>
</blockquote></td>

<p>Systolic ejection murmur</p>
</blockquote></td>

<p>QT-interval prolongation (polymorphic)</p>

</tr>

<p>ECG abnormalities (eg, sinus pauses, dropped QRS complexes)</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

</tr>

</table>

**Parkinson disease + orthostatic hypotension + standing后心率不代偿增加**\
→ **<u>autonomic insufficiency / neurogenic orthostatic hypotension</u>**

看到 **orthostatic hypotension** 时，先看**心率有没有代偿性升高**

> **有** → 想**低血容量**
>
> **没有** → 想**自主神经功能不全**

<table style="width:93%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 15%" />
<col style="width: 77%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Vasovagal &amp; situational syncope</strong></p>
<p><strong>强烈情绪/疼痛刺激 → 迷走神经过强 + 交感抑制 → 血管扩张、心率下降 → 脑灌注下降 → 晕厥</strong></p></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong><mark>Triggers</mark></strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Pain,* anxiety,*</strong> emotional stress, heat, prolonged standing</p>
<p>Situational: <strong>cough,* micturition,*</strong> defecation, eating, hair-combing*</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>

presentation</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>

<p><strong><mark>Rapid recovery</mark></strong> of consciousness (eg,<strong> &lt;1-2 min</strong>)</p>

<p><strong><mark>Counterpressure techniques</mark> for recurrent episodes</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>

<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">*Particularly common triggers in the <strong>pediatric population</strong></td>

<img src="images/media/image56.png" style="width:6.52708in;height:0.91181in" />

**梅毒螺旋体（Treponema pallidum）** 晚期累及

**1. dorsal columns**

> **位置觉下降**
>
> **振动觉下降**
>
> **感觉性共济失调（sensory ataxia）**🡪走路不稳、Romberg 阳性（闭目难立）

**2. dorsal roots**

> **闪电样疼痛 / stabbing pain / lancinating pain**
>
> **反射减弱或消失**

**3. 自主神经受累**

> **神经源性膀胱**
>
> 尿失禁、尿滴沥

**4. 瞳孔异常**

> **Argyll Robertson pupil**
>
> 小而不规则
>
> **light-near dissociation**

**<u>Vitamin B12 deficiency🡪subacute combined degeneration</u>**

spinocerebellar tracts

ataxia

**lateral corticospinal tracts**

spastic paresis

hyperreflexia

**dorsal columns**

loss of position and vibration sense

positive Romberg sign

<img src="images/media/image57.png" style="width:6.52708in;height:1.11111in" />

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 17%" />
<col style="width: 82%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><p><strong>Carotid artery dissection</strong>🡪false lumen, aneurysm, intramural hematoma🡪arterial obstruction, thromboembolic events</p>
<p>Common cause of <strong><mark>stroke in young pts</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>年轻人轻微创伤后出现1）单侧头颈痛，2）partial Horner syndrome ，3）短暂神经功能缺损</mark></strong></p></th>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>Etiology</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Trauma; spontaneous</strong> occurrence</p>
<p>Underlying contributors: <strong>HTN, smoking, CTD</strong></p>
</blockquote></td>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Unilateral head &amp; neck pain</mark></strong></p>
<p><strong><mark>cerebral ischemia (stroke, TIA)</mark>🡪 focal weakness, transient vision loss</strong></p>
<p><strong>Ipsilateral <mark>partial Horner syndrome</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p><strong>Ptosis &amp; miosis without anhidrosis</strong></p></td>

</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong><mark>Thrombolysis (if ≤4.5 hr</mark></strong> after symptom onset)</p>
<p><strong><mark>Antiplatelet therapy (eg, aspirin) ± anticoagulation</mark></strong></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>

<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>CTD</strong> = connective tissue disease; <strong>HTN</strong> = hypertension.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

**为什么轻微外伤后会发生**

颈动脉夹层可发生在：

> 自发
>
> 轻微创伤后，如：

跌倒

运动损伤

颈部过伸/旋转

内膜受损后，血液进入动脉壁，形成：

> **intramural hematoma**
>
> 假腔
>
> 血流受阻
>
> 血栓形成与远端栓塞

**为什么会出现 Horner syndrome？**颈内动脉周围走行着交感神经纤维。夹层或壁内血肿压迫这些交感纤维，就会出现：

> **ptosis**
>
> **miosis**

这是 **partial Horner syndrome**。

为什么叫 partial？因为**无汗减少（anhidrosis）常不明显**，因为面部出汗相关纤维多沿 **external carotid** 走，而不是 internal carotid。

**为什么会有 transient leg weakness？**夹层可导致：

> 动脉狭窄
>
> thromboembolism

从而引起短暂脑缺血：

> **TIA**
>
> stroke

所以题干里的 **transient leg weakness** 就是脑缺血表现。

<img src="images/media/image58.png" style="width:2.65833in;height:3.275in" />

<colgroup>

<img src="images/media/image59.png" style="width:4.23086in;height:3.75316in" />

Findings consistent with **<u>benign microcephaly</u>** include:

> **Absence of dysmorphic features**
>
> **Normal head shape and neurologic examination**
>
> **Normal development**
>
> **Absence of rapidly declining growth percentiles: ≥2 major percentiles**

**Isolated microcephaly + relatively small parental head circumference**🡪**<u>benign (familial) variant of growth</u>**. 

Signs concerning for **<u>pathologic microcephaly</u>** include:

> **Neurologic abnormalities** (eg, hypotonia, developmental delay)
>
> **Dysmorphic** features
>
> Rapidly declining head circumference percentiles (ie, curve crossing multiple major percentiles)

The **first step** for suspected **pathologic microcephaly** is **<span class="mark">MRI of the brain</span>**

detect a congenital **brain malformation** (eg, encephalocele, lissencephaly \[absence of gyri\])

**perinatal hypoxic-ischemic insult** (eg, white matter injury)

**infection** (eg, calcifications in cytomegalovirus)

postnatal **traumatic brain injury** (ie, nonaccidental trauma)

💡 **MRI** is preferred over **CT scan** because MRI lacks ionizing radiation and is more sensitive in identifying infarction or structural abnormalities.

**婴儿 Hypotonia 先分两大类：**

**Central（中枢性） vs Peripheral（周围性）**

**一、先记总原则**

**<u>Central hypotonia:</u>** 问题在 **脑/脊髓中枢**\
更常见提示：

> **发育迟缓**
>
> **认知/社交也异常**
>
> **癫痫**
>
> **异常眼神/意识问题**
>
> **反射正常或亢进**
>
> **可能合并 microcephaly**
>
> 轴性低张明显，但肢体力量不一定特别差

**<u>Peripheral hypotonia</u>:** 问题在 **前角细胞、周围神经、神经肌接头、肌肉**\
更常见提示：

> **真正肌无力明显**
>
> **抗重力动作差**
>
> **喂养差/吸吮差**
>
> **呼吸无力**
>
> **反射下降或消失**
>
> **意识通常正常**
>
> **眼神通常清楚、社交可正常**

| **特点** | **Central hypotonia** | **Peripheral hypotonia** |
|:---|:---|:---|
| 病变部位 | 脑/中枢神经系统 | 前角细胞、神经、NMJ、肌肉 |
| 精神状态/互动 | 可异常 | 常正常 |
| 发育 | 常全面落后 | 主要运动落后 |
| 肌力 | 可相对保留 | **明显无力** |
| 深腱反射 | 正常或↑ | **↓或消失** |
| 腱反射/病理反射 | 可有中枢体征 | 无中枢体征 |
| 抽搐/癫痫 | 可有 | 少见 |
| 头围异常 | 可有 microcephaly | 通常没有 |
| 面容/畸形 | 可有 dysmorphism | 较少，除部分遗传肌病 |
| 喂养/呼吸 | 可受影响 | 常明显受影响 |
| 首选检查 | **<span class="mark">MRI brain / genetic eval</span>** | **CK、SMN检测、EMG/NCS、毒素/代谢评估** |

**三、<span class="mark"><u>Central hypotonia</u></span> 高频病因**

> **hypotonia**
>
> **developmental delay**
>
> **microcephaly / seizures / dysmorphism**

**CNS problem → MRI brain**

**1. 缺氧缺血性脑损伤 / 脑发育异常**

提示词：

> developmental delay
>
> seizures
>
> microcephaly
>
> 异常神经查体
>
> 出生窒息史/围产期问题

**秒选点**

**hypotonia + developmental delay + microcephaly → MRI brain**

**2. 染色体/遗传综合征**

比如：

> Down syndrome
>
> Prader-Willi syndrome
>
> 其他遗传综合征

提示词：

> hypotonia from birth
>
> dysmorphic features
>
> feeding difficulty
>
> developmental delay

**高频：**

**Prader-Willi**

> 新生儿/婴儿期 **hypotonia + poor feeding**
>
> 后期变成 **hyperphagia, obesity**

**3. 先天感染**

比如：

> CMV
>
> toxoplasmosis
>
> Zika

提示词：

> microcephaly
>
> hearing loss
>
> calcifications
>
> chorioretinitis
>
> hepatosplenomegaly

**4. 婴儿脑瘫早期**

早期可先表现低张，后期可能转高张。\
提示：

> 围产期损伤史
>
> 发育异常
>
> 持续原始反射
>
> motor milestone delay

**<u>Peripheral hypotonia</u> 高频病因**

Peripheral 再分四层：

**anterior horn cell**

**peripheral nerve**

**neuromuscular junction**

**muscle**

**1. Anterior horn cell：<span class="mark"><u>SMA（Spinal muscular atrophy）</u></span>**

> **floppy baby**
>
> **<span class="mark">tongue fasciculations</span>**
>
> **areflexia**
>
> severe weakness
>
> paradoxical breathing
>
> alert infant

**经典特点**

> 意识清楚
>
> 眼球运动通常保留
>
> 深腱反射降低/消失
>
> 舌束颤动很高频

**秒选: floppy baby + areflexia + tongue fasciculations = SMA**

<img src="images/media/image60.png" style="width:7.68009in;height:1.31229in" />

**2. Peripheral nerve：少见**

可见于某些遗传性神经病或代谢病。\
Step 2 不是最常考核心。

**3. Neuromuscular junction：<span class="mark"><u>Infant botulism</u></span>**

> **constipation**
>
> poor feeding
>
> weak cry
>
> ptosis
>
> hypotonia
>
> descending weakness
>
> honey exposure（经典但不一定有）
>
> cranial nerve findings

**机制:** 肉毒毒素抑制 **ACh release**

**秒选: constipation + floppy baby + ptosis/poor suck = infant botulism**

检查可做粪便毒素检测，但临床上常先支持治疗。

**4. Neuromuscular junction：Transient neonatal myasthenia**

妈妈有 MG 时要想。

提示词：

> 母亲有 **myasthenia gravis**
>
> 婴儿出生后几天内：

poor suck

weak cry

hypotonia

呼吸困难

是**母体抗体经胎盘传给婴儿**。

**5. Muscle：Congenital myopathy / muscular dystrophy**

提示词：

> hypotonia
>
> facial weakness
>
> feeding difficulty
>
> delayed motor milestones
>
> CK 可升高（依病种）
>
> 反射下降

**经典考试偏向**

> 真正肌无力
>
> 中枢体征少
>
> 认知通常正常

**六、最实用的鉴别表**

| **疾病** | **central / peripheral** | **高频提示词** | **反射** | **意识/社交** | **其他特色** |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **病理性小头/脑发育异常** | Central | microcephaly, delay, head lag | 正常或↑ | 可异常 | **MRI先做** |
| **缺氧缺血性脑损伤** | Central | 围产期异常, seizures, delay | 正常或↑ | 可异常 | 中枢体征 |
| **Down syndrome** | Central | hypotonia + dysmorphic facies | 可正常 | 可有发育迟缓 | 先天畸形 |
| **Prader-Willi** | Central | 新生儿低张+喂养差，后期暴食肥胖 | 可正常 | 发育迟缓 | 遗传印记 |
| **SMA** | Peripheral | areflexia, tongue fasciculations | **↓/无** | 正常 | 前角细胞病 |
| **Infant botulism** | Peripheral (NMJ) | constipation, ptosis, poor suck | ↓ | 通常清醒 | 下降性无力 |
| **Transient neonatal MG** | Peripheral (NMJ) | maternal MG, weak suck/cry | 可↓ | 清醒 | 母体抗体 |
| **Congenital myopathy** | Peripheral (muscle) | facial weakness, motor delay | ↓ | 正常 | CK/肌活检帮助诊断 |

**七、做题流程图**

**第一步：先看有没有“脑线索”**

有以下任一个，先偏 **central**：

> developmental delay
>
> seizures
>
> microcephaly
>
> dysmorphic features
>
> abnormal mental status
>
> reflexes normal/brisk

**→ 先做 brain MRI / genetic evaluation**

**第二步：如果神志清楚、互动好，但“没力”**

就偏 **peripheral**

再分：

**A. tongue fasciculations + areflexia**

→ **SMA**

**B. constipation + ptosis + poor feeding**

→ **infant botulism**

**C. mother has MG**

→ **transient neonatal MG**

**D. isolated muscle weakness / CK高**

→ **myopathy / muscular dystrophy**

**八、最强记忆口诀**

**中枢低张看脑子：小头、发育差、反射不低**

**周围低张看力气：真无力、反射低、娃还很清醒**

再给你一个更考试版的：

**Central = “脑小、发育慢、反射还在”**

**Peripheral = “娃清醒、没力气、反射下去”**

**九、超短秒选版**

**Central hypotonia**

> developmental delay
>
> microcephaly
>
> seizures
>
> dysmorphism
>
> reflexes normal/brisk\
> → **MRI brain**

**Peripheral hypotonia**

> alert baby
>
> weakness \> developmental issues
>
> poor suck/respiratory weakness
>
> reflexes decreased\
> → 想：
>
> **SMA**（tongue fasciculations）
>
> **botulism**（constipation, ptosis）
>
> **neonatal MG**（maternal MG）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />
<col style="width: 86%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th colspan="2" style="text-align: left;"><strong>Concussion</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Clinical features</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p><strong>Transient neurologic disturbance/neuronal functional disturbane (eg, dizziness, disorientation, amnesia)</strong> after mild TBI</p>
<p>No structural intracranial injury</p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Management</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Remove from same-day physical play</p>
<p>Neurologic evaluation</p>
<p>Rest for ≥24 hr</p>
<p><strong>Gradual return to normal activity</strong> if symptoms do not worsen</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Physical: light aerobic exercise → noncontact sports → contact sports</p>
<p>Neurocognitive: limited screen time, school accommodations (eg, frequent breaks, shortened days)</p></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td colspan="2" style="text-align: left;">TBI = traumatic brain injury.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

• **Atypical signs** that should prompt further evaluation with a **<span class="mark">head CT scan</span>**.

> **Focal neurologic deficits**
>
> **depressed or worsening mental status**
>
> **signs of possible skull fracture** (eg, battle sign, temporal hematoma)

**<u>Postconcussive syndrome</u>**

**persistent headache, confusion, difficulty concentrating, and poor sleep** for the **past month** after hitting their head

other manifestations include amnesia, vertigo, and mood alterations; symptoms typically resolve with **symptomatic treatment** (headache management, behavior therapy) within a few weeks to months.

> **Physical**: headache, dizziness, sleep disturbances
>
> **Cognitive**: difficulty concentrating, impaired memory
>
> **Emotional**: irritability, anxiety, depression

Symptoms typically resolve with **<span class="mark">symptomatic treatment</span>** (eg, headache management, behavior therapy) within a few weeks to months following TBI; however, some patients continue to have symptoms for ≥3 months

<img src="images/media/image61.png" style="width:2.04653in;height:2.70903in" /><img src="images/media/image62.png" style="width:3.49783in;height:2.66757in" />

**<u>Blepharospasm</u>**

A form of **focal dystonia**, 即基底节/运动调控异常导致局部肌群不自主收缩

Caused by **Parkinson disease, antipsychotics, idiopathic (MC)**

**反复发作的bilateral, symmetric眼睑不自主闭合（痉挛），一时睁不开眼**

**<span class="mark">Bright light</span> <span class="mark">trigger</span>, <span class="mark">touching or brushing the skin</span> around eye <span class="mark">terminate</span> (sensory trick)**

**频繁眨眼**

神经系统其他检查正常

**治疗：**

**<span class="mark">Mild: trigger avoidance</span> (wearing dark glasses)**

**<span class="mark">Severe: botulinum toxin injection</span>**

**<u>Meige syndrome</u>: Blepharospasm + spasm of lower face (jaw, tongue)**

<img src="images/media/image63.png" style="width:6.52708in;height:0.33264in" />

**1️⃣ 先理解原理**

**A. 正常听觉AC \> BC**

声音正常传入耳朵的主通路是**空气传导（AC）**：外耳 → 鼓膜 → 听小骨 → 耳蜗

**骨传导（BC）**是：颅骨振动 → 直接刺激耳蜗

正常情况下，**空气传导效率比骨传导高**，所以正常人做 Rinne：AC \> BC

这也是为什么 **感音神经性 hearing loss** 时，虽然整体听力下降，但空气和骨传导都一起变差，**相对关系仍然常是 AC \> BC**。

**B. 传导性 hearing loss 为什么 BC \> AC**

传导性问题在：外耳、中耳、鼓膜、听小骨，也就是 **空气传导这条路被挡住了**。\
但耳蜗本身还在，所以骨传导绕过外中耳，仍可相对保留。

所以：Conductive loss → AC下降更多 → BC \> AC，这就是 **Rinne 阴性**。

Rinne阴性（BC \> AC）= 传导性\
Rinne阳性（AC \> BC）= 正常 or 感音神经性

**C. Weber 为什么会偏向不同侧**= Conductive to bad ear, Sensorineural to good ear

**传导性 hearing loss：偏向患侧**

因为患侧外界环境噪音进入少，**背景噪音减少**，骨传导声音显得更响；所以 Weber 会偏向 **传导性听力下降那一侧**。

**感音神经性 hearing loss：偏向健侧**

因为患侧耳蜗/听神经本身接收能力下降，所以骨传导传过去也听不清；因此 Weber 会偏向 **听力较好的健侧**。

**3️⃣ 一张总表秒记**

| **类型**                | **Weber** | **Rinne**    |
|:------------------------|:----------|:-------------|
| 正常                    | 不偏      | AC \> BC     |
| 传导性 hearing loss     | 偏向患侧  | **BC \> AC** |
| 感音神经性 hearing loss | 偏向健侧  | AC \> BC     |

**“传导偏坏耳，神经偏好耳；Rinne 反了才是传导耳。”**

**Rinne**定**传导性BC\>AC** vs感音性 AC\>BC

**Weber**定哪一侧，**传导性患侧声音大，感音性健侧声音大**

**7️⃣ 常见病因顺手一起记**

**传导性 hearing loss，**问题在外耳/中耳：耵聍堵塞、中耳积液、鼓膜穿孔、otosclerosis

**感音神经性 hearing loss，**问题在内耳/听神经：presbycusis、噪音暴露、acoustic neuroma、ototoxic drugs

**【Presbycusis】**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 14%" />
<col style="width: 85%" />
</colgroup>

<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>Increasing incidence with age &gt;60</p>
<p><strong>Cochlear hair cell loss</strong></p>
<p><strong>Degeneration of spiral ganglion cells</strong> in the vestibulocochlear nerve <strong>(CN VIII)</strong></p>

**<span class="mark">presbycusis和<u>noise-induced hearing loss</u></span> 的共同点**

> **sensorineural hearing loss**
>
> **双侧**
>
> **高频下降**

**区别**

> **Presbycusis**：年龄相关退变
>
> **Noise-induced hearing loss**：长期噪音暴露导致毛细胞损伤cochlear hair cell damage

**Hearing protection (earplugs)**

**Conduct screening hearing evaluations**

**Cerebellar stroke, 早期CT正常**

Ankle reflex B12缺乏🡪 ankle reflex增高（影响cortical spinal髓鞘），多年病史才缺乏

VZV🡪Ramsay Hunt syndrome, 累及VII, VIII🡪前庭vertigo；膝状神经节以上神经

HSV🡪bell palsy, 不累及auditory canal

**【Aminoglycoside ototoxicity】**

Cochlea🡪sensorineural hearing loss

Vestibular system🡪vertigo

<span class="mark">URI之后出现眩晕</span>

<span class="mark">眩晕+有听力↓🡪</span>**labyrinthitis迷路炎**

<span class="mark">无听力↓🡪</span>**Vestibular neuritis**

<span class="mark">【Vertigo】</span>

**Central vertigo（脑干CN VIII/小脑，前庭神经核）**

brainstem (**CNIII**)

**脑干/小脑卒中**，也可见于偏头痛、多发性硬化等；要警惕持续症状、垂直或变向眼震、明显步态不稳和其他脑神经/长束征；

> **<span class="mark">Lateral medullary syndrome (Wallenberg) PICA🡪前共交火球</span>**
>
> **(前庭神经受损🡪central vertigo)**

**acoustic neuroma**

前厅区，4组前厅神经核，横跨延髓和脑桥

损伤后出现眩晕的机制

> <img src="images/media/image64.png" style="width:2.97318in;height:1.72499in" />

听神经瘤🡪压迫前庭神经核🡪vertigo

**Peripheral vertigo（**前庭神经核以下，**内耳/前庭神经）**常有位置诱发、水平/旋转性眼震、少见其他神经定位体征

**BPPV**

**Labyrinthitis**

**vestibular neuritis**

**Ménière disease**

<img src="images/media/image65.png" style="width:5.08864in;height:5.49788in" />

**1. Ménière disease**= **Episodic vertigo + Hearing loss + Tinnitus/fullness**

**原理：**本质是 **<span class="mark">endolymphatic hydrops（内淋巴过多/压力升高）</span>**，影响内耳，**前庭**+**耳蜗**，所以会同时出现 **眩晕 + 听力问题**。经典表现：**反复发作的眩晕、波动性感音神经性 hearing loss、耳鸣、耳闷胀感**。

**诊断要点**

> **Vertigo (episodic) <span class="mark">反复发作性</span>**，**<span class="mark">20 分钟到数小时</span>** vs **BPPV眩晕十几秒**
>
> **Sensorineural hearing loss（fluctuating）波动性，时好时坏，但逐渐下降**
>
> **tinnitus耳鸣 (刺激耳蜗)**
>
> **aural fullness**

**治疗逻辑：**<span class="mark">急性发作可对症</span>；<span class="mark">长期预防常用 **低盐饮食 + 利尿剂**</span>。

**“耳鸣耳堵又耳聋，反复眩晕是梅尼埃。”**

**2. BPPV（benign paroxysmal positional vertigo/良性阵发性位置性眩晕）<span class="mark">体位诱发，发作短暂</span>**

**= Brief + Position-triggered + Positive Dix-Hallpike“<span class="mark">一动头就晕，一分钟内停</span>，想到 BPPV。”**

半规管：感受身体位置（前，上，水平）

壶腹：盖的膜与感受细胞相互运动；如果膜脱落🡪<span class="mark">**耳石**/debris</span>，**脱落入半规管**随内淋巴液循环，运动时，耳石随重力运动，局部形成涡流，刺激感受细胞🡪诱发眩晕发作，**石头停下来就好**

<img src="images/media/image66.png" style="width:4.61692in;height:2.75592in" />

本质是 **otoconia（耳石）脱落**，最常进入 **posterior semicircular canal后半规管**。

头位变化时，耳石在半规管里移动，异常刺激壶腹嵴，导致短暂眩晕和眼震，眼震可疲劳（重复做会减弱）

**诊断要点**

> **反复、短暂发作（\<60秒）**
>
> **<span class="mark">Dix-Hallpike 阳性</span>：支持外周性 BPPV，头转向患侧**、放倒后患侧朝下（头转45度，躺下，耳石进入半规管）**诱发眩晕/<span class="mark">眼震</span>**
>
> 一般 **无 hearing loss / tinnitus**

**治疗：<span class="mark">以复位手法为主</span>**，药物不是核心。**<span class="mark">canalith repositioning maneuver</span>（如 <span class="mark">Epley maneuver</span>）**(左转45度，迅速躺下，头右边翻90度，身体翻90度，坐起来)🡪把耳石“搬回去”，后半规管石子回到壶腹部。

**3. Vestibular neuritis（前庭神经炎）**

<span class="mark">病毒感染导致🡪急性发作，眩晕持续时间长（病毒一直刺激），**不伴**随其它神经损害体征</span>

Acute prolonged vertigo + No hearing loss

本质是 **<span class="mark">CN VIII 前庭支炎症</span>**，和病毒后炎症有关。因为主要累及**前庭支**，不累及耳蜗🡪**持续性急性眩晕**，但**没有hearing loss（**前厅神经（传入神经）🡪影响前厅神经支配的功能，所以只有眩晕，无耳蜗受累，不会听力下降**）**

**Head impulse test🡪vestibular hypofunction causing dizziness**

**诊断要点**

> 常在 **viral syndrome** 后
>
> **单次急性发作,** 突然严重眩晕、恶心、步态不稳
>
> **可持续数天**，属于自限性疾病
>
> **abnormal <span class="mark">head impulse/thrust test头冲实验</span>：**查 VOR **vesitublo-ocular reflex（**前庭-眼反射**）**：正常头与眼睛运动方向相反；头快速转向某侧时，如果眼睛守不住目标、**需要 corrective saccade**，说明**那一侧外周前庭功能受损**；持续性眩晕里若 HIT 正常，要警惕中枢性卒中（外周前庭器官和 VOR 弧常常还是完整的）🡪“HIT 异常偏外周，HIT 正常防中风。”

**眼震：往一侧快，另一侧慢**🡪**快相方向是眼震方向**

**周围vs中枢：眼震方向不会随看的方向改变（快相不变）**🡪**周围性眼震**

> 左侧前庭受损，向大脑传，右边的刺激比左边刺激多🡪大脑以为头向右运动，眼睛要朝左运动（vestibuloocular reflex）🡪大脑发出纠正信号（saccade扫视）
>
> <span class="mark">**Peripheral眼震🡪unidirectional**，眼震方向不会随左右看的方向改变</span>
>
> <span class="mark">**Central眼震🡪bi-directional**，眼震方向随左右看的方向改变（前庭神经核以上调节出问题，眼震方向不固定，垂直眼震down-beating）</span>
>
> **听力通常正常**

**和 【labyrinthitis迷路炎】的区别:** 在 vestibular neuritis 的基础上再加 **单侧 hearing loss**，因为迷路**同时累及<span class="mark">前庭+耳蜗</span>**。有**前驱URI**，单次发作，病毒感染好了就好了

**治疗逻辑：对症治疗**，如抗眩晕药、止吐；多数可自行恢复。糖皮质激素可能加快恢复。

**“一场大晕好几天，听力没掉是前庭炎。”**

<img src="images/media/image67.png" style="width:5.76806in;height:3.28125in" />

**4. Vestibular migraine（前庭性偏头痛）**Vertigo + Migraine features = Vestibular migraine

**<span class="mark">血管舒张功能异常，眩晕伴头痛，可有prodroma，发作间期正常</span>**

**偏头痛通路和前庭网络异常耦合** 造成的眩晕，临床上常和偏头痛史、畏光、视觉先兆等一起出现。

**诊断要点**

> 眩晕和 **headache / aura / photophobia** 有关
>
> 发作间期通常可恢复
>
> 没有固定的耳科三联

**“头痛先兆一起转，想到偏头痛性眩晕。”**

**5. Brainstem / cerebellar stroke（脑干/小脑卒中）**

**<span class="mark">眩晕开始时间明确sudden-onset，持续时间长，常伴其它神经症状和体征</span>**

本质是 **后循环缺血或出血**，损伤前庭核、小脑、脑干通路，所以也会眩晕，但这类眩晕属于 **central vertigo**。中枢性眩晕更常有其他神经定位体征，如复视、构音障碍、感觉或运动异常、严重共济失调。

**诊断要点**

> **突然起病、持续性**
>
> **垂直眼震或方向改变眼震**
>
> **眼震不被凝视固定抑制**
>
> **明显步态不稳**
>
> 常有 **其他 CNS symptoms/signs**

在 **acute vestibular syndrome** 里，某些床边眼动检查对识别中枢性卒中很重要，因为早期影像尤其 CT 可能不敏感。

Persistent vertigo + Neuro deficits = Central stroke until proven otherwise

**“眩晕再加神经征，先当后循环卒中。”**

**6. Peripheral vs Central**

<table style="width:94%;">
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 20%" />
<col style="width: 45%" />
<col style="width: 28%" />
</colgroup>

</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>

</tr>

<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>不稳但多能走</strong></td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><strong>可严重不能站</strong></td>
</tr>

</table>

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 13%" />

<thead>
<tr>
<th style="text-align: center;"></th>
<th style="text-align: center;"><strong>Peripheral vertigo</strong></th>
<th style="text-align: center;"><strong>Central vertigo</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Etiologies</td>
<td style="text-align: left;"><blockquote>
<p>BPPV</p>
<p>Ménière disease</p>
<p>Vestibular neuritis</p>
</blockquote></td>
